AVy_1,1.1–1,1.3	nārāyaṇam nikhila pūrṇa guṇa eka deham nirdoṣam āpyatamam api akhilaiḥ su vākyaiḥ asya udbhavāt idam aśeṣa viśeṣataḥ api vandyam sadā priyatamam mama sat namāmi tam eva śāstra prabhavam praṇamya jagadgurūṇām gurum añjasā eva viśeṣataḥ me parama ākhya vidyā vyākhyām karomi anu api ca aham eva prādurbhūtaḥ hariḥ vyāsaḥ viriñca bhava pūrvakaiḥ arthitaḥ paravidyā ākhyam cakre śāstram anuttamam 
AVy_1,1.4–1,1.7	 guruḥ gurūṇām prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇām bādarāyaṇaḥ yatas tat uditam mānam aja ādibhyaḥ tad arthataḥ vaktṛ śrotṛ prasaktīnām yat ā āptiḥ anukūla tā āpta vākya tayā tena śruti mūla tayā tathā yukti mūla tayā ca eva prāmāṇyam trividham mahat dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇām ekadhā anyatra sarvaśas atas na etādṛśam kiñcid pramāṇatamam iṣyate svayam kṛtā api tadvayā ākhyā kriyate spaṣṭatā arthataḥ 
AVy_1,1.8–1,1.11	 tatra tārātha mūla tvam sarva śas astrasya ca iṣyate sarvatra anugata tvena pṛthak oṅkriyate akhilaiḥ otatva vācī hi oṅkāraḥ vaktayasau tad guṇa utatām saḥ eva brahma śabda arthaḥ nārāyaṇa pada uditaḥ saḥ eva bharga śabda arthaḥ vyāhṛtīnām ca bhūmataḥ bhāvanāt ca eva sutvāt ca saḥ ayam puruṣaḥ iti api saḥ eva sarva veda arthaḥ jijñāsyaḥ ayam vidhīyate jñānī priyatamaḥ atas me tam vidvān eva ca amṛtaḥ 
AVy_1,1.12–1,1.15	 vṛṇute yam tena labhyaḥ ityāt yukti balena hi jijñāsā uttha jñāna jāt tad prasādāt eva mucyate dravyam karma ca kālaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ jīvaḥ eva ca yat anugrahataḥ santi na santi yat upekṣayā na ṛte tvat kriyate kiñcid iti ādeḥ na harim vinā jñāna svabhāvataḥ api syāt muktiḥ kasya api hi kvacid ajñānām jñāna daḥ viṣṇuḥ jñāninām mokṣa daḥ ca saḥ ānanda daḥ ca muktānām saḥ eva ekaḥ janārdanaḥ 
AVy_1,1.16–1,1.19	 iti ukteḥ bandha mithyātvam na eva muktiḥ apekṣate mithyātvam api bandhasya na pratyakṣa virodhataḥ mithyātvam yadi duḥkha ādeḥ tad vākya agratas bhavet mithyāyāḥ sādhaka tvam ca na siddham prativādinaḥ tat ca mithyā pramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā satā ced dvaita siddhiḥ syāt na siddham ca anya sādhanam sādhaka tvam sataḥ tena sākṣiṇā siddhim icchatā svīkṛtam hi aviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhaka tā punar 
AVy_1,1.20–1,1.23	 tat ca āviśeṣa mānena sādhyam iti anavasthitiḥ anaṅgīkurvatām viśvasatyatām tat na vāditā tasmāt vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satya iti eva vyavasthitāḥ vyāvahārikam etasmāt satyam iti eva ca āgatam vyavahārasataḥ ca api sādhaka tvam tu pūrvavat sattraividhyam ca mānena siddhayet kena iti pṛcchyate tasya api ukta prakāreṇa na eva siddhiḥ kathañcana vailakṣaṇyam sat asatoḥ api etena niṣidhyate 
AVy_1,1.24–1,1.27	 vailakṣaṇyam sataḥ ca api svayam sat bheda vādinaḥ asataḥ ca api viśvasya tena aniṣyam katham bhavet yadi ucyate api sarvasmāt iti sadbheda saṃsthitiḥ sat mātra tvam brahmaṇaḥ api tasmāt tat api naḥ bhavet jñāna bādhya tvam api tu na siddham prativādinaḥ vijñātasya anyathā samyak vijñānam hi eva tat matam asat vilakṣaṇa jñaptyai jñātavyam asat eva hi tasmāt asat pratītiḥ ca katham tena nivāryate 
AVy_1,1.28–1,1.31	 anyathātvam asat tasmāt bhrāntau= eva pratīyate sattvasya asate evam hi svīkārya eva pratīta tā tasya anirvacanīya tve syāt eva hi anavasthitiḥ nirviśeṣe svayam bhāte kim ajñāna āvṛtam bhavetaḥ mithyā viśeṣaḥ api ajñāna siddhim eva hi apekṣate nacāa varaṇam ajñānam asatye tena ca iṣyate aprakāśa svarūpa tvāt jaḍe ajñānam na manyate ajñāna abhāvataḥ śāstram sarvam vyarthībhaviṣyati 
AVy_1,1.32–1,1.35	 ajñānasya ca mithyātvam ajñānāt iti kalpane anavasthitiḥ tathā ca syāt anyonya āśrayatā athavā svabhāva ajñāna vādasya nirdoṣa tvāt na tat bhavet avidyā durghaṭa tvam ced syāt ātmā api hi tādṛśaḥ atas adhikāri viṣaya phala yoga ādi varjitam ananta doṣa duṣṭam ca heyam māyā matam śubhaiḥ satya tvāt tena duḥkha ādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ na brahma tām vadet vedaḥ jīvasya hi kathañcana 
AVy_1,1.36–1,1.39	 yajamāna prastara tvam yathā na arthaḥ śruteḥ bhavet brahma tvam api jīvasya pratyakṣasya aviśeṣataḥ sārvajñi ādi guṇam jīvāt bhinnam jñāpayati śrutiḥ īśam tām upajīvya eva vartate hi aikya vādinī upajīvya virodhena na asya aḥ tat mānatā bhavet svātantrye ca viśiṣṭa tve sthāna mattya aikyayoḥ api sādṛśye ca aikya vāc samyak sa avakāśāḥ yathā iṣyataḥ avakāśa ujkhitā bheda śrutiḥ na atibalā katham 
AVy_1,1.40–1,1.43	 ajñāna asambhavāt eva mithyā bhedaḥ nirākṛtaḥ atas yathā artha bandhasya vinā viṣṇu prasādataḥ anivṛtteḥ tad artham hi jijñāsā atra vidhīyate yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandha apanoda kṛt evam dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryāt bandha vibhedanam kārya tā ca na kācid syāt iṣṭa sādhana tām vinā kāryam na hi kriyā vyāpyam niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ na bhaviṣyat kriyā kāryam srakṣyati īśaḥ iti hi api 
AVy_1,1.44–1,1.47	 kāryam syāt na eva ca akartum aśakyam kāryam iṣyate sāmyāt eva niṣiddhasya tat iṣṭam sādhanam tathā kāryam sādhanam iṣṭasya bhagavān iṣṭadevatā mukhyeṣyam vā sumanasām preyaḥ tat iti ca śrutiḥ prāṇa buddhi manaḥ kha ātma deha apatya dhana ādayaḥ yad samparkāt priyāḥ āsan= tatas kaḥ nu aparaḥ priyaḥ ityādi vākyaiḥ ākāṅkṣā sannidhiḥ yogya tā yatas asmin= eva samastasya itīṣye vyutpattiḥ iṣyate 
AVy_1,1.48–1,1.51	 attya pūpān= tava bhrātā iti ādau= au= āpataḥ api ca udvāpāt vartamāna tvāt ākāṅkṣa ādi balāt api bālaḥ vyutpattim apyeti nānayā ityādi vākyataḥ ānīyamāna dṛṣṭayā eva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati eṣyat ānayanāya ayam kutas eva pratīkṣate vyutpannaḥ vartamāne tu kriyā śabde bhaviṣyati punar dṛṣṭyā eva śabda śrudh paścāt vyutpattim eṣyati vartamānam atītam ca bhaviṣyat iti ca kramāt 
AVy_1,1.52–1,1.55	 ākāṅkṣa ādi yutam yasmāt vidheḥ vyutpādanam kutas dṛṣṭyā jñāta padārthasya pada ākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmāt vatarmāne gate tatas iṣṭam ākāṅkṣate sarvaḥ na pravṛttim apekṣate aparokṣam parokṣam vā jñānam iṣṭasya sādhanam kvāpi ceṣyā tad arthā syāt attiḥ hi rasa vittaye vākya artha jñāna mātreṇa kvacid iṣṭam bhavet api na ca srukasruva vahnayā adāvatāt paryam śruteḥ bhavet 
AVy_1,1.56–1,1.59	 yat kiñcit karaṇa rasya api yajña tā eva anyathā bhavet tasmāt upāsana artham ca sva arthe tātparyavat bhavet iti śabda unnaye agnau= iti unnīte smṛtiḥ bhavet iti śabda vyapetāni hi api santi vacāṃsi alam ātmānam eva ityādīni yoge agnau= api tat samam eka vākya tva yoge tu vedasya api hi aśeṣatas vākya bhedaḥ na yuktaḥ syāt yogaḥ ca syāt mahā phale iti brūyāt iti vacaḥ gatam agnau samīpa gam 
AVy_1,1.60–1,1.63	 kalpanā gauravam ced syāt pṛthak tātparya sambhave kalpanā gauravāt eva padārthāḥ na syuḥ eva hi pramāṇa avagata tvam ced tātparyāṇaśam tathā eva hi tasmāt padārthe vākya arthe tātparyam ubhayatra ca pṛthak eva ca vākya tvam pṛthak anvayataḥ bhavet avāntara tvāt vākyānām vākya bhedaḥ na dūṣaṇam aṅgīkṛta tvāt api taiḥ padārthānām pṛthak pṛthak kriyā padena anvayasya vākya bhedāt hi dūṣaṇam 
AVy_1,1.64–1,1.67	 pratyakṣa ādi virodhe atas gauṇa arthasya api sambhavāt atātparyam padārthe api na kalpyam avirodhataḥ atas jñāna phalāni eva karmāṇi jñānam eva hi mukhya prasāda dam viṣṇoḥ jijñāsāyāḥ ca tat bhavet kartavyā tena jijñāsā śruti prāmāṇya yogataḥ pratyakṣa vat ca prāmāṇyam svatas eva āgamasya hi anavasthā anyathā hi syāt aprāmāṇyam tathā anyatas mithyājñapti pralambha ādeḥ tena veda virodhi yat 
AVy_1,1.68–1,1.71	 na mānam api vedānām aṅgī kāryā hi nitya tā na hi dharma ādi siddhiḥ syāt nitya vākyam vinā kvacid avipralambhaḥ tat jñānam tad kṛta tva ādayaḥ api ca kalpyā gaurava doṣeṇa puṃvākyam jñāpakam na tat pratyakṣaḥ kasyacid dharmaḥ vastu tvāt iti codite na buddhaḥ dharma darśī syāt puṃstvāt iti anumāhatiḥ adharma vādinaḥ vākyam aprayojanam eva hi dharma abhāvaḥ api no tena pratyakṣa avagataḥ bhavet 
AVy_1,1.72–1,1.75	 atas saṃśaya sampattau vākyam pratyakṣa vat pramā śaktiḥ ca eva anvite sva arthe śabdānām anubhūyate atas anvita abhidhāyi tvam gauravam kalpane anyathā naca aśakyā abhidhāyi tvam pravṛttiḥ ca dvidhā anyathā etat sarvam tarkaśāstre brahmatarke hi vistarāt uktam vidyā pṛthaktavāt tu saṅkṣepeṇa atra sūcitam pramāṇa nyāyasa= śikṣā kriyate tarka śāstrataḥ māna nyāyaiḥ tu tad siddhaimīmāṃsāḥ meya śodhanam 
AVy_1,1.76–1,1.79	 brahmatarkam ca bhagavān saḥ eva kṛtavān prabhuḥ pañcāśat koṭi vistārāt nārāyaṇa tanau kṛtāt uddhṛtya pañca sāhasram kṛtavān bādarāyaṇaḥ atas tad artham saṅkṣepāt atas iti abhyasūcayat yatas anubhavataḥ sarvam siddham etat atas api ca devaiḥ ca durgama artheṣu vyāpṛtaḥ na ati vistṛtim cakāra etāḥ hi avajñeyāḥ yuktayaḥ pratipakṣa gāḥ pratyakṣekṣa akṣamaḥ pakṣam kam eva atra abhivīkṣate 
AVy_1,1.80–1,1.83	 tasmāt akṣama pakṣa tvāt mokṣa śāstre abhyupekṣitaḥ svayam bhagavatā viṣṇuḥ brahma iti etat purā uditam sa viṣṇuḥ āha hīyante deva śāstrasya tena hi ādi antam deva śāstrasya svayam bhagavatā kṛtam madhyam tad ājñayā paila śeṣābhyām kṛtam añjasā atas tatra eva viṣṇu tva siddheḥ brahma iti asūcayat doṣa ara= chidra śabdānām paryāya tvam yatas tatas guṇāḥ nārāḥ iti jñeyaḥ tadvān nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVy_1,1.84–1,1.87	 brahma śabdaḥ api hi guṇa pūrtim eva vadati ayam atas nārāyaṇasya eva jijñāsā atra vidhīyate siddha tvāt brahma śabdasya viṣṇau spaṣṭa tayā śrutau ambhasi apāraḥ iti uktaḥ nārāyaṇa pada īḥ itaḥ āpaḥ nārāḥ iti hi āha saḥ eva apsu antarīritaḥ kāmataḥ vidhi rudrā ādi pada dātṛyā svayam śriyā yoni tvena ātmanaḥ viṣṇoḥ tiṣṭhanti iti uditasya ca yasmin devāḥ adhi iti uktavā samudram sthānam eva ca 
AVy_1,1.88–1,1.91	 nāma ca akṣaram iti eva ṛcaḥ iti uditam tu yat yatas prasūtā iti uktavā ca tat eva brahma ca abravīt antar samudra gam viśva prasūteḥ kāraṇa ṭha tu yat sūkta upaniṣad ādi uktam janma ādyasya iti lakṣyate sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiḥ ca saṃhāraḥ niyatiḥ jñānam āvṛtiḥ bandha mokṣau= api hi āsu śrutiṣu uktāḥ hareḥ sadā yam nāmāni viśanti addhā yaḥ devānām iti hi api śruteḥ nāmāni sarvāṇi viṣṇoḥ eva yatas tatas 
AVy_1,1.92–1,1.95	 atas na mukhyatas nāma tad anyasya hi kasyacid guṇāḥ śrutāḥ iti hi asmāt na doṣaḥ arthaḥ śruteḥ bhavet prītyā mokṣa paratvāt ca tātparyam na eva dūṣaṇe sarveṣām api vākyānām mahātātparyam atra hi tad virodhe na māna tvam phalam muktiḥ hi vākyataḥ na purāṇa ādi māna tvam viruddha arthe śruteḥ bhavet darśana antara mūla tvāt moha artham ca ājñayā hareḥ na sarvanāma tā anyeṣām śrutau= uktā hi kutracid 
AVy_1,1.96–1,1.99	 adoṣa vacanāt ca eva niyamena hareḥ śrutau ajñānam pāratantryam ca praaye abhāvaḥ eva ca aśaktiḥ coditāni eṣām sarveṣām api ca śrutau janma ādyasya iti tena etat viṣṇoḥ eva sva lakṣaṇam asya udbhava ādi hetu tvam sākṣāt eva sva lakṣaṇam kṛṣṇaddhayā na= chalena eva svayam bhāgavate abravīt atas jīva aikyam api sa nirācakre jagadguruḥ na hi janma ādi hetu tvam jīvasya jagataḥ bhavet 
AVy_1,1.100–1,1.103	 hita akriyā ādi doṣam ca vakṣyati eva svayam prabhuḥ nirguṇa tvam ca tena eva niṣiddham prabhuṇā svayam bhedena eva tu mukhya artha sambhave lakṣaṇā kutas katham nitya guṇasya asya syāt aikyam guṇa hānataḥ sadā eva guṇavat tve asya bhinnam syāt nirguṇam sadā na ca mithyā guṇa tvam syāt anirvācyasya dūṣaṇāt nirguṇa tvam tadā ca syāt āsura tvam na ca anyathā lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā yadi vā ubhayam 
AVy_1,1.104–1,1.107	 iti pṛṣṭe tad aikyasya gatiḥ eva na vidyate aikya abhede na śāstreṇa jñeyam tat sva prakāśataḥ bhede mithyātvataḥ bheda satya tvam syāt balāt api bheda abhedau yadi tadā syāt eva hi anavasthitiḥ sva nirvāhaka tā ced syāt bāhyam bāhakam iti api paryāyaḥ bhedavān vā syāt anavasthobhayatra ca satya jñāna ādike api eva na vyāvṛttyā prayojanam vyāvṛttasya aviśeṣa tve tat akhaṇḍam ca khaṇḍitam nirviśeṣa tvam etena mūkaḥ aham iti vat bhavet 
AVy_1,1.108–1,1.111	 abhinne api viśeṣaḥ ayam balāt āpatati hi atas viśeṣa tadvatoḥ ca eva sva nirvāhaka tā bhavet bheda hīne tu aparyāya śabda antara niyāmakaḥ viśeṣaḥ nāma kathitaḥ saḥ asti vastuṣu aśeṣatas viśeṣāḥ te api anantāḥ ca paraspara viśeṣiṇaḥ sva nirvāhaka tā yuktāḥ santi vastuṣu aśeṣatas atas ananta guṇam brahma nirbhedam api bhaṇyate evam dharmān iti śrutyā tad abhedaḥ api udīryate 
AVy_1,1.112–1,1.115	 śaiva ādi āgama samprāpta dṛṣṭa gena phalena tu tad vākya upamaya anyat ca pramāṇa tve anumīyate īśa vākya tvataḥ iti ced tad gavya bhicāriṇā aprāmāṇya anumā ca syāt na pṛthak ca anumeśvare puṃstva hetu balāt eva pūrva uktena eva vartmanā śāstra yoni tvam etena kāraṇasya balāt bhavet na aveda vid na tarkeṇa matiḥ ityādi vākyataḥ tarkaḥ jñāpayitum śaktaḥ na īśitāram kathañcana 
AVy_1,1.116–1,1.118	 vana kṛt tvā ādi rūpeṇa pakṣa bhūtasya ca īśituḥ kiñcid jñānam hi puṃstvena śakyam sādhayitum sukham vṛkṣa kṛt na akhilam vṛkṣam vetti puṃstvāt hi caitra vat ityādi anumayā spardhi na anumānam pareśituḥ śaktam vijñāpane ca atiprasaṅgaḥ anumaya īdṛśāḥ vastu tvāt turagaḥ śṛṅgī puṣpa vat kham sutaiḥ yutā citriṇī ca rasaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ rasa tvāt sa uttaraḥ bhavet upakrama ādi liṅgebhyaḥ na anyāsyāt anumā tatas 
AVy_1,1.119–1,1.122	 te eva anvaya nāmānaḥ taiḥ samyak pravicārite mukhya arthaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva śāstrasya na aparaḥ īkṣaṇīya tvataḥ viṣṇuḥ vācyaḥ eva naca anyathā lakṣya tvam kvāpi dṛṣṭam hi kim tat iti anavasthitiḥ mādhurya ādi viśeṣāḥ ca tad śabdaiḥ uditāḥ sadā vākya arthaḥ api hi vākya artha śabdena eva uditaḥ bhavet na avācyam tena kiñcid syāt yatas iti ādikaiḥ vadan avācya tvam katham brūyāt mūkaḥ aham iti vat sudhīḥ 
AVy_1,1.123–1,1.125	 yena lakṣyam iti proktam lakṣya śabdena saḥ avadat ekasya api hi śabdasya gauṇa artha svīkṛtau satām mahatī jāyate lajjā yatra tatra akhilāḥ ravāḥ amukhya arthāḥ iti vadan yaḥ tad mārga anuvartinām katham na jāyate lajjā vaktum śābda tvam ātmanaḥ ātma brahma ādayaḥ śabdāḥ sākṣāt pūrṇa abhidhāyinaḥ janma ādi kāraṇam brahma lakṣitam ca yadā tadā 
AVy_1,1.126–1,1.129	 vandhyā putra upamam māyā śabalam vācyam iti api kalpayitvā vinā mānam lakṣyam śuddham vadan padaiḥ ātma śabda uditasya eva jñānam muktauvasādhanam āha śruta parityāgaḥ syāt ca asya aśruta kalpanam syāt sarvatra ca yatra ekam api lokaḥ jugupsate niyamena ubhayam syāt hi yasya sva parayoḥ mate alaṅkṛtaḥ sadā eva ayam durghaṭaiḥ eva bhūṣaṇaiḥ andhantamaḥ nityu duḥkham tasya syāt vasana dvayam 
AVy_1,1.130–1,1.133	 anandāḥ nāma te lokāḥ andhena tamasā avṛtāḥ tān= te pretya abhigacchanti avidvāṃsaḥ budhaḥ janāḥ asuryāḥ nāma te lokāḥ andhena tamasā avṛtāḥ tān= te pretya abhigacchanti ye keca ātmahanaḥ janāḥ iti ādi śrutayaḥ mānam śataśas atra samantataḥ heya tva avacanāt ca eva na ātmā gauṇaḥ śrutau śrutaḥ tam eva ekam jānathā anyāḥ vācaḥ muñcatha ca iti ha uktaḥ ātmā katham gauṇaḥ heya pakṣe hi asau śrutaḥ 
AVy_1,1.134–1,1.137	 parivāra tayā grāhyāḥ api heyāḥ pradhānataḥ pūrṇasya pūrṇam ādāya pūrṇam eva avaśiṣyate iti svasya eva pūrṇasya pūrṇe api ayaḥ udāhṛtaḥ katham māyā vyavacchinnaḥ pūrṇaḥ mukhya tayā bhavet padam ca nirguṇaḥ iti katham gauṇam vadiṣyati guṇa abhāva upalakṣyam ced padam tat api vācakam atas anavasthiti mukha sarva doṣa mahā āspadam katham etat matam sadbhiḥ ādriyeta vicakṣaṇaiḥ 
AVy_1,1.138–1,1.141	 na ca sāṅkhayaniḥ ākṛtyai sūtrāṇi etāni acīkpad bhagavān na hi aśabda tvam pradhāne aṅgīkaroti asau samanvaye pratijñāte śabda gocara tā eva hi prathama pratipādyā syāt tad abhāve kutas anvayaḥ katham ca lakṣaṇa āvādī brūyāt brahma samanvayam yaḥ asau śabdasya mukhya arthaḥ tatra eva syāt samanvayaḥ janma ādi kāraṇe sākṣāt āha devaḥ samanvayam uktam tat eva jijñāsyam kva avakāśaḥ atra nirguṇe 
AVy_1,1.142–1,1.145	 kathañca asambhavaḥ tasya mukhya arthasya nirākṛtau mānena kena vijñeyam avācyā jñeya nirguṇam ameyam ced na śāstrasya tatra vṛttiḥ kathañcana tasmāt śāstreṇa jijñāsyam asmadīyam guṇa arṇavam vāsudeva ākhyam advandvam param brahma akhila uttamam vijñeya vācya lakṣya tva pūrva aśeṣa viśeṣataḥ nirgatam manasaḥ vācaḥ yadi tat syāt agocaram astu tat mā vadet vādī na ca asmad śāstra gam tu tat 
AVy_1,1.146–1,1.149	 avācyam vācyam iti uktavā kim iti unmatta vat mṛṣā asmad śāstrasya cauryāya yatate svokti dūṣakaḥ janma ādi kāraṇam yat tat sākṣāt nārāyaṇa abhidham vadantu śrutayaḥ brahma śāstram ca etat tad arthataḥ sva prakāśa tvam api tu yaiḥ jñānasya nivāritam katham sarvajña tā tasya sva jñāna adhigamam vinā pravṛttamastu avācyam te mā eva brūyāḥ kathañcana sarva śabdaiḥ avācyam tat uktavā tad viṣayam punar 
AVy_1,1.150–1,1.152	 vayam tvām śruti yuktibhyām baddhvā asmad śāstram añjasā vicārayāmaḥ śrutibhiḥ yuktibhiḥ ca eva sa ādaram adbhuta tvāt avācyam tat atarkya ājñeyam eva ca ananta guṇa pūrṇa tvāt iti ūde paiṅginām śrutiḥ avācyam iti loke api vaktayāḥ cāryatamam bhuvi evam śāstrau= agamya tve vibhāgena samanvayam ānanda mayaḥ ityādinā dhyāyena vadati ajaḥ 
AVy_1,1.153–1,1.156	 tatra anyatra prasiddhānām viṣṇau= eva samanvayam śabdānām prathame pāde guṇi sāmānya vācinām guṇa vācinām ca prathamam āha devaḥ samanvayam samudra śāyinam sarva prasūti prasavam śrutiḥ tat eva brahma paramam iti sāvadhṛtiḥ jagau yatas atas brahma śabdasya tatra eva niyata tvataḥ yaḥ annam brahma ityādi rūpāt abhyāsāt taittirīyake anyāsu ca etad rūpāsu śākhāsu api sahasraśas 
AVy_1,1.157–1,1.160	 ānanda mayaḥ ityādyaiḥ śabdaiḥ vācyaḥ hariḥ svayam upalakṣaṇa tvam śabdānām ānanda maya pūrviṇām sūtrasya alpa akṣara tvena sarva śākhā vinirṇaye punar ca prāpakāt hetoḥ tatra adhikaraṇa antaram sarve vedāḥ āmananti yat padam tu iti hi śrutiḥ ānanda maya rūpe tu brahmaṇaḥ pucchatā uktitaḥ samasta abrahma tā prāpteḥ ānanda maya nāma hi brahma śabdasya ca abhyāsāt pañca rūpa ādiṣu sphuṭam 
AVy_1,1.161–1,1.164	 brahma tā avayave api syāt tathā avayavini svatas yathā eva kṛṣṇa keśasya kṛṣṇasya brahma tā akhilāḥ darśitā ca eva pārthāya niḥsīmāḥ śaktayaḥ asya hi ṛtam satyam param brahma puruṣam kṛṣṇa piṅgalam viṣṇu ākhyam uktam anyatra hi ūrdhvaretam ca tat prati virūpākṣa ākhyam avaram brahma uktam tat vrate sthitam samāna adhikṛta tvam ced uttaram nīlalohitam kṛṣṇa piṅgala rūpeṇa punaruktam bhaviṣyati 
AVy_1,1.165–1,1.168	 brahma adhipatiḥ iti atra tāpanīya śrutau puras svarita brahma śabda antam bahu vrīhi tvam eṣyati svāhā indra śatru vardhasva yat bahu vrīhitām agāt mahāvyākaraṇe sūtram iti svara vinirṇaye pūrva anta svarite puṃsoḥ bahu vrīhi tvam eṣyati mahāvyākaraṇe sūtram iti svara vinirṇaye ṛtam satyam param brahma ityādi uddeśya dvitīyakāḥ vibhaktiḥ ūrdhvareta ādiḥ prathamā rudra gocarāḥ 
AVy_1,1.169–1,1.172	 tasmāt viṣṇum param brahma prati rudraḥ vrate sthitaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ iti hi eva śruti arthaḥ avasitaḥ bhavet ṛtam satyam param brahma prati viṣṇum sadāśivaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ dhyāyati ha śaṅkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ iti artham etam eva āha nīlagrīva śrutiḥ parā ārtharvaṇī param brahma tasmāt ekaḥ hariḥ śrutau tat eva ṛtam iti prāha katham eva anyathā śrutiḥ avadhārayantī tasya eva hi ṛta tva ādikam añjasā 
AVy_1,1.173–1,1.176	 ekaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ vāsudevaḥ agre eva āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ na indra sūryau na ca guhaḥ na somaḥ na vināyakaḥ ityādi vākyataḥ viṣṇoḥ utpattiḥ avatāra gāḥ mukhyam brahma hariḥ tasmāt prastāvaḥ param iti api mukhya brahma grahe yukte na amukhyam yujyate kvacid asambhave hi mukhyasya gauṇa artha aṅgīkṛtiḥ bhavet prācurya arthāḥ ca mayaṭaḥ sarve atra pratipāditāḥ 
AVy_1,1.177–1,1.180	 bhogya tvam atra ca adya tvam upajīvyatayā hareḥ mahā bhoktā mahā bhogyaḥ iti arthaḥ anna maye bhavet mahā prāṇaḥ mahā bodhaḥ mahāvijñānavān api viśeṣa sāmānyatayā vijñānam manaḥ iti api ekasya jñāna rūpasya hareḥ uktiḥ vibhāgataḥ abhede api viśeṣeṇa eva anyaḥ iti uditaḥ hariḥ bheda śabdāḥ viśeṣam tu harau= anyatra bhinna tvāt brūyuḥ hareḥ jīva jaḍaiḥ api bhedam hi mukhyatas 
AVy_1,1.181–1,1.184	 brahma tarka vacaḥ api evam atas ekaḥ sa pañcadhā uktaḥ anna mayaḥ ityādi bhṛgoḥ ca etat vadiṣyati prāpya tvena mayaṭprokteḥ na tatra api anyat ucyate pracura anna ādiḥ eva atas hi annamat namayā iti api ucyate hi aviśeṣeṇa na anyat kiñcid iha ucyate mahā ānanda tvaḥ eva asya hetuḥ kaḥ anyāt iti sphuṭam uktaḥ śruti antare yasmāt sukham labdhvā karoti ayam karoti na asukhī bhūmā sukham na alpe sukham bhavet 
AVy_1,1.185–1,1.188	 iti uktam yat pravṛttiḥ ca nṛtta gāna ādikā sukhāt duḥkhāt rodādikā ca eva sarva kartṛ tvataḥ asya ca sarva śakteḥ na duḥkham syāt atas kevala līlayā pravartakaḥ na ced eṣa prāṇyāt anyāt ca kaḥ pumān brahma vid param āpnoti iti yat prathama sūcitam tat eva mantra varṇena satyam jñānam ananta vat lakṣitam tatra satya tvam sṛṣṭayā anna prāṇayoḥ api uktam jñānam tu manasā vijñānena api udīritam 
AVy_1,1.189–1,1.192	 ananta tvam tathā ananda maya vācā api udāhṛtam sadbhāvam yāpayet yasmāt satyam tat tena kathyate iti sṛṣṭiḥ iha proktā jagat sadbhāvayāpakam brahma iti sthāpanāya eva sattvam jīvanam eva ca viśīrṇa tā ca sattvam syāt sannam iti āhuḥ eva yat atas adyatāt tṛta anna tvam satya śabda arthaḥ eva hi prāṇam devāḥ anuprāṇanti manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ ca ye āyuḥ prāṇaḥ hi bhūtānām iti yat gati jīvane 
AVy_1,1.193–1,1.196	 ukte saditi dhātu arthaḥ gatiḥ ca atas hi satya tā prāṇa tvam avabodha arthaḥ manudhātuḥ prakīrtitaḥ na alpe sukham iti proktayā eva ānanda maya tā uktitaḥ ananta tvam sunirṇītam pūrṇa ānandaḥ hi na alpake atas hi mantra varṇa ukta vistṛtiḥ tu samastayā kriyate parayā yasmāt itaraḥ atra na kathyate puruṣam vetti yaḥ mucyet na anyaḥ panthāḥ hi vidyate iti śruteḥ anyavedī katham muktim prayāsyati 
AVy_1,1.197–1,1.200	 puruṣaḥ paraḥ ātmā ajaḥ brahma nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ mahān ānandaḥ ud viṣṇuḥ bhargaḥ omaḥ iti īryate svayam nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ na anyasya etāni kasyacid tasmāt om iti udāhṛtya yajña dāna ādi kurvate sūktena pauruṣeṇa enam yajanti adhyātma kovidāḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ tena na anya jñānāt vimucyate brahma śabda udite tasmin= ātma śabdam prayujya ca tasmāt ākāśa sṛṣṭim ca provāca atra catuvirdhām 
AVy_1,1.201–1,1.204	 bhūtam bhūta abhimānī ca tad dehaḥ antar niyāmakaḥ hariḥ ca ākāśa śabda uktaḥ mukhyatas hariḥ eva ca ā samantāt kāśate yat ākāśaḥ mukhyatas hariḥ bala jñāna svarūpa tvāt vāyuḥ agniḥ agam nayan āpaḥ āpālanāt ca eva pṛthivī prathitaḥ yatas uṣyānām āśraya tvena saḥ eva uṣadhi nāmakaḥ oṣadhīṣu sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ kṣudhitaiḥ āśritaḥ bhavet puri śete yatas saḥ atha puruṣaḥ ca iti gīyate 
AVy_1,1.205–1,1.208	 kriyā pravartaka tvena prādurbhāvaḥ hareḥ janiḥ ākāśa ādiṣu na anyā asti hi abhimānaḥ abhimāninaḥ abhimāni śarīrasya sākṣāt bhūtasya ca udbhavaḥ evam deha ādi paryantam āgatam harim eva tu parāmṛśati tasya eva pañca rūpa tva vittaye tyaktavā bhūta ādikam sarvam sa vai eṣaḥ iti śrutiḥ saḥ iti ātma pada uddiṣṭaḥ eṣa jīva śarīra gaḥ sāra anna mayaḥ eva ayam na loka anna mayaḥ prabhuḥ 
AVy_1,1.209–1,1.212	 iti tam rasa śabdena viśinaṣṭi śarīra gam idam iti eva nirdeśaḥ vastra prāvṛta vat vibhoḥ śiraḥ ādeḥ bhavet jīvaśiraḥ ādau vyavasthiteḥ tam viditvā asya muktiḥ syāt na anya jñānāt kathañcana āditye puruṣe ca ayam iti bheda upadeśataḥ na asya abhedaḥ asti jīvena na anumā kāma cāriṇī vimatāni śarīrāṇi mad bhoga āyatanāni yat śarīrāṇi iti ādikā tu tattva jñāne hi apekṣyate 
AVy_1,1.213–1,1.215	 pratyakṣa ādi viruddha tvāt akṣa āgama bhaya ujkhitā anumā kāma vṛttā hi kutra na avasaram vrajet jaḍaḥ ātmā eva vastu tvāt prameya tvāt jaḍam citiḥ ghanaḥ ākāśaḥ ityādyāḥ vāryante kena hetunā na jīva bheda sūtrāṇām śaṅkayā atra punar ukta tā vākya antara dyotaka tvāt pṛthak iti atra pūrṇa tā yogam annamayādyaiḥ yat phala tvena asya śaṃsati sthāna dvaye api atas kośāḥ ete iti ati sāhasam 
AVy_1,1.216–1,1.219	 upasaṅkramaṇam ca eva dvitīya uddeśitam prati atikramam vadantam tam upaśabdaḥ nivārayet aśrutasya ati śabdasya sthānam dadyāt katham punar śruta aśruta parityāga kalpane vigata hriyām mṛtau= eva parityāgaḥ kṛtaḥ hi anna mayasya ca ye annam brahma ityādi upāsām sāmāna adhikaraṇyataḥ uktavā pañca svarūpāṇām punar tad prāpti vādinī sthāna dvaya gatā veda vāṇī tad apalāpinām 
AVy_1,1.220–1,1.223	 tamasaḥ anyatra saṃsthānam katham eva saheta sā adhīhi bhagavaḥ brahma iti uktaḥ anna prāṇa pūrvakam āha brahma katham tat na dvāram tat iti vādinaḥ upasattim katham vidyuḥ upasannāya hi triśas vaktavyam brahma guruṇā catur vāram atha api vā sakṛt vā iti āgamā brūyuḥ sampradāya vidaḥ api ca tat yat kiñcid katham brūyāt upasannāya dikpatiḥ na vadet brahma ca katham māyāvī na hi vārirāj 
AVy_1,1.224–1,1.227	 caṣṭaḥ iti eva tat cakṣuḥ śravaṇāt śrotram ucyate vacanāt eva vāc brahma sṛṣṭi sthiti ādi kāraṇam tat ca vā āghūla śākhāyām aṣṭa rūpam udāhṛtam vijñāna ānanda sahitam pṛthak sṛṣṭayā ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ āvāpa udvāpa taṣa śākhāḥ yatas āhuḥ param padam yatas bhūtāni jāyante ityādyaiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ svayam lakṣitam guruṇā paścāt tapasā eva aparokṣataḥ dṛṣṭvā ekaikam svarūpam tu samasta ukta anudarśanam 
AVy_1,1.228–1,1.230	 icchatā ajñām guroḥ prāpya tapasā evāra ukṣitam abrahma iti eva vadatām śruta hānyaśruta grahau sākṣāt lakṣaṇa tām prāptau= iti lajjā tad uktiṣu samīpe saha bhogasya mukti tvena uktitaḥ asakṛt bhedaḥ jīveśayoḥ mithyā iti eva mithyā svayam bhavet etena mayaṭaḥ ca eva dvaividhyena artha kalpanāt tad anyeṣām matam api sat saṃsatsu na bhāsate 
AVy_1,1.231–1,1.234	 atas nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ niḥśeṣa guṇa vācakaiḥ guṇi sāmānya vacanaiḥ api mukhya tayā uditaḥ adhyātma gaiḥ ca prāṇa ādyaiḥ tathā eva hi adhibhūta gaiḥ anna ādi śabdaiḥ bhagavān ekaḥ mukhya tayā uditaḥ janma ādyasya iti sūtreṇa guṇa sarva sva siddhaye brahmaṇaḥ lakṣaṇam proktam śāstra mūlam yatas tatas anvayaḥ sarva śabdānām guṇa sarva sva vedakaḥ śabda pravṛtti hetūnām tasmin mukhya samanvayāt 
AVy_1,1.235–1,1.238	 anya artheṣu alpatā hetoḥ tad nimitta tvataḥ tathā tad vācaka tvam śabdānām bahula ati prayogataḥ rūḍham iti eva sādhyam syāt rūḍhiḥ hi dvividhā matā avidvat vidvat āptyā eva mukhyāḥ hi viduṣām tu sā vidvat rūḍhiḥ vaidikā syāt sā yogāt eva labhyate tasmāt mukhyā artha tā viṣṇoḥ iti kṛtvā hṛdi prabhuḥ samanvayam sādhayati devānām tatra śakta tām āśaṅkaya tatra rūḍhim ca tad śabdānām api svayam 
AVy_1,1.239–1,1.242	 samudra anta sthita tva ādyaiḥ tad dharmaiḥ viṣṇu rūḍha tām sādhayitvā abhidām taiḥ ca punar eva nyavārayat ceṣṭā hi cetanānām yā sā bhavet tad prasādataḥ acetana svabhāvaḥ tu vivara ādiḥ katham tatas iti śaṅkā nivṛtti artham ākāśaḥ iti nāma ca paratas api varīyaḥ tu apūrvāt liṅgāt hareḥ bhavet iti śaṅkā nivṛtti artham ākāśaḥ iti nāma ca paratas api varīyaḥ tva pūrvāt liṅgāt hareḥ bhavet 
AVy_1,1.243–1,1.246	 prāṇa ādi hetuta adṛṣṭeḥ ati deśaḥ hi tādṛśaḥ liṅgam balavat eva syāt prerakaḥ asya api yat hariḥ nitya tvāt eva śabdasya tad svabhāvaḥ katham hareḥ katham prasiddha bahula śabdānām ayathārtha tā iti ced tad hareḥ eva bāhulyāt śruti liṅgayoḥ tādṛśa tvāt ca tad śakteḥ bāhulye śruti liṅgayoḥ anyasya mukhya vācya tvam iti tad na atra gasya hi viṣṇoḥ eva tu liṅgāni prāṇa sthāni tu sarvaśas 
AVy_1,1.247–1,1.252	 prāṇa saṃvāda pūrvāṇi mukhyatas jīvagāni ca abhyārcat śata varṣāṇi prāṇa vaṃśa tvam iti api tasmāt anyatragaiḥ śabdaiḥ ukta nyāyaiḥ samantataḥ ekaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ bhaṇyate na atra saṃśayaḥ vāsudeva ādi rūpeṇa catur mūrtiḥ ca sarvaśas athavā pañcamūrtiḥ sa proktaḥ adhikaraṇam prati pratisūtram pratipadam pratyakṣaram atha api vā taiḥ taiḥ yukti śruti nyāya viśeṣaiḥ yogya tā yathā bṛhat tantra pramāṇena bahu artham api saṅgrahāt ucyate nara buddhīnām api kiñcid graha arthataḥ granthaḥ ayam api bahu arthaḥ bhāṣyam ca atyartha vistaram bahu jñāḥ eva jānanti viśeṣaṇa artham etayoḥ tasmāt mahā guṇaḥ viṣṇuḥ nāmnā āya punaruktitaḥ 
AVy_1,2.1–1,2.4	 liṅga ātmakānām śabdānām vṛttiḥ nārāyaṇe pare cintyate sarvaga tvam tu prathamam pravicāryate tatra tatra sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ tad tad śakti prabodhakaḥ dūratas api atiriktaḥ sa līlayā kevalam prabhuḥ iti jñāpayitum karma kartroḥ utsargataḥ bhidā abhedaḥ api viśeṣe syāt balī saḥ api anapoditaḥ etat bhāva abhidham liṅgam kriyā liṅge tatas param antaryāmī antaraḥ ca iti kriyā bhāva ākhyam ucyate 
AVy_1,2.5–1,2.8	 adṛśya tva ādi abhāva ākhyam śrutiḥ liṅga adhikā parā anitya tvāt kriyāṇām tu katham eva svarūpa tā iti ced sa viśeṣaḥ api kriyā śaktayā ātmanā sthiraḥ śakti tā vyakta tā ca iti viśeṣaḥ api viśeṣavān abhinnaḥ api kriyā ādiḥ ca svabhāvaḥ iti hi śrutiḥ jñānam nityam kriyā nityāḥ balam śaktiḥ para ātmanaḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca āha śakti sadbhāvaḥ eva tu kriyā ādi nitya tā jñeyā tad anyatra tu anitya tā 
AVy_1,2.9–1,2.12	 iti sat tattva vacanam dvi tvam ca ekasya yujyate yaḥ setuḥ iti ca eka tva vacanena viśeṣaṇāt antar sthitvā ramaṇa kṛt antaraḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ramaṇam ca ātma śabdena ādeyam mātī iti ca ucyate viśiṣṭa sukha vat tvāt ca brahma tvam ca viśiṣṭa tā anyonya niyatiḥ ca īśa ni yame na anyathā bhavet cetanānām viśeṣaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ api īśvara apirtaḥ anyonya niyame tasmāt anavasthiti asambhavau 
AVy_1,2.13–1,2.15	 īśvaraḥ ced niyantā ca saḥ eva prathama āgataḥ kim iti apodyate kasmāt vṛthā avasthiti kalpanā doṣavatī eva tasmāt sā na eva kāryā kathañcana ramaṇam na ati yatnasya vikṣepāt eva yujyate iti ced sarva niyamaḥ yasya kasmāt na śakyate ātmanā aniyatam vastu pratīpam hi ātmanaḥ bhavet svādhīna sattā śaktayā ādi katham ātma pratīpakam 
AVy_1,2.16–1,2.19	 guṇa kriyā ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ yat ivā syuḥ abhedinaḥ abhedaḥ abhāva dharmāṇām brahmaṇā yujyate katham na abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ iti ca viśeṣaḥ prāyaśas bhavet atadbhāvaḥ anya tā ca iti na viśeṣaḥ asti kaścana doṣa abhāvaḥ guṇaḥ iti prasiddhaḥ laukikeṣu api adṛśya tva ādikān= tasmāt guṇān āha svayam prabhuḥ bhāva abhāva virodhaḥ api na tu sarvatra vidyate tad abhāvaḥ hi tad bhāva virodhī na tatas aparaḥ 
AVy_1,2.20–1,2.23	 pṛthaktava abhāva tad rūpān bhedān= trīn kalpayanti ced kalpanā gaurava ādyāḥ tu doṣāḥ tatra virodhinaḥ pṛthak tava anyatva bhedāḥ tu paryāyeṇa eva laukikaiḥ vyavahriyante satatam vaidikaiḥ api sarvaśas dṛṣṭa hāniḥ adṛṣṭasya kalpanā iti eva dūṣaṇam yadā tad adhikaḥ doṣaḥ vidyate kaḥ nu vādinām bhāva abhāva svarūpāḥ tu viśeṣāḥ eva vastunaḥ abhinnāḥ eva saṅgrāhyā vyavahāra prasiddhaye 
AVy_1,2.24–1,2.27	 yathā ekaḥ samavāyaḥ api bheda abhedau ca vastuni aṅgīkāryāḥ viśeṣeṇa sthāneṣu vyavahartṛbhiḥ akhaṇḍa vādinaḥ a pi syāt viśeṣaḥ anicchataḥ api asau vyāvṛtte nirviśeṣe tu kim vyāvartyabahutvataḥ bahu liṅga samāyuktaiḥ bahubhiḥ rūḍha nāmabhiḥ prasiddhaiḥ anya ga tvena vācyaḥ sākṣāt janārdanaḥ vaiśvānara ādayaḥ śabdāḥ api tad vācinaḥ tatas tāni liṅgāni te śabdāḥ api tad gāḥ hi sarvaśas bahulāpyajña rūḍhiḥ tad prajñā ārūḍhim na bādhate 
AVy_1,3.1–1,3.4	 tatra anyatra ca siddhānām liṅganāmnām punar hariḥ viśeṣāt mukhyatas vṛttim svasmin= eva atra vaktaya jaḥ viṣṇau= eva ātma śabdasya rūḍha tvāt na śiva ādikān śrutiḥ vakti akhila īśa tvāt bhūmāḥ viṣṇuḥ sukha adhikaḥ atas viruddha vat bhātam api vyākhyāya tattvataḥ yojanīyam harau vākyam viruddhaiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ yutam brahma eva tāni liṅgāni tat anyatra tvasanti api avirodhena govinde santi asthūla ādikāni ca 
AVy_1,3.5–1,3.8	 anya vastu svabhāvānām sthaulya ādīnām apākṛtim nārāyaṇe śrutiḥ vakti na tu tasya asvabhāva tām sarva dharmā sarva nāmā sarva karmā guṇāḥ śrutāḥ doṣāḥ śrutāḥ ca na ityādyā pramāṇam śrutiḥ atra ca liṅgam sādhāraṇam śabdau sthānam liṅgam anugrahaḥ punar śabdāḥ liṅga śabdau vicāryāḥ dvi sthitāḥ iha bāhulyam liṅga śabdānām anuktiḥ ca viruddha tā adṛṣṭiḥ anvaya abhāvaḥ viparīta śruti bhramaḥ 
AVy_1,3.9–1,3.11	 liṅga avakāśarāhiti a bhramaḥ tādṛś dvayam tathā bahu tādṛś tavam uktasya virodhaḥ arthāt tathā gatiḥ samastam etat iti atra pūrva pakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ tāḥ eva balavantaḥ tu gati antara vivarjitāḥ siddhānta yuktayaḥ jñeyāḥ dṛśyante tāḥ ca sarvaśas mukta upasṛpyatā prāṇāt ādhikyam sarvatas tathā vailakṣaṇyam svabhāvasya prekṣā pūrva kriyā tathā 
AVy_1,3.12–1,3.15	 arasya ṇyasya ca īśa tvam sūrya ādi anukṛtiḥ tathā vāmana ākhyā sarva kampaḥ tad śabda an anya siddha tā anāma rūpa tā bhedasya upajīvya pramāṇa tā sarva aiśvarya ādika ādyāḥ tāḥ veda īśena pradarśitāḥ adhikāraḥ ca tad hāniḥ prasaṅgāt eva cintitau tad phalāya vidhiḥ siddhe ca upāsāyāḥ nirākṛtaḥ yatas jaimininā anya artham asiddhe arthe vidhiḥ tathā vidyā adhirājasya matam avirodhaḥ tayoḥ tatas 
AVy_1,3.16–1,3.19	 mokṣe phala viśeṣaḥ asti na ca sarvam prakāśate sarvadā tena devānām api yuktā hi upāsanāḥ nityam vṛddhi kṣaya apetam viṣṇoḥ pūrṇam tu vedanam spaṣṭa ati spaṣṭa viśadam brahmaṇaḥ aśeṣa vastu gam anyeṣām kramaśas jñānam mita vastu gatam sadā ityādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ tu sadā vidyā pateḥ hṛdi jaimini ādyāḥ tu sāmānya vettṛ tvāt tat tathā avadan vidyeśa m atam etasmāt na eva sadbhiḥ viruddhayate 
AVy_1,4.1–1,4.4	 duḥkhi baddha avara ādyāḥ tu tad adhīna tva hetutaḥ śabdāḥ brahmaṇi vartante rājñi yadvat parājayaḥ svātantryam tad gata tvam ca śabda vṛtteḥ hi kāraṇam svātantryam tatra mukhyam syāt kutas rājñi jayaḥ anyathā na hi bhṛtyasya vijayi śabdaḥ tāvat prayujyate yāvat rājñi anya ga tve api svātantrya ābhāsa mātrataḥ bhṛtya bandha ādikam rājñi rājñaḥ bandha ādi yogyataḥ kāraṇam saṃśayasya syāt iti na eva prayujyate 
AVy_1,4.5–1,4.8	 amaṅgala tvāt śabdānām rājñā yogāt amaṅgale apriya tvāt tu śabdasya syāt prayoga nivartanam guṇāḥ tu tādṛśāḥ yatra prayujyante akhilāḥ api pūjyeṣu eva viśeṣeṇa svātantryam mukhya kāraṇam tatas doṣa atidūra tvāt saṃśayasya api asambhavāt doṣāṇām viṣṇu ga tvasya prājña buddhi vyapekṣayā svātantrya artham abhipretya doṣa śabdāḥ ca viṣṇavi vāsudeva śrutiḥ ca āha na eva viṣṇau= amaṅgalam 
AVy_1,4.9–1,4.12	 maṅgala amaṅgale anyatra tatas na amaṅgalam vadet svātantrya apekṣayā viṣṇau doṣaḥ na amaṅgala uktitaḥ bahu bhuktavam yathā doṣaḥ nṛṣu na eva harau kvacid evam duḥkhī a ādi śabdāḥ ca svātantrya apekṣayā uditāḥ na eva doṣāḥ harau tad gabuddhayā uktāḥ doṣa kāriṇaḥ tasmāt te doṣa śabdāḥ ca tatra eva guṇa vācakāḥ jāta motam harau yasmāt jyotiḥ ṣaḥ prāṇa rūpataḥ āyajñetas ca ayajetaḥ vasantiḥ ca vasantataḥ 
AVy_1,4.13–1,4.15	 vigata= chādana tvāt tu gaccha bhūta kṣayaṅkaraḥ bhuṅkṣā iti uktaḥ hariḥ hum ca hutam asmin jagat yatas sphuṭa tvāt phaṭ iti proktaḥ kava rakṣaṇaḥ iti atas kavacam vata ṛte yasmāt ṣaḍguṇa tvena sarvadā vaṣaṭ tad gatvataḥ teṣām vauṣaṭ itya iva kathyate svīyam svīkurute yasmāt svāhā iti uktaḥ janārdanaḥ namanti asmin guṇāḥ yasyāt namaḥ iti eva kathyate 
AVy_1,4.16–1,4.19	 iti aśeṣa kriyā nāma śabdaiḥ ekaḥ janārdanaḥ ucyate mukhyatas yasmāt pada varṇa svara ādibhiḥ tasmāt ananta guṇa tā śruti tāt paryataḥ asya hi vijñāna artha tvataḥ sarva śabdānām na asti dūṣaṇam aṅgīkṛte api na eva asti doṣaḥ vākya samanvaye tad artha tvena karma ādeḥ sambhavāt alpabuddhaye kaḥ chandasām yogam iti śruteḥ yoga artha tattva vid brahmā ekaḥ na eva ca anyaḥ asti kaḥ iti asya ra ubhaya arthataḥ 
AVy_1,4.20–1,4.22	 tasya api pūrva siddhasya jñānam eva iti niścayāt nitya yogaḥ api śabdānām arthaiḥ na eva niṣiddhayate strī śabdāḥ ca niṣedha arthāḥ sarve api brahma vācakāḥ virodhi sarva bāhulya kāraṇa strī niṣedhinām pṛthak samanvaya arthāni sthānāni etāni sarvaśas sarva mānaiḥ virodhaḥ ca vyutpatteḥ api aśakyatā paraspara virodhaḥ ca virodhaḥ kārya tadvatoḥ strī liṅga tvam niṣedhaḥ ca pūrva pakṣeṣu hetavaḥ 
AVy_1,4.23–1,4.26	 doṣāti aspṛṣṭi niyamaḥ śabda artha aneka tā tathā bahu rūpa tvam īśasya vyaktaya vyakti viśeṣitā utpādanam sva dehāt ca durjana avyakta tā tathā itayā ādyāḥ yuktayaḥ sākṣāt siddhānta sthāpakāḥ iha anvayaḥ sarva śabdānām aśakyaḥ jñātum añjasā iti yat loka vaimukhyam jaiminī ādi matam vadan vidyā adhināthaḥ bhagavān apācakre svayam prabhuḥ sva śiṣyāṇām prasiddhayartham matam ātmīyam aṃśataḥ 
AVy_1,4.27–1,4.30	 vijñātam taiḥ jagāda atra tāratamyam nṛṇām vadan teṣu teṣu padārtheṣu rūḍhiḥ aṅgīkṛtā yatas prayojana bahu tvena tasya tasya avirodhataḥ upadeśa ādi sāmarthyāt viṣṇau śaktiḥ ca gṛhyate tathā api etat virodhe tu tat vāci tvam apodyate avirodhe tu bahu arthāḥ etad mūla tayā matāḥ itas hi rūḍha tā anyeṣām upajīvya tvam atra hi tad siddhiḥ tad apekṣā ca sa apekṣā ca hari icchayā 
AVy_1,4.31–1,4.34	 tasmāt parama mukhya tvam viṣṇau= anyatra mukhya tā upalakṣaṇā ca gauṇī ca tisraḥ śabdasya vṛttayaḥ pravṛtti hetoḥ bāhulyam jñeyam parama mukhya tā tatra prayoga bāhulyam yadi tat para tā kimu ubhayam dṛśyate viṣṇau śabdānām api sarvaśas prayoga mātra bāhulyam rūḍhiḥ iti abhidhīyate prayoga yukta sādṛśyam sambandhaḥ vā api amukhyataḥ vṛtti hetuḥ iti jñeyaḥ pūrva ayoge para grahaḥ 
AVy_1,4.35–1,4.38	 etam eva tathā santam śataṛcī iti ādi nāmabhiḥ ācakṣate iti hi atra santam iti avadhāraṇāḥ yogasya rūḍheḥ prābalyam vidvat rūḍhim ca tatragām bahuśas darśayati añjastāt paryāt sa niruktikam aḥ iti brahma kathitam tadvaya ākhyānāt matā tathā śabdānām api sarveṣām nāma vid kṛta kṛtya tā viṣṇu nāma artha rūpa tvam saṃhitā ādeḥ athā bravīt ṇakāram ca ṣakāram ca bala ceṣṭā ātmakam vadan 
AVy_1,4.39–1,4.42	 tat jñāna pūrvaka tvena saṃhitā adhyayanam tathā upasarga tvataḥ vestu tāt śīlya arthādunaḥ tathā ṇakāraḥ ca ṣakāraḥ ca nāma rūpa tayā matau tasmāt samanvayaḥ viṣṇau svara varṇa pada ātmanaḥ api vedasya kim uta vākya rūpeṇa saṅgatiḥ ghoṣāḥ sarve api vedāḥ ca sarve vedāḥ ca yat padam indram mitram yam indram ca prathamaḥ saṅkṛtiḥ tathā nāmadhāḥ sarva devānām ekaḥ iti ādikā śrutiḥ 
AVy_1,4.43–1,4.46	 pramāṇa mukta viṣaye tat eva uktam upakramāt iti svayam bhagavatā bruvata aśeṣam anvayam na śabdavācya tā eva atra pradhanasya niṣiddhayate sarva veda itihāseṣu purāṇeṣu ca saṅgrahāt sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ prakṛti sambhavāḥ nibadhnanti mahā bāho dehe dehinam avyayam ityādi vākya rūpeṇa yatra arthaḥ na anyaḥ iṣyate tejaḥ abanna ātmakam vā api yadi upādānam iṣyate 
AVy_1,4.47–1,4.49	 anādi eva aparādhaḥ kaḥ pradhānam iti codite ajām ekām iti prāha śrutiḥ etām yadā tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ sarvathā eva asti pariṇāmi jaḍam yadi asmākam parama mukhya arthaḥ bhagavān ekaḥ eva tu mukhya mātra tayā rūḍham sarvam abhyupagamyate sarveṣām api śabdānām gauṇya ādyam tad ayogataḥ artha dvayam abhipretya pravṛtte hariḥ uktavān 
AVy_1,4.50–1,4.52	 kāryāṇām kāraṇam pūrvam vacasām vācyam uttamam yogānām paramām siddhim paramam te padam viduḥ iti buddhau samārohāt ubhayoḥ yoga rūḍhayoḥ tyāge ca kāraṇa abhāvāt ubhaya artha tvam iṣyate viparīta pramābhāve pūrva ārohaḥ tu kāraṇam sā bhavet yatra sa vyarthaḥ pūrva ārohaḥ bhramaḥ yathā atas jagat upādānam pradhānam vakti sā śrutiḥ 
AVy_1,4.53–1,4.56	 yat tat triguṇam avyaktam nityam sat asat ātmakam pradhānam prakṛtim prāhuḥ aviśeṣam viśeṣa vat pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ brahma caturbhiḥ daśabhiḥ tathā etat caturviṃśatikam gaṇam prādhānikam viduḥ iti bhāgavate prāha vidyādhīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ na ca prakṛti śabdena brahma upādānam ucyate avikāraḥ sadā śuddhaḥ nityaḥ ātmā sadā hariḥ sadā eka rūpa vijñāna balaḥ ānanda rūpakaḥ 
AVy_1,4.57–1,4.60	 nirvikāraḥ akṣaraḥ śuddhaḥ nirātaṅkaḥ ajaraḥ amaraḥ aviśvaḥ viśvakartājaḥ yaḥ paraḥ saḥ abhidhīyate nirvikāram anaupamyam sadā ekara samakṣayam brahma iti paramātmā iti yam viduḥ vaidikāḥ janāḥ iti śruti purāṇa uktayā na vikārī janārdanaḥ para adhīna viśeṣa āptiḥ anivartyā ani athā bhavaḥ kṣīra ādi vat vikāraḥ syāt na eva sa syāt hareḥ kvacid apādāna tvam eva asya yadi upādānatā iṣyate 
AVy_1,4.61–1,4.64	 aṅgīkṛtam tat pitṛ vat na tu viśva ātmanā bhavaḥ na ca ūrṇa nābhi janitṛ mātṛṇām ca vikāritā cetana tvāt tat annam hi kārya rūpa tayā bhavet apādāna tayā viśvakartṛ tvam buddhi pūrvakam uktam bhālla viśākhāyām brahmatarke ca sa ādaram icchā mātrāt prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiḥ avikārasya sarvadā svabhāvaḥ ayam anantasya rajaḥ yena abhavat jagat sva dehāt icchayā viśvam bhukta pūrvam janārdanaḥ 
AVy_1,4.65–1,4.68	 sasarja mātā pitṛ vat ūrṇa nābhi vat eva vā pradhānam pariṇāmyeśaḥ nirvikāraḥ svayam sadā na cetana vikāraḥ syāt yatra kvāpi hi acetanam na acetana vikāraḥ api cetanaḥ syāt kadācana na ca anyasya anya rūpa tvam vikṛta tve api dṛśyate na kṣīrāt anya tā dadhnaḥ kenacid dṛśyate kvacid sarvajñāt brahmaṇaḥ anya tvam jagataḥ hi anubhūyate abhedaḥ sattva mātreṇa syāt kharva svaṇayoḥ api 
AVy_1,4.69–1,4.72	 bhāgena pariṇāmaḥ ced bhāgayoḥ bhedaḥ eva hi yaḥ bhāgaḥ na vikārī syāt saḥ eva asmākam īśvaraḥ bhinnānām samudāyasya nāma brahma iti ced bhavet brahma upāda āna tā na syāt tadā viśvasya hi kvacid śṛṅgāt śaraḥ avilomabhyaḥ dūrvā gomayataḥ tathā vṛścikaḥ ca iti evamādyeṣu apādāna tvam iṣyate upādāna eka deśa tvam yadi api atra pradṛśyate api apādānatā eva atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhavet 
AVy_1,4.73–1,4.76	 na hi upādānatā eva atra bāhya avayava gauravāt na ca acetanataḥ tatra cetanasya samudbhavaḥ upādāna tayā kintarhi apādānam hi acetanam kārya deha gatasya asya cetanasya pradṛśyate sat ca tyat ca abhavat iti na asya viśva tvam ucyate tat sṛṣṭvā iti girā eva asya pūrvam viśvasya siddhitaḥ sattvāt tateḥ vaidika tvāt samyak vaktum aśakyatas āśraya tvāt sva āśraya tvāt jñāna tvāt durvidatvataḥ 
AVy_1,4.77–1,4.79	 sat tateḥ yātanāt ca eva hi aprāpta tvāt ca durjanaiḥ nitya asādhu guṇa vyāpti yantṛ rūpa tvataḥ sadā jagat gatena rūpeṇa brahmā eva hi tathā ucyate vyaktiḥ ukta guṇānām hi puruṣa apekṣayā nṛṇām bhavet abhavat ityādyaḥ prayogaḥ ca atra yujyate tasmāt aśeṣa kartā ekaḥ nirvikāraḥ ramāpatiḥ śabdaiḥ prakṛtiḥ ityādyaiḥ strī liṅgaiḥ abhidhīyate 
AVy_1,4.80–1,4.83	 bahu syām iti tasya eva hi ukta mārgeṇa yujyate tad tad gatena rūpeṇa tad artham hi asṛjat jagat yat ca avikṛtam eva etat brahma viśvātmanā mṛṣā dṛśyate manda dṛṣṭayā eva sa sargaḥ iti kathyate sā manda dṛṣṭiḥ tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ kim tatas anya gāḥ brahmaṇaḥ ced kva sārvajñyam anya gā ced svatas anya tā na adeha yoginaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ iti tat kāraṇam svatas dehinaḥ kāraṇa yutāḥ dehāḥ ca yadi na bhramāt 
AVy_1,4.84–1,4.87	 kim bhrānti kalpitam tatra bhedaḥ api bhrama jaḥ yadi bhrānteḥ ajñāna mūla tvāt tasya bheda vyapekṣayā na ajñāna kalpakam kiñcid anyonya āśraya tā yatas bhrama tve tu iyamuktiḥ ca tad antar patanāt na hi vyāvahārika tā ca asya syāt abādhya tvaḥ eva hi bādhyam na artha kriyā kāri na ca svapnaḥ api naḥ mṛṣā vāsanā janita tvena tasya api aṅgīkṛta tvataḥ sa hi kartā iti vākyāt ca jāgrat tvam iti hi bhramaḥ 
AVy_1,4.88–1,4.91	 sarpa bhrama ādau= api hi jñānam asti eva tādṛśam tat eva artha kriyā kāri tat sa deva artha kārakam brahma tu artha kriyā kāri paratas svatas eva vā aṅgīkṛtam hi tena eva paratas tve na ca pramā amukhya satyamānasya sādhaka tve sadā avayoḥ na hi sampratipattiḥ syāt atas tiṣṭhatu sā pramā na hi vipratipannena śakyam sādhayitum kvacid sādhaka tvam tu satyasya sākṣiṇaḥ hi āvayoḥ dvayoḥ samyak sampratipannam tat na vivatarma matam bhavet 
AVy_1,4.92–1,4.95	 yadi na aṅgīkṛtam kiñcid anaṅgīkṛta tā api hi na aṅgīkṛtā iti mūkaḥ syāt iti na asmad vivāditā viśvam satyam yat ciketa praghān vasya yathārthataḥ iti ādi śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ viśvasatya tva vācakāḥ satya tvam gagana ādeḥ ca sākṣi pratyakṣa sādhitam sākṣi siddhasya na kvāpi bādhya tvam tat adoṣataḥ sa varkāleṣu abādhya tvam sākṣiṇā eva pratīyate kālaḥ hi sākṣi pratyakṣaḥ suṣuptau ca pratītitaḥ 
AVy_1,4.96–1,4.99	 atīta anāgatau kālau= api nāsā akṣi gocarau pakṣīkartum aśakyatvāt na anumā tatra vartate tat etat iti sarvam ca dṛśyam vā smṛti gocaram sākṣi siddhena kālena khacitam hi eva vartate tasmāt na tam vinā kiñcid smartum draṣṭum atha api vā śakyam tat nitya siddheḥ hi na anumā avasaraḥ bhavet atas adoṣa pratītasya satya tvam sākṣiṇā matam parīkṣā ādeḥ ca satya tvam tena hi eva matam bhavet 
AVy_1,4.100–1,4.103	 anyathā śruti yuktayā ādi pramāṇaiḥ ca saha eva tu akasmāt vinivṛttiḥ ca kim viśvasya na śaṅkayate itas pūrvam tathā abhāvāt yadi no saṃsṛteḥ gatiḥ vākyānumāditaḥ ced syāt tad prāmāṇyam ca sākṣitaḥ tad prāmāṇyam yathā sākṣī sthāpayati evam eva hi sarva kāleṣu api sthairyāt vyabhicāram apohya ca evam akṣajamāna tva siddhām viśvasya satyatām kim iti sthāpayet na ayam nirdoṣa jñāna śaktitaḥ 
AVy_1,4.104–1,4.107	 eka jñāna kṛtam viśvam iti yat ca uṣyate mṛṣā bahu jñāna kṛtam viśvam iti tasya uttaram bhavet parasya satya tām jānan= api yaḥ sva ātma taskaraḥ paraḥ na asti iti vadati kim iti unmatta vat vadet para abhāve hi vāc vyarthāḥ yadi na eva ucyate tadā kaśā vetra ādikam tasya taskarasya uttaram vadet prapañcaḥ yadi vidyeta nivarteta na saṃśayaḥ māyā mātram idam dvaitam advaitam paramārthataḥ 
AVy_1,4.108–1,4.111	 vikalpaḥ vinivarteta kalpitaḥ yadi kenacid upadeśāt ayam vādaḥ ajñāte dvaitam na vidyate iti atra yadi śabdau ca nivarteta iti ca dvayam viśvasya satya tām āhuḥ vidyeta utpattim eva ca vidā utpattau= iti hi asmāt dhātoḥ utpattiḥ eva hi nivṛtti vyāpti yuj prāyas prapañcaḥ bheda pañcakaḥ jīveśvara bhidā ca eva jaḍeśvara bhidā tathā jīva bhedaḥ mithas ca eva jaḍa jīva bhidā tathā mithas ca jaḍa bhedaḥ yaḥ prapañcaḥ bheda pañcakaḥ 
AVy_1,4.112–1,4.115	 saḥ ayam satyaḥ hi anādiḥ ca sādiḥ ced nāśam āpnuyāt dvaitam na vidyate iti tasmāt ajñāninām matam iti śruteḥ mitam trātam māyā ākhya hari vidyayā uttamaḥ arthaḥ hariḥ tu ekaḥ tat anyat madhyama adhyamam vācā ārabdham tu sāṅketyam nāma syāt vikṛtam bahu nityam tu nāmadheyam yat mṛttikā ityādi vaidikam prādhānyāt tad parijñānāt prākṛta ajñaḥ api pūruṣaḥ vidvān iti ucyate sadbhiḥ evam nitya para ātma vid 
AVy_1,4.116–1,4.119	 sadātanam satyam iti nityam eva ucyate budhaiḥ prayogaḥ ca uttaratra asti jarā yadi enam āpnuyāt dehaḥ pradhvaṃsate vā ayam kim tatas asya atiśiṣyate hanyate na vadhena ayam jarayā ca na jīryati etat satyam brahma puram iti nitya tvaḥ eva hi vācā ārambhaṇam iti ukte mithyā iti aśruta kalpanam punaruktiḥ nāmadheyam iti iti asya nirarthatā ekaḥ piṇḍaḥ maṇiḥ ca iti pada vaiyathya rmā iva ca 
AVy_1,4.120–1,4.123	 vikāra tva vivakṣāyām naca eka nakha kṛntanam sarva kārṣṇāyasam ca syāt atas sādṛśyaḥ eva ca vivakṣā atra tu nitya tve prādhānye ca ukta vartmanā prādhānya pratipatti artham sṛṣṭayā ādeḥ ca eva vistaraḥ tasmāt kena api mārgeṇa na vivarta matam bhavet tad asaṅkha yāta doṣetam heyam eva śubha arthibhiḥ asaṅkhayatvena doṣāṇām grantha ādhikya bhayāt api uparamyate tatas viṣṇuḥ icchā pūrva kam aśramaḥ karoti pitṛ vat viśvam pūrṇa śeṣa guṇa ātmakaḥ 
AVy_2,1.1–2,1.3	 iti śrīmat ānanda tīrtha bhagavat pāda ācārya viracite śrīmat brahmasūtra anuvyākhyāne prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uktaḥ samanvayaḥ sākṣāt avirodhaḥ atra sādhyate caturvidhasya tasya ādau yauktaḥ tatra api ca smṛteḥ tasyāḥ catur svarūpa tvāt pratyekam catur ātmakāḥ pādāḥ sarve tad aṃśāḥ ca mūrtīnām varṇam ā agamāt āpta tā samatā dṛṣṭi śruti sāmya balāt bhavāḥ sarva anusāraḥ laghu tā viśeṣa adarśana aphale 
AVy_2,1.4–2,1.7	 iṣṭa siddhiḥ ca niyamaḥ pūrva pakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ etāḥ eva tu atibalā siddhāntasya niyāmakāḥ āptaiḥ pratyakṣatas dṛṣṭvā proktam artham katham śratiḥ pipīlikā lipi nibhāḥ vārayeta sarvagāḥ hi te iti ced yadi aśeṣa jñāḥ rudra ādyāḥ hari pūrvakāḥ kim na aśeṣa vidaḥ mānam hi ubhayatra samam bhavet na ca āpti niścayaḥ tatra śakyate vyabhicārataḥ naca asyāḥ vyabhicāre api hīyate mānatā kvacid 
AVy_2,1.8–2,1.11	 veda uktasya adhikārasya durnirūpa tvataḥ sadā niyamaḥ vyabhicāraḥ vā na eva jñātum hi śakyate adhikāraḥ hi sulabhaḥ kathitaḥ anya āgameṣu alam veda uktaḥ hi adhikāraḥ tu durlabhaḥ sarva mānuṣaiḥ anya āgameṣu vipra tvam api caṇḍāla janmanām maṇḍala antar praveśena kramaśas pratipādyate adhikāram durāpādya m ukta vāti sulabham punar aśakyam sādhanam ca uktavā suśakam tad phala āptaye ucyate atas tat uktam hi vyabhicāri phale api tu 
AVy_2,1.12–2,1.15	 katham pramāṇa tām gacchet nitya tvāt puruṣa udbhavaiḥ ujkhitam sarva doṣaiḥ ca katham naḥ māna tām vrajet virūpa nityayā vācā nityayā anityayā sadā ityādi śrutibhiḥ vedaḥ nityaḥ iti avagamyate pipīlikā lipiḥ ca api pramāṇam avirodhataḥ yathā drauṇeḥ ulūkena kṛtam api āsa bodhakam aviruddham viruddham tu virodhāt eva bādhitam virodha adarśanāt tasmāt veda prāmāṇyam iṣyate 
AVy_2,1.16–2,1.19	 tad mūla tvāt smṛtīnām ca virodhaḥ yatra na kvacid virodhaḥ api saḥ eva uktaḥ pratyakṣeṇa āgamena vā āgamena āgamasya eva virodhe yuktiḥ iṣyate upajīvya virodhe tu vedasya anya artha kalpanā pratyakṣam upajīvyam syāt prāyas yuktiḥ api kvacid āgama eka pramāṇeṣu tasya eva hi upajīvyatā yuktaḥ ayuktaḥ ca yadi arthaḥ āgamasya pratīyate syāt tatra yuktaḥ eva arthaḥ yuktiḥ ca trividhā matā 
AVy_2,1.20–2,1.23	 vyāptiḥ pratyakṣatā yasyāḥ yukti gā agama gā tathā pratyakṣa āgama mūlā tu yuktiḥ tatra balīyasī yāthārthyam eva māna tvam tat mukhyam jñāna śabdayoḥ artha tva marya tā eva syāt na kriyā artheṣu sā matā jñāna arthe jñeyatā mukhyā śabda arthe tad anantaram yathā artha jñāna janakāḥ yathārthāḥ yuktayaḥ smṛtāḥ anupramāṇam etāni hi akṣa yukti vacāṃsi atas prāmāṇyam na anuvādasya smṛteḥ api vihīyate 
AVy_2,1.24–2,1.27	 yāthārthyam eva prāmāṇya śabda arthaḥ yat vivakṣitaḥ aṅgīkṛtam ced prāmāṇyam smṛti ādeḥ kā virodhatā nacā phala tvam vaktavyam sarva smṛti anuvādayoḥ phalavat tvam naca asmābhiḥ prāmāṇyam hi vivakṣitam tṛṇa ādi darśane kim ca phalavat tvam nigadyate sukha duḥkha ādikam kiñcid smṛtau= api hi dṛśyate na pariccheda kāryā iva pramāṇam iti ca pramā nirdoṣa akṣa udbhavam hi atra pratyakṣam iti gīyate 
AVy_2,1.28–2,1.31	 prākṛtam śuddha caitanyam akṣam tu dvividham matam śuddham īśaramāmukteṣu anyatra prākṛtaiḥ yutam nirdoṣam eva caitanyam anyatra ubhayam iṣyate sukha duḥkha ādi viṣayam śuddham saṃsāra geṣu api nirdoṣa tva ati niyamāt tat baliṣṭhatamam matam pañca indriya manaḥ bhedāt prākṛtam ṣaḍvidham smṛtam anumā yuktiḥ eva uktā vyāptiḥ eva tu sā smṛtā pratijñāta artha siddhayartham vyāptiḥ eva yadā uditā 
AVy_2,1.32–2,1.35	 avaśiṣṭam kim atra asti liṅgam tatra vijānataḥ yadi liṅgam asiddham syāt kutas eva asya mānatā yadi smāraka mātram syāt smartuḥ na atra prayojanam na pañca avayā uktau ca vivādau= asitiḥ bhavet dṛṣṭānta ādiṣu ca evam syāt sādhanam punar eva hi liṅga uktau= api ca evam syāt anumāva sitiḥ dhruvā virodhaḥ asaṅgatiḥ ca eva sākṣāt yukteḥ tu dūṣaṇam pratijñāyām asambandhaḥ yukteḥ uktā hi asaṅgatiḥ 
AVy_2,1.36–2,1.39	 virodhaḥ api tridhā eva syāt pratijñā artha viruddha tā liṅga rāhityam avyāptiḥ nyūna ādhikye tu vācike sādhya vyāpaka vailomyam avyāptiḥ sādhanasya ca durbalena virodhe api na pramāṇam asādhakam sva vākyena virodhe api na eva sādhaka tām vrajet saṃvāda anukti saṃyuktāḥ ete eva ca nigrahāḥ vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍa iti kathāḥ tisraḥ vijānatām sva artham para artham api vā tattva nirṇaya sādhanī 
AVy_2,1.40–2,1.43	 kevalam tu kathā vādaḥ jalpaḥ artha ādi vyapekṣayā satām eva kathā jñeyā vitaṇḍā tu asatām satām aprakāśya sva siddhāntam asatām pakṣa dūṣaṇam ukte taiḥ prathamam māne vaktavyam tasya dūṣaṇam vidyā parīkṣā pūrvā eva vitaṇḍā jalpaḥ eva ca ucca nīca tva nirṇītiḥ yatas jaya parājayau vinā eva tattva nirṇītim na hi jalpa ādinā kvacid ucca nīca tva vijñānam iti vidyā parīkṣaṇam 
AVy_2,1.44–2,1.47	 vādena ca ucca nīca tva vijñānam bhavati sphuṭam iti vādasya pūrva tvam tad siddhau vyarthatā anyayoḥ bahu vidya tva siddhau tu na eva vādaḥ api kāraṇam sa bhāsa bhāpa prāśnīka pūrvaḥ tu spardhinām api vādaḥ eva ubhaya arthaḥ syāt nirṇīti jaya kārakaḥ tattva aprakāśaḥ eva ekaḥ vitaṇḍā jalpayoḥ phalam vinā vādena vidyāyāḥ yadi śakyam parīkṣaṇam syāt jalpa ādiḥ api kvāpi vādaḥ eva anyathā bhavet 
AVy_2,1.48–2,1.51	 jalpaḥ iti api nāma syāt vādasya etādṛśasya tu pratijñā mātra sādhya tvam api syāt yājñavalkya vat sabhā sabhā patiḥ ca eva prāśnikāḥ ca eva vaiṣṇavāḥ rāga dveṣa vihīnāḥ ca syuḥ sabhyāḥ sarva vedinaḥ prāśnikāḥ ca etat ajñāne sabhyāḥ ca eṣām ca dūra gāḥ pramāṇam nirṇayāya syuḥ pakṣapāta vivarjitāḥ ubhābhyām sādhanam ca eva dūṣaṇam vāda jalpayoḥ sadbhiḥ āgamaḥ eva ekaḥ prayojyaḥ abhīṣya sādhakaḥ 
AVy_2,1.52–2,1.54	 sva siddhānta anusāreṇa hi asadbhiḥ anumā ucyate pratyakṣa āgama vairūpyam āśritya anyārtha tā eva tu āgame daśarnīyā atra doṣaḥ liṅga viloma tā liṅga ānukūlyam sva arthasya śruti ādīnām anugrahaḥ tri pañca avayavām eva yugma avayavinīm api niyamāt yaḥ anumām brūyāt tam brūyāt yadi tādṛśī na anumā iti tadā kena sādhya avayava kalpanā 
AVy_2,1.57–2,1.59	 niyata avayava asiddhau vyāpti mātreṇa sādhanam kartavyam eva tena syāt tasmāt sā eva anumā matā anubhūtiḥ pramāṇam ced kena smṛtiḥ apa udyate pūrva anubhūte kim mānam iti ukte syāt kim uttaram mānasam tat hi vijñānam tat ca sākṣi pramāṇakam atīta anāgatam yadvat yogibhiḥ dṛśyate añjasā evam pūrva anubhūtam ca manasā eva avagamyate 
AVy_2,1.60–2,1.63	 vijñātam manasā pūrvam mayā etat kṛtam iti api sākṣāt anubhavāt siddham katham eva hi apodyate evam lakṣaṇake māna traye brahma ādi vastuṣu pramāṇam vedaḥ eva ekaḥ tad prāmāṇyam ca sādhitam tathā api mṛd jala ādīnām buddhi vāc ādi vācakaḥ dṛṣṭa vyāpti viruddha tvāt tatra mānam katham bhavet tatas tad nāmakaḥ kaścid pumān anyaḥ bhavet iti yuktayā āgama avirodhena prāptam atra abhidhīyate 
AVy_2,1.64–2,1.67	 bāla rūḍhim vinā eva api vidvat rūḍhi samāśrayāt tat tad nāmānaḥ eva ete tat tat vastu abhimāninaḥ santi teṣām viśeṣeṇa śaktiḥ anyebhyaḥ ucyate vyāptiḥ ca ukta anusāreṇa dṛśyante ca ādhikāribhiḥ śāstra ukta vastunaḥ ca eva vyutpattiḥ śāstra liṅgataḥ vyutpattiḥ sā balavatī mūrkha vyutpattitāḥ hi yat dṛḍha yukti virodhe tu sarvatra nyāya īdṛśaḥ alpa vākya yutā yuktiḥ bahulā eva virodhinī 
AVy_2,1.68–2,1.71	 yatra tatra katham vastu nirṇayaḥ syāt i ti īrite virodhi yukti bāhulyāt iti nyāyaḥ viniścitaḥ yukteḥ tu yukti bāhulyam āgamāt āgamasya ca katham na nirṇayam kuryāt iti asat kāraṇam na hi śruti arthaḥ bhavati kvāpi śruti prāya upapattibhiḥ avirodhaḥ caturthe tu pāte samyak samarthyate asat kāryam yathā dṛṣṭam vastu tvāt kāraṇam tathā iti ced na niṣedha eka svarūpasya na kartṛ tā 
AVy_2,1.72–2,1.74	 buddhi pūrva pravṛttiḥ hi kartṛ tvam iha niścitam pratiṣedha ātmaka tvam tu bhāvasya abhāva dharmataḥ dharma dharma aikyataḥ ca eva na tu tanmātra tā bhavet abhāvasya ca bhāvaḥ api dharmaḥ atha api hi dharmiṇaḥ tādṛktavam mātratā iha uktā buddhirāhityam eva tat viśeṣya tā eva dharmi tvam prathama pratipattiṣu niṣedha vidhi rūpa tvam bhāva abhāva tvam atra hi 
AVy_2,1.75–2,1.78	 sarva nāśeṣu api sadā śiṣṭa tvāt yasya kasya nuḥ nāśaḥ ayam vimataḥ api syāt nāśa tvāt kartṛ śeṣavān naca aśeṣa nṛnāśaḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ dṛśyaḥ asti vā kvacid dharma adharma āśraya tvena svīkāryaḥ api naraḥ laye anādi tvam vinā adṛṣṭam katham syāt kāraṇam kvacid pūrva adṛṣṭāt parādṛṣṭam yadi na eva uttaram kutas adṛṣṭam kāraṇam no ced laye mānam ca kim bhavet utpatti nāśa kārī hi buddhimān dṛśyate kvacid 
AVy_2,1.79–2,1.81	 tad dṛṣṭāntena sarvatra kartā kim na anumīyate āgama anugṛhītā tu mānam eṣa anumāpitu āgama anugraha abhāve na tarkaḥ syāt pratiṣṭhitaḥ akṣaja āgama mūlasya syāt eva asya pratiṣṭhitiḥ anyathā asya apratiṣṭhā ca sva vācā vyāhatā eva hi na ca śiṣyā gṛhīta tvam nirīśāt īśa vādinaḥ atas avaśiṣṭa jīva ādi kartṛ tā atra niṣiddhayate 
AVy_2,1.82–2,1.85	 tad manaḥ akuruta iti ādeḥ asataḥ manasaḥ janiḥ nivāritā tu pūrvatra hi akasmāt iti tat vinā asataḥ viśva jananam āśaṅkayā atra niṣiddhayate prāpakam vākya mātram tu parihāraḥ viśeṣitaḥ kvacid jīva akṛtam dṛṣṭvā cetanāt eva ca akṛtam tadvat eva anumāni atra vastu tvāt kriyate śruteḥ na anyat anya tvam āpannam kvacid dṛṣṭam kathañcana atas jīvasya na brahma bhāvaḥ syāt hi kadācana 
AVy_2,1.86–2,1.89	 kvacid bhinna tayā dṛṣṭam tad abhinnatayā katham dṛśyet naḥ dṛṣṭa pūrvam hi tādṛśam na ca dṛśyate bhoktṛ tvā āpattitaḥ iti yat matam tat kutas hariḥ bhoktrā āpatteḥ iti prāha katham ca tad ananyatā jagataḥ tu avikāra tvaḥ ukta nyāyena sādhite svatantra kāraṇa anya tvam tena hi atra niṣiddhayate dravyam karma ca kālaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ yad prasādāt ime santi na santi yat upekṣayā iti śruteḥ tad vaśasya bhāvaḥ na paraḥ iti atas 
AVy_2,1.90–2,1.93	 śaktaḥ api hi anyathākartum sva icchā niyamataḥ hariḥ kāraṇaiḥ niyataiḥ eva karoti idam jagat sadā nitya bhedaḥ nimittena hi upādānena tu dvayam asat yat kārya rūpeṇa kāraṇa ātma tayā asti hi anavasthā anyathā hi syāt sarvatra utpatti nāśayoḥ śaktaḥ api bhagavān viṣṇuḥ akartum kartum anyathā sva bhinnam kāraṇa abhinna bhinnam viśvam karoti ajaḥ iti śruteḥ avasitaḥ ukta arthaḥ ayam aśeṣatas 
AVy_2,1.94–2,1.97	 anaṃśasya api jīvasya kiñcid sāmarthya yojanām kāryeṣu yaḥ kara uti addhā namaḥ tasmai svayambhuve yadi bhāgena kāryeṣu jīva śaktim na yojayet hariḥ tadā hi sarvatra kṛtsnayatnoṃ aśitā api vā aṃśinaḥ hi paṭa ādyāḥ ye bhinnaiḥ eva parasparam aṃśaiḥ aṃśinaḥ ucyante na evam eva hi cetanāḥ atas anaṃśinaḥ iti eva śrutiḥ eteṣu vartate api aneka svarūpeṣu viśeṣāt eva kevalam 
AVy_2,1.98–2,1.101	 bahu svarūpa tā ākhyā tu teṣu asti eva hi sa aṃśatā bahu tvena āvinābhāvāt bhinna tā niyamāt bhavet yadi na evam niyama kṛt bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ tasya tu aśeṣa śakti tvāt yujyate sa varmā iva ca virodhaḥ sarva vaiśiṣṭaye yaḥ dvitīye nirasyate nārāyaṇasya tu adhyāye tad anye tatra tatra gāḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vākyānām jīva rūpa abhidhāyinām api anyonya avirodhaḥ tu dvitīya adhyāya gocaraḥ 
AVy_2,1.102–2,1.105	 māna meya viśeṣeṇa punar uktiḥ na jāyate sadā pravṛttiḥ īśasya svabhāvāt eva kevalam aṅga ceṣyāḥ yathā puṃsaḥ kāścid uddeśa varjitāḥ devasya eṣa svabhāvaḥ ayam iti āha śrutirañjasā krīḍām prayojanam kṛtvā sṛṣṭiḥ śruti virodhinī iti kevala līlā eva nirṇītā prabhuṇā svayam ātma prayojana arthāya spṛhām śrutiḥ avārayat na prayojanavat tvena iti atas āha jagadguruḥ 
AVy_2,1.106–2,1.108	 icchā mātram prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiḥ iti sṛṣṭau viniścitāḥ iti praśaṃsayā kāmaśrutibhyaḥ ca eva yuktitaḥ mahātātparya yukteḥ ca na icchā mātram niṣiddhayate mokṣa arthāḥ śrutayaḥ yasmāt sa ca tasya prasādataḥ unninīṣati vākyāt ca loka dṛṣṭa anusārataḥ icchāṃnimittakaḥ yasmāt tad abhāve kutas śrutiḥ mahātātparya rahitā pramāṇa tvam gamiṣyati 
AVy_2,1.109–2,1.112	 yāthārthyam eva māna tvam api vākyam prayojakam māna tvam eti tatra api yat sampūrṇa prayojanam vaiṣamyam ca eva nairghṛṇyam veda aprāmāṇya kāraṇam na aṅgīkāryam atas anyat tu na vaiṣamya ādi nāmakam yad adhīnāḥ guṇāḥ ca eva doṣāḥ api hi sarvaśas guṇāḥ tasya katham na syuḥ syuḥ deṣāḥ ca katham punar sarva dharma āpapatteḥ tat vākyaiḥ api hi tādṛśaiḥ nirdoṣa aśeṣa guṇakaḥ nirṇītaḥ bhagavān hariḥ 
AVy_2,2.1–2,2.4	 smṛti yukti śruti guṇa yuktayaḥ bahu yuktayaḥ evam caturvidhāḥ na eva viruddhayante anvayam prati iti prathama pādena nirṇīte api abhiyogataḥ darśanānām pravṛtta tvāt mandaḥ āśaṅkate punar anādi kālataḥ vṛttāḥ samayā hi pravāhataḥ naca ucchedaḥ asti kasya api samayasya iti atas vibhuḥ bhrānti mūla tvam eteṣām pṛthak darśayati sphuṭam tarkaiḥ dṛḍhatamaiḥ eva vākyaiḥ ca āgama vādinām 
AVy_2,2.5–2,2.7	 daurlabhyāt śuddha buddhīnām bāhulyāt alpa vedinām tāmasa tvāt ca lokasya mithyājñāna prasaktitaḥ vidveṣāt parame tattve tattva vediṣu ca aniśam anādi vāsanā yogāt asurāṇām bahu tvataḥ durāgraha gṛhīta tvāt vartante samayāḥ sadā tathā api śuddha buddhīnām īśa anugraha yoginām yuyuktayaḥ tamaḥ hanyuḥ āgama anugatāḥ sadā 
AVy_2,2.8–2,2.10	 iti vidyā patiḥ samyak samayānām nirākṛtim cakāra nija bhaktānām buddhi śāṇa tva siddhaye cetana acetanam tattva dvayam eva nirīśvarāḥ āhuḥ tat pañca pañcatva vibhāga stham acetanam cetanam tat asaṅkha yātam bhinnam anyat layam bhavet acetanasya kartṛ tvam svātantryeṇa nigadyate paraspara vibhedaḥ ca kāryāṇām ālayam bhavet 
AVy_2,2.11–2,2.14	 bhoktṛṇām cetanasya āhuḥ kecid tām api na apare sva rūpa caitanya balāt sva prakāśāt ca bhogitām prakṛteḥ ca svarūpasya viveka agraham eva tu abhoga vādinaḥ bhogam āhuḥ bheda grahāt tayoḥ bhoginām muktiḥ uddiṣṭā saḥ eva ābhoga vādinām īśasya asaṅgrahāt eva na yuktau tau= ubhau= api cetana icchā anusāreṇa yadā dṛṣṭaḥ paṭa udbhavaḥ etādṛśa tvam anyasya vastu tvāt kena vāryate 
AVy_2,2.15–2,2.18	 na ca kācid pramokta arthe śrutiḥ eva pramā hi naḥ āpta tvam ukta mārgeṇa vaktuḥ na eva upapadyate aprāmāṇi asvataḥ tu asya svīkārāt api māyi vat sva ukta akhila niṣedhī syāt na ca kiñcid prasiddhayati idam na acetana vaśam vastu tvāt pratipanna vat iti eva pratiṣiddhasya kena mūla anumā bhavet svatantra vṛttiḥ racanā sā ca eva acetane kutas acetana tvam svātantryam iti ca ātma pramāhatam 
AVy_2,2.19–2,2.22	 sva icchā anusāritām eva svātantryam hi vidaḥ viduḥ kutas icchā acetanasya seccham ced kim acetanam icchāmi aham iti hi eva nija anubhava rodhataḥ acetanecśāpa gatā yadi bheda āgrahaḥ atra ca katham na sa ghaṭasya syāt manaḥ me iti bhedataḥ manasaḥ api gṛhīta tvāt ubhaya ātmaka tā yatas kāmasya tu manaḥ kāmaḥ priya apriya vibhedataḥ dvaividhyam dṛśyate ca asya tasmāt bheda āgrahaḥ kutas 
AVy_2,2.23–2,2.26	 racanā anupapatteḥ tat na sarvajñānum āgatam acetanam jagatkartṛ payaḥ ambu ādi ca na upamā etad praśāsti vacanāt cetanā acetanasya ca dvaividhye api tu kāma ādeḥ kutas svāmi tvam ātmanaḥ sākṣāt anubhava ārūḍham śakyate apoditum kvacid icchā svāmi tvam eva uktam icchāvat tvam na ca aparam kiñcid tad vaśa ga tve api svāmi tvam loka vat bhavet sarva ātma tantra kāma ādeḥ kim uta eva pareśituḥ 
AVy_2,2.27–2,2.30	 na ca anubhava gam kāma svāmi tvam veda vāc api śakta apavaditum tasmāt sā tad anya abhidhāyinī mokṣa kāmaḥ bhavet anyaḥ yadi muktāt bhaviṣyataḥ mokṣa kāmasya kim tena sva nāśa artham ca kaḥ yatet kartṛ tvam yasya tasya eva bhoktṛ tvam upalabhyate vibhāge ca tayoḥ mānam na eva kiñcid kvacid bhavet sarva māna virodha eka durdīkṣā dīkṣitaḥ tu ayam māyā vādi upamām yāyāt tat caśabdāt nirākṛtaḥ 
AVy_2,2.31–2,2.34	 sāṅkhayaḥ tu sa īśvaraḥ brūte kṣetra anugraha śaktimān asti īśvaraḥ svayambhātaḥ kleśa karma ādi varjitaḥ kṣetra śaktimatī sā eva prakṛtiḥ bīja śaktimān jīvaḥ parjanya vat daiva śaktimān īśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ pṛthivī vat pradhānam tad jīvaḥ sannidhi mātrataḥ bīja avapana kartā iva iti atra prāha prabhuḥ svayam anyatra kā api śaktiḥ na svātantryeṇa īśaḥ eva hi śaktīḥ tāḥ prerayati añjaḥ tad adhīnāḥ ca sarvadā 
AVy_2,2.35–2,2.38	 sattā pradhāna puruṣa śaktīnām ca pratītayaḥ pravṛttayaḥ ca tāḥ sarvāḥ nityam nitya ātmanā yatas yathā nitya tayā nityam nitya śaktayā svayā īśvaraḥ niyāmayati nityam ca na ṛte tvad iti śruteḥ svabhāva jīva karmāṇi dravyam kālaḥ śrutiḥ kriyāḥ yad prasādāt ime santi na santi yat upekṣayā iti śruteḥ na sattā ādyāḥ api nārāyaṇam vinā tad patañjali vindhya ādi matam na puruṣa artha dam 
AVy_2,2.39–2,2.42	 cārvākaiḥ ucyate mānam akṣa jam na aparam kvacid dehaḥ ātmā pum arthaḥ ca kāma arthābhyām vinā na hi yat evam darśanena asya kaḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣa gocaraḥ labdhaḥ tena eva hi naraiḥ śāstrāt kim mohanam vinā sva para artha vihīna tvāt sva matena eva niṣphalam kim iti unmatta vat śāstram vṛthā pralapati svayam dehāt anyaḥ anubhavataḥ ātmā bhāti śarīriṇām mama dehaḥ iti vyaktam mama arthaḥ iti vat sadā 
AVy_2,2.43–2,2.46	 pratyakṣasya eva māna tvam iti kena avasīyate yadi tad sādhakam veda prāmāṇye na katham bhavet na ca anyāmāna tā kvāpi pramāṇena avasīyate sva matena artha rahitaḥ upekṣyaḥ pakṣaḥ īdṛśaḥ sannidhānāt cetanasya vartate yadi acetanam tathā api abuddhi pūrva tvāt ukta doṣaḥ samaḥ bhavet aṅgi tvam puruṣasya eva sarvaiḥ api anubhūyate tad aṅga tva uktitaḥ ca eva syāt sarvasya apalāpakaḥ kimu sarva īśvarasya asya hi apalāṣāt yatas akhilam 
AVy_2,2.47–2,2.49	 aṅgi tvam yadi tasya eva svātantryam ced naca akhilam tad preraṇe api aśakta tvāt svatantraḥ anyaḥ hi apekṣitaḥ na ca svātantryam asya eva pratyakṣa ādi virodhataḥ hita ākṛtya ādi doṣāt ca bhadram na anīśvaram matam saṃsāriṇaḥ anyam sarva īśam sarva śaktim anaupamam cetana acetanasya asya sattva ādeḥ tad adhīna tām na aṅgīkurvanti ye teṣām sarveṣām ca samāḥ ime 
AVy_2,2.50–2,2.52	 tasmāt śruti pramāṇena yuktibhiḥ ca paraḥ hariḥ aṅgīkāyartamaḥ nityaḥ sarvaiḥ api su niścitam nitya jñāna prayatna iccham saṅkhayat yaiḥ api pañcabhiḥ yuktam īśam vadanti anye tad icchā dṛṣṭa coditāḥ paramāṇavaḥ caturvargāḥ saṃyujyante dviśas akhilāḥ paramāṇu dvayena eva dvayaṇukam nāma jāyate dvayaṇukatrayeṇa tṛyaṇukam taiḥ caturbhiḥ tad ātmakam 
AVy_2,2.53–2,2.56	 tatas tu aniyamena eva khaṇḍa avayavinām bhavaḥ tatas ca aniyamena eva sarva avayavi sambhavaḥ kāraṇam samavāyi ākhyam paramāṇu ādi tatra hi īśa icchā dṛṣṭa kālāḥ tu nimittam kāraṇam matam sāmānya antya viśeṣau ca samavāyaḥ ca tat trayam nityam kriyāḥ anityāḥ tu guṇa dravye dvirūpake kārye guṇa kriyāṇām tu samavāyi anya kāraṇam kāraṇa sthāḥ guṇa ādyāḥ tu saṃyogaḥ dravya kāraṇam 
AVy_2,2.57–2,2.60	 evam sthite api siddhānte viśeṣaḥ tatra kalpitaḥ dvayaṇuke paramāṇau ca hrasva tvam parimaṇḍalam na kāraṇam kārya guṇe vairūpyam tatra kāraṇam iti āhuḥ tān atha uvāca vidyādhīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ mahat tvam ca eva dīrgha tvam tṛyaṇuka ādyeṣu kalpitam tasmāt ca sadṛśam kāryam tad kāryeṣu upajāyate yathā tathā eva hrasva tvāt pārimāṇḍalī ataḥ api hi jāyeta sadṛśam kārye parimāṇam samatvataḥ 
AVy_2,2.61–2,2.63	 na ced mahat tvataḥ ca eva dīghaṛtvāt api naḥ bhavet sadṛśasya hi kāryasya na eva yogaḥ kathañcana apratyakṣa tvam evam syāt yatas kāryeṣu aṇutvataḥ iti ced na mahat tvam ca paramāṇauvaṇau= api katham tṛyaṇuka pūrveṣu na aṇu tvam api kathyate pratyakṣa tva tad anya tve puruṣa apekṣayā akhile aṇu tvam ca mahat tvam ca yatas vastu vyapekṣayā 
AVy_2,2.64–2,2.67	 tāratamya sthitāḥ yasmāt padārthāḥ sarve eva ca yathā mahat tva viśrāntiḥ tathā aṇu tvasya ca iṣyate parimāṇa tvataḥ ced na mahattvasya api viśramaḥ dṛśyate anantaḥ iti eva tathā ananti amaṇau= api na mahat tatva guṇataḥ etāvān iti hi īśvaraḥ paricchinnaḥ tathā aṇoḥ ca na etāvat bhāga tā kvacid viśrāntaḥ yadi ananta aṃśaḥ kaścid asti iti gamyate na avasāyayitum śakyaḥ virodhāt eva kevalam 
AVy_2,2.68–2,2.71	 kevalam sākṣi mānena kālaḥ deśaḥ api na antavān aparyavasitiḥ ca aṇoḥ dṛśyate sakṣiṇā dvayoḥ yadi no sākṣi gamyam tat mahat tvam kena gamyate viśrāntiḥ tāratamyena dṛśyate hi anumānataḥ yadi āgamāt anantam tat mahat tvam avagamyate anantam eva ca aṇu tvam kutas na eva avasīyate mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ na eva viśrāntiḥ upalabhyate anyat eva hi ananta tvam mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ samam 
AVy_2,2.72–2,2.75	 bahutva alpa tvayoḥ yadvat sāṅkhayāyām upalabhyate ānantyam eka bhāgānām tāvat tvam hi eva gaṇyate aṇīyān= ca mahīyān= ca bhagavān āgama uditaḥ ānantya vācakaḥ śabdaḥ dvidhā ānantye api mānatām yāti na eva guṇa alpa tvam kālāt patvam ca mānagam sarva kāla gatasya alpa kāle api syāt avasthitiḥ mahā guṇasya ca alpaḥ api guṇaḥ syāt iti ced bhavet tāvat tvam eva na eva syāt deśe api etat na naḥ matam 
AVy_2,2.76–2,2.79	 mahataḥ alpa tvam api hi vyoma vat prāha veda vid yadi alpa deśa saṃsthānam na sarvatra api naḥ bhavet sthitasya hi alpa deśeṣu sarvaga tvam bhavet dhruvam ekatra api anavasthasya kutas eva akhila stha tā śūnya tvam eva tasya syāt yasya ekatra api na sthitiḥ atas na aṇu tva viśrāntiḥ na mahattvasya ca kvacid ubhaya ānantya yuj tasmāt yadi mukhya mahat bhavet tat ca brahma param sākṣāt sarva ānantya yutam sadā 
AVy_2,2.80–2,2.83	 yadi sākṣī svayambhātaḥ na mānam kena gamyate akṣa ja ādeḥ ca māna tvam anavasthā athavā bhavet atas sarva padārthānām bhāgāḥ santi eva sarvadā sarva dikṣu api sambandhāt avibhāgaḥ parāṇu tā tad saṃyogāt aniyatāt padārthānām janiḥ bhavet dvayoḥ eva tu saṃyogaḥ iti kena avasīyate kāraṇasya guṇāḥ tena bhaveyuḥ kārya gāḥ api tāratamyena sarve api mahāntaḥ ca aṇavaḥ yatas 
AVy_2,2.84–2,2.87	 na ca tad prokta sṛṣṭau tu mānam kevala kalpanā katham sākṣi mitasya asya śaknuyāt vāraṇe kvacid yadi sākṣi mitam na etat na anumā tatra vartate pakṣīkartum aśakyatvāt kutas eva anumā bhavet yatra na asti padanyāsaḥ kaḥ tam viṣayam āpnuyāt deśa antara ādi śabdaḥ ca śaśaśṛṅga ādi śabda vat sadṛśam ca sajātīyam na asmad pakṣe kim eva hi yena eva ca prakāreṇa atya siddham anumīyate tena eva śaśṛṅga ādeḥ śakyam astitva kalpanam 
AVy_2,2.88–2,2.90	 pratyakṣam āgamaḥ vā api bhavet yatra niyāmakaḥ sā eva vyāptiḥ bhavet mānam na anyā sandigdha mūlataḥ saha darśana mātreṇa na vyāptiḥ avasīyate yadā eva avyatirekasya hi akṣa jam vā āgamaḥ bhavet tad nirdhārita yuktiḥ vā vyāptiḥ sā eva aparāḥ na hi anyathā saptama rasa bhavaḥ api anumayā apatet aniṣṭāni ca sarvāṇi hi anumā kāma cāriṇī 
AVy_2,2.91–2,2.94	 kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca eva guṇa ādeḥ pañcakasya ca bhinnasya eva tu sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ anyaḥ īryate bhinna tva sāmyataḥ tasya tābhyām yogaḥ bhavet dhruvam sa sva nirvāhakaḥ ced syāt dravyam eva tathā na kim viśeṣaḥ tad gata tva ādiḥ yadya bhinne avasīyate guṇa kriyā ādi rūpasya niṣedhaḥ kena hetunā dravyam eva tatas ananta viśeṣa ātma tayā sadā nānā vyavahṛteḥ hetuḥ ananta tvam viśeṣataḥ 
AVy_2,2.95–2,2.98	 viśeṣaḥ ca viśeṣī saḥ svena eva samavāya vat kalpanā guru tā doṣāt padārtha antara tā na hi kalpayitvā ṣaṭ padārthān sābhāvān api kevalam ekasmin sa viśeṣaḥ ced kim pūrvam tasya vismṛtiḥ yena pratyakṣa siddhena vyavahāraḥ akhilaḥ bhavet bhāva abhāva vibhāgena yam vinā na kathañcana abhedena pratītiḥ ca kārya kāraṇa pūrvake abhāva ante padārthe asmin sa viśeṣa avasīyate 
AVy_2,2.99–2,2.102	 sāmānya ādi padārtheṣu tad niṣṭha tva ādayaḥ akhilāḥ katham dharmāḥ nivāryante vastu aikye api hi vādibhiḥ kāryasya tad tad niṣṭha tvam guṇa ādeḥ vyāpita ādikaḥ katham viśeṣaḥ na eva asti sa ca dharmaḥ aparaḥ yadi ṣaṣ padārtha atirekaḥ syāt padārtha aniyame api hi dharmasya dharma santānāt anavasthā karaḥ bhavet sāmānyasya api sāmānyam guṇasya api guṇaḥ hi atas na aṅgīkṛtaḥ sa ca yadi na anavasthā kvacid bhavet 
AVy_2,2.103–2,2.106	 asmad pakṣe guṇa ādyāḥ ca tat vantaḥ hi viśeṣataḥ ananya tvāt na anavasthā bhedaḥ nāśe bhavet tathā viśeṣam eva saṃśritya viśeṣaḥ balavān yatas dṛṣṭi pramāṇataḥ ca eva virodhaḥ darśane katham virodhaḥ hi avirodhaḥ ca yatas darśanam ānagau tatas dṛṣṭe virodhaḥ tu sadbhiḥ āpādyate katham abhinnaḥ bhagavān svena tad anyena vibhedavān nityāḥ dharmāḥ tadīyāḥ tu sarve asmān na eva bhedinaḥ 
AVy_2,2.107–2,2.110	 sāmastya ucchedinaḥ anyatra dharmāḥ ubhaya rūpakāḥ bhāve te eva ca ucchedāt tad anye ca samastaśas aṃśāṃśinā uḥ abhedena tu aṃśa saṃyogaḥ eva hi aṃśinaḥ na anavasthātaḥ yadi api aṃśeṣu aviśramaḥ ekasmin jātaḥ eva anyaḥ saṃyogaḥ jāyate yadi anavasthā tadā eva syāt saṃyoga aikye bhavet kva sā aṃśe saṃyoga dṛṣṭeḥ ca dṛṣṭe kā sānavasthitiḥ yadi aṃśa gaḥ na saṃyogaḥ kāryeṣu prathimā katham 
AVy_2,2.111–2,2.113	 paramāṇoḥ aṇoḥ na asti mahattā iti adbhutam vacaḥ aṇūnām prathimā apekṣām vinā eva tṛyaṇuke api saḥ paramāṇoḥ mahat tvam ca vinā iti etat vacaḥ katham aṃśinaḥ aṃśaiḥ abhedaḥ ayam aṃśena tu bhidā abhidā sarva pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ katham eva hi apohyate saṃyogaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ ca bhedaḥ ca eva pṛthak pṛthak anyonya pratiyogena hi ubhayoḥ api dṛśyate 
AVy_2,2.114–2,2.117	 bhinnāḥ iti tu bhedānām samudāyaḥ hi dṛśyate yathā eva ca padārthānām anayoḥ bhedaḥ iti api itas amuṣya amutas api asya bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ dvi dharmikaḥ tatra eka vacanam yat tat viprāṇām bhojanam yathā nara tva ādikam api evam tat tad dharmatayeyate na sarva dharmaḥ ekaḥ asti samudāyaḥ tu bhinna gaḥ etādṛśam ca sādṛśyam padārtheṣu pṛthak pṛthak ekasmin sa vinaṣṭe api yatas anyatra eva dṛśyate 
AVy_2,2.118–2,2.121	 kutas bhasma tvam āptasya nara tvam punar iṣyate eka tve na asti mānam ca śrutiḥ api āha sa ādaram bhinnāḥ ca bhinna dharmāḥ ca padārthāḥ akhilāḥ api svaiḥ svaiḥ dharmaiḥ abhinnāḥ ca svarūpaiḥ api sarvaśas anivṛtta vināśāḥ tu dharmāḥ ubhaya rūpakāḥ na kenacid abhinnaḥ atas bhagavān sva guṇaiḥ vinā iti vyutpattiḥ api hi sādṛśyena eva gamyate sarveṣu yugapad śabdaḥ sadṛśeṣu pravartate 
AVy_2,2.122–2,2.125	 tathā api prāptitaḥ tu eka vacanāt ca viśeṣataḥ abhīṣya avagatiḥ ca syāt śaktiḥ sādṛśya gāḥ yatas tādṛśaḥ ayam ca tad śabdaḥ iti jñāpayati sphuṭam jātitaḥ ced katham tāsu tatra ced anavasthitiḥ tathā eva vyakti vijñānam vyakti tva abhāva dūṣitam yadi tat ca asti tasya api viśeṣeṣu anavasthitiḥ katham svarūpa tvam api jñāyate anugatam yadi eka vyutpatti paryantam anavasthā ādi dūṣitam kalpanā gauravāt tena yuktā na anuga kalpanā 
AVy_2,2.126–2,2.129	 aupādhika viśiṣṭa ādyam api tat vastu kim tatas anyat tat eva ced agnimat tvam kim tatra bhaṇyate agni saṃyoga mātram ced bhavet tat siddha sādhanam bhūdharasya agni saṃyogaḥ yadi ṣaṣṭhayarthaḥ eva kaḥ samavāyaḥ yadi hi asya ca eka tvāt siddha sādhanam yadi asi a aupādhikaḥ bhedaḥ kutas eka tvam iṣyate na anirvācyam hi tena iṣyam atas aupādhika anyayoḥ satya tvāt kaḥ viśeṣaḥ syāt māyāvādi anyathā bhavet 
AVy_2,2.130–2,2.132	 upādhi janyam tat gamyam iti vaupādhikam bhavet ubhayatra api anantāḥ syuḥ samavāyāḥ itas tatas bhinna tvam ca eva teṣu asti kaḥ viśeṣaḥ upādhi ge avidyamānaḥ eva anyaḥ samavāyaḥ adhigamyate upādhinā tad gamakam anumānam na mā bhavet evam eva asataḥ satta samavāyaḥ janirmatā tatra api hi ukta doṣāṇām na eva kiñcid nivārakam 
AVy_2,2.133–2,2.135	 asmad pakṣe viśeṣasya sarvatra aṅgīkṛta tvataḥ na asti doṣaḥ kvacid bhāvaḥ hi abhāvaḥ ca saḥ eva hi abhāvasya ca dharmāḥ syuḥ bhāvāḥ teṣām ca te akhilāḥ pratyakṣamānataḥ sarvam etat naḥ vāraṇa kṣamam sarve bhāvāḥ abhāvāḥ ca padārthāḥ tena sarvadā tathā api prathamam buddheḥ yaḥ niṣedhasya gocaraḥ saḥ abhāvaḥ vidhi buddheḥ tu gocaraḥ prathamam paraḥ 
AVy_2,2.136–2,2.139	 tasmāt pradhvasta bheda ādi sat iti eva avagamyate asti abhāvaḥ asti ca dhvaṃsaḥ deha abhāvaḥ ca bhasma tā ityādi yujyate sarvam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇataḥ anyonya abhāva bhedau ca pṛthaktavam ca pṛthak pṛthak yat kalpayanti tat ca eva kalpanā gauravāt gatam paryāya tvena te śabdāḥ jñāyante sarve eva hi bhedasya tu svarūpa tve ye vadanti ca śūnyatām adbhuta tāḥ te yatas anyasya pratiyogi tvam iṣyate 
AVy_2,2.140–2,2.143	 pratiyoginaḥ hi bhedaḥ ayam na tu svasmāt kathañcana vibhāgena alpa tā eva syāt kutas eva ca śūnyatā na śūnyānām hi saṃyogāt bhāvaḥ vastunaḥ iṣyate vidāraṇa arthaḥ dhātuḥ ca vibhāga guṇa vācakaḥ avidāraṇe api hi āsyasya bhinnau= oṣṭhau tu tasya ca atas unmatta vākya tvāt māyā vādaḥ abhyupekṣitaḥ na ca amandasat ānanda syandī ananta guṇa arṇavaḥ īśvaraḥ aṣṭaguṇa tvena prameyaḥ apramita tvataḥ 
AVy_2,2.144–2,2.147	 mayi ananta guṇe anante guṇataḥ ananta vigrahe ananta guṇa māhātmya śakti jñāna mahā arṇavaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ aśeṣa cetanebhyaḥ param padam ityādi veda tad vākyaiḥ anantaiḥ ca avasīyate ananta guṇa tā viṣṇoḥ katham eva hi apodyate yadi ananta viśeṣāḥ ca tad jñāna ādeḥ nivāritāḥ katham tad tad viṣaya tā sārvajñya artham vidhīyate aupādhika viśeṣaḥ tu pūrvam eva nirākṛtaḥ 
AVy_2,2.148–2,2.151	 sva prakāśa tvam api tu yaiḥ jñānasya nivāritam katham sarvajña tā tasya sva jñāna adhigamam vinā jñānam viśva adhigam tu ekam tat jñāna viṣayam param iti jñāna dvayena eva sarva vid parameśvaraḥ iti ced eṣaḥ eva arthaḥ tad jñāna avasitaḥ yadi sva prakāśa tvam eva syāt jñānam hi etat viśeṣaṇam jñāna antareṇa ced atra bhavet eva anavasthitiḥ sva prakāśa tvam etasmāt durnivāryam samāpatet 
AVy_2,2.152–2,2.155	 sukhavān duḥkhavān= ca syāt iti vyāptiḥ ca naḥ bhavet nirduḥkha tvam mahānandaḥ śrutyā eva īśasya bhaṇyate yaḥ aśanāyā pipāse ca śoka ādīn= ca ativartate ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān vipāpmā iti ādikā ca sā īśvarasya tathā iṣṭa tvam duḥkhitvā upādhiḥ iti api ukte kim uttaram brūyāt śruti anādara tatparaḥ naca ātma duḥkhita icchā syāt atas etat nivāryate saha darśana mātreṇa śrutī nām apalāpakaḥ 
AVy_2,2.156–2,2.158	 yajña ādeḥ api pāpasya hetu tvam hiṃsayā yuteḥ na anumāti katham tatra yadi upādhiḥ niṣiddha tā aduḥkhi tvena ca anuktiḥ katham na upādhitām vrajet aduḥkham itarat sarvam jīvāḥ eva tu duḥkhinaḥ teṣām duḥkha prahāṇāya śrutiḥ eṣā pravartate iti śrutiḥ hi paramā śruti uktiḥ yadi kāraṇam kim kāryam anumānena gaa stana samena hi 
AVy_2,2.159–2,2.161	 anumānena yadi arthaḥ śruti dṛṣṭaḥ vyapodyate pūrva uktena prakāreṇa na īśvaraḥ dharmaḥ eva ca syāt tad phalam ca tena atra śrutiḥ eva pramā bhavet īśasya anumayā siddheḥ śrutiḥ dhamiḥ pramā bhavet tayā sarva guṇaiḥ pūrṇaḥ uktaḥ īśaḥ yatas tatas anānanda anumā tasya dharmi grāhi virodhataḥ na pramāṇam bhavet tasmāt na anumātra upayoginī 
AVy_2,2.162–2,2.165	 nitya icchatvāt para īśasya paramāṇu sadātvataḥ adṛṣṭa kālayoḥ ca eva bhāvāt kāryam sadā bhavet na hi kāla vibhedaḥ asti tat pakṣe asmad mate hareḥ viśeṣa kāle eva etat sṛṣṭayā ādi icchā sadātanā viśeṣāḥ ca eva kālasya hareḥ icchā vaśāḥ sadā sarve nimeṣāḥ iti hi śrutiḥ eva āha sa ādaram udīrayati kāla ākhya śaktim iti asya vāc api kālasya kāla ga tvena na virodhaḥ api kaścana 
AVy_2,2.166–2,2.169	 asaṅkha yāta viśeṣa tvāt icchāyāḥ api sarvadā īśaḥ deśaḥ ca kālaḥ ca sva gatāḥ eva sarvadā īśa adhīnau ca tau nityam tad ādhārau ca tad gatau iti śrutiḥ api prāha kāle sva uddiṣṭaḥ eva tu tad kāla sṛṣṭim eva atas vāñchati īśaḥ sadā eva hi syāt kālaḥ sa tadā eva iti kālasya sva gata tvataḥ svabhāvāt eva hi icchā eṣā devasya eva iti śruteḥ svabhāvaḥ api pareśa icchā vaśaḥ iti uditaḥ purā 
AVy_2,2.170–2,2.173	 nityāḥ anityāḥ ca tatas tad adhīnāḥ iti śrutiḥ rūpa sparśa ādi hetubhyaḥ paramāṇoḥ anitya tā anumeyā śrutīnām ca viruddha tvāt na tat matam upādeyam atas ca ayam aviruddhaḥ samanvayaḥ vaibhāṣikāḥ ca sautra antāḥ svara sakṣaṇikam jagat aṇūnām samudāyam ca kāla karma nimittataḥ utpatti kāle yuktānām ātmānam ca kṣaṇa sthitim nityam santānam eteṣām pañca skandha ātmanā sthitam 
AVy_2,2.174–2,2.177	 saṃskāra rūpa vijñāna sañjñā duḥkha ātmanā sthitiḥ duḥkha abhāvam sukham ca āhuḥ arūpa jñāna santatim mokṣam sa samudāyaḥ hi na ekasmāt eva yujyate na ubhayoḥ ca ubhaya tvam yat samudāya vyapekṣayā atas anyonya āśraya tvena samudāyaḥ na yujyate anyonya apekṣayā puṃsaḥ samudāya tva vedanam syāt tad sadātana tve api tat ca sāmīpya hetukam iti ced kārya sambhūti mātra vyāpṛti kāraṇam 
AVy_2,2.178–2,2.180	 na tu kārya viśeṣeṣu vyāpṛtam kāraṇam bhavet atas artha indriya saṃyogi rūpa kāraṇa tā ātmanaḥ saṃyogi rūpa rāhityāt na eva tad jñāna tā api hi viśaṣaṣa kārya janakam yadi kāraṇam iṣyate kutas samāna rūpa tvam kāryāṇām api sarvaśas atas aniyatyā yat kiñcid yasya kasya api kāraṇam adṛṣṭasya api tasya eva viśeṣa āpādakam kutas 
AVy_2,2.181–2,2.184	 yasya kasya api yat kiñcit viśeṣam upapādayet kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva yat kiñcid yasya kasyacid bhavet niyāmaka abhā= a ādi damasya eva kāraṇam iti nitya vināśi tve kena mānena gamyate idam na jāyate amuṣmāt iti atra api na kāraṇam vināśa utpattayaḥ ca eva na dṛśyante sadātanāḥ dṛśyate pratyabhijñātaḥ sthira tvam sarva vastuṣu phala ādīnām viśeṣeṇa sarvatra api anumīyate 
AVy_2,2.185–2,2.188	 sattvena kṣaṇika tvam ced ākāśasya aviśeṣatas aviśeṣaḥ akhilasya api sattvāt kim na anumīyate yadi ākāśasya sattvam na kutas eva nara ādiṣu sa dharmi pratiyogi tvam ākāśasya avagamyate tau vinā na hi abhāvaḥ ca kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ kadācana adharmi pratiyogi tvam ākāśasya avagamyate svīkāra tyāgataḥ adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭayoḥ sarva vastuṣu guṇān unmattaḥ eva asau vidadhāti adhikam punar 
AVy_2,2.189–2,2.191	 uttara utpatti mātreṇa vināśāt pūvarvaḥ tunaḥ na saṃskāra arpaka tvam ca yujyate kasyacid kvacid atas jñātam mayā ityādi na jñeyam anumā kutas eka tvam anubhūti stham tyaktavā nirmānakāḥ bhidā kutas ātma ādikeṣu syāt balyā iva anubhavaḥ yatas kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca eka kālīna tvam vinā katham pūrva saṃskāra yogī syāt uttaraḥ niyamena ca 
AVy_2,2.192–2,2.195	 sambaddhaḥ eva saṃskāram anyatra ādattate akhilāḥ asambaddhaḥ katham pūrvaḥ uttare vāsanākaraḥ eka kāla tayā yogam vinā saṃskārataḥ katham kṣaṇa mātram avasthānam svīkṛtam sarva vastuṣu pūrva madhya apara kalā ra hitaḥ kṣaṇaḥ iṣyate pūrva bhāva bhavam kāryam uta tad nāśa sambhavam yaugapadyam sati bhavet utpādyānām aśeṣatas vināśe ced na tat kāryam kārya utpattau ca kā pramā 
AVy_2,2.196–2,2.199	 abhedena viśeṣeṇa deha dīpa phala ādiṣu viśeṣa darśanam yuktam asmākam anubhūtitaḥ viśeṣa darśanam mānam yadi na sthairya dṛś kutas diś sukhe ca kha dṛṣṭāntāt bhāvau sat ced kvacid bhavet viśvam pratyakṣa gam tyaktavā tayoḥ yaḥ anumitam vadet māyā vādi vat eva asau= upekṣyaḥ bhūtim icchatā sarva pramāṇa siddham yat buddheḥ bhedena sarvadā katham nu tasya buddhi tvam viśvam anyat ca kimpramam 
AVy_2,2.200–2,2.203	 sarva lokaḥ bibheti añjaḥ yasmāt anubhavāt sadā tasya apalāpinaḥ kim na niṣpramāṇaka vādinaḥ saḥ aham tat idam eva aham sukhī sat gaganam diśaḥ satyāḥ ityādi anubhavāḥ sadā tad pratipakṣa gāḥ atas nirmānam akhila pramāṇa pratipakṣa gam durmatam kaḥ nu gṛhṇīyāt vināsuḥ atatim kvacid aparaḥ śūnyam akhilam manaḥ vācām a gocaram nirviśeṣam svayambhātam nirlepam ajara amaram 
AVy_2,2.204–2,2.206	 aśeṣa doṣa rahitam anantam deśa kālataḥ vastutas ca tat asmi iti nitya upāsā para ukṣitam rāga ādi doṣa rahitam tad bhāvam yoginam nayet tasya eva anādi saṃvṛttyā nānābheda ātmakam jagat sat iva ābhāti satya tvam sāṃvṛtam tasya ca iṣyate pāramārthika sattvam tu śūnyāt anyasya na kvacid sāṃvṛtena eva satyena vyavahāraḥ akhilaḥ bhavet 
AVy_2,2.207–2,2.209	 śūnyāt saṃvṛti yogena viśvam etat pravartate sṛṣṭi kāle punar ca ante stimitam śūnyatām vrajet iti brūte tam uddiśya jagāda jagatām guruḥ na asataḥ jagataḥ bhāvaḥ na hi dṛṣṭā asataḥ janiḥ sataḥ kvacid pramāṇam ca dṛṣṭiḥ eva akhilāt varam yadi evam saptama rasān madhurāt iva pīnatā bhavet janasya mārjārṛṅgam goḥ iva ghātakam 
AVy_2,2.210–2,2.213	 kārya arthī kāraṇam sat ca na upādadyāt kathañcana na pravarteta ceṣyāya śūnyādeva iṣya sambhavāt deśa kāla ādi niyamaḥ niṃha śūnyāt sataḥ bhavet puruṣa icchā anusāreṇa yadi kiñcid prajāyate kim na anumīyate tadvat vastu tvāt puruṣāt bhavaḥ sarvasya api naca abhāvaḥ viśvam sat iti gamyate yatas anubhava rodhe tu vacanam vādinaḥ kutas svapna bhrānti vat eva idam saṃvṛttyā eva upalabhyate 
AVy_2,2.214–2,2.216	 yadi sattvena kiñca atra bhramaḥ na eva nivartate anādeḥ asya viśvasya nivṛttiḥ yadi ca iṣyate nivṛttiḥ ca nivarteta tasyāḥ bhrānti tva sambhavāt dṛṣṭasya bhrāntitā ced syāt adṛṣṭe na bhramaḥ kutas gavāma śṛṅgi bhāvena na hi syāt śaśaśṛṅgitā asmākam tu pramāṇena prasādāt īśvarasya ca ukta bhaṅgayā agamānām ca prāmāṇyāt yujyate akhilam 
AVy_2,2.217–2,2.219	 dṛśya tvāt vimaṃta mithyā svapna vat ced iyam ca mā mithyā ced sādhya siddhiḥ na vyabhicāraḥ na ced bhavet sādhaka tvam asatyasya sādhyam vipratipattitaḥ tasya ca iti anavasthā syāt sattvam ca asya anubhūtitaḥ anubhūti virodhena mithyātve mā na kācana atīta anāgatau kālau= api naḥ sākṣi gocarau tad sambandhi tayā sattvam api dṛṣṭasya sākṣi gam
