AVy_2,2.220–2,2.222	 dṛḍha dṛṣṭam tu yat dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭa ābhāsaḥ tatas aparam bhrānteḥ saṃvṛti satyasya viśeṣaḥ avyabhicāravān tena api aṅgīkṛtaḥ samyak sa naḥ satya tvam eva hi vijñānāt vyabhicāraḥ asya kadācid syāt iti pramā na eva dṛṣṭā pramā sā ca na bhavet sva virodhataḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣya dharmyādi grahaṇa apekṣayā yadi anyonya āśraya tā hetoḥ durgāhyaḥ iti yat na tat 
AVy_2,2.223–2,2.226	 svarūpam vastunaḥ bhedaḥ yat na tasya grahe grahaḥ anyathā asya amunā bhedaḥ iti vaktum na yujyate agṛhītaḥ yadā bhedaḥ tadā svasmāt iti grahaḥ syāt pratīti virodhāt ca na hi kaścid tathā vadet dharmi tva pratiyogi tva tad bhedāḥ yugapad yadi viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca tad bhāvaḥ ca eva gṛhyate kaḥ virodhaḥ sva rūpeṇa gṛhītaḥ bhedaḥ eva tu asya amuṣmāt iti punar viśeṣeṇa eva gṛhyate 
AVy_2,2.227–2,2.230	 kiñca bhedaḥ katham grāhyaḥ iti yaḥ paripṛcchati dharmya ādi bheda grahaṇāt tena uktaḥ anyonya saṃśrayaḥ anyatva agrahaṇe proktaḥ katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ anya tvam yadi siddham syāt katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ etādṛśasya vaktārau= ubhau jāti uttara ākarau māyī mādhyamikaḥ ca eva tad upekṣyau bubhūṣubhiḥ yat śūnya vādinaḥ śūnyam tat eva brahma māyinaḥ na hi lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ asti nirviśeṣa tvataḥ tayoḥ 
AVy_2,2.231–2,2.233	 anṛta ādi virodhi tvam ubhayoḥ ca sva lakṣaṇam sva vākya abhāva saṃvādāt na kṛtyam prativādinaḥ tad pakṣaḥ iti vaidharmyāt na svapna ādi vat ityajaḥ aprayatnāt nirācakre ca iti dṛṣṭi viruddha tām niṣpramāṇa tvam api asya sūcayāmāsa viśvakṛt jñānam eva ekam akhila jñeya ākāram prabhāsate tatra santati bhedaḥ ca sva bhedaḥ bhedaḥ eva ca kalpitāḥ pratibhāsante nānā saṃvṛti bhūmiṣu 
AVy_2,2.234–2,2.236	 iti etat api naḥ yuktam na hi jñāna tayā jagat bhāsate anubhavasya eva viruddha tvāt apeśalam tat matam kṣaṇika tvāt ca jñānasya sthira rūpataḥ jñeyasya ukta prakāreṇa sarva śruti virodhataḥ anubhūti viruddha tvāt api pakṣāḥ ime aśivāḥ āha kṣapaṇakaḥ viśvam sat asat dvayamadvayam dvayāt vayam atat sarvam sapta bhaṅgi sadātanam 
AVy_2,2.237–2,2.239	 na etat padārthaḥ ekasmin yuktam dṛṣṭi virodhataḥ bhāva abhāva tayā viśvam yena rūpeṇa mīyate tad rūpam eva tat iti niyamaḥ kena vāryate tad tad doṣa nivṛtti artham svīkṛtā tad tad ātmanā yadi taiḥ akhilaiḥ deṣaiḥ lipyate cala darśanaḥ atihāya pramāṇa āptam niyamam sat asat tayā aśeṣam āviruddham ca nirmānam vyāhatam sadā 
AVy_2,2.240–2,2.243	 sarva prakāram vadataḥ dṛṣṭa hāniḥ amagrahaḥ sva vyāhata tvam iti ādyāḥ doṣāḥ sarve bhavanti hi vakti sva prabham ātmānam deha mānam tat api alam duṣyam nānā śarīreṣu praveśāt anyathā abhavāt anyathā bhāvi yat vastu tat anityam iti sthitiḥ tad mate tad anitya tvam pudgalasya anivāritam na anitya tā asmad pakṣe tu caitanya ādeḥ viśeṣiṇaḥ lakṣaṇasya nivṛttau tu syāt na tad cetane kvacid 
AVy_2,2.244–2,2.247	 ota prota ātmaka tvam tu paṭe dehe aṅga saṃsthitiḥ ityādi lakṣaṇasya eva nivṛttau syāt anitya tā bhautikam tu eva rūpa ādi vyāptam nāśena naḥ mate na evam tasya anyathā bhāvaḥ yasya anitya tvam īritam rūpa ādi yuktasya tathā jagat nāśi tva siddhaye vyāptyā tayā anyathā bhāvāt ātmanaḥ anitya tā bhavet nitya ūrdhva gatiḥ api eṣā yā muktiḥ iti kathyate aloka ākāśam āptasya katham na vikṛtiḥ ca sā 
AVy_2,2.248–2,2.250	 kīdṛśaḥ ca anyathābhāvaḥ nāśa hetutayā iṣyate saṃsthāna apagamaḥ ced sa na hi bhū sāgara ādiṣu yaḥ kaścid anyathā bhāvaḥ yadi muktiḥ ca tādṛśī deha māne vikāraḥ syāt iti sthāsnūnana ātmanaḥ āha hasti ādi deheṣu hi api syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ aṇu dehasya jīvasya gaja tve vikṛtiḥ hi yā deha vyāptyai viśeṣaḥ kaḥ tasyāḥ sthāsnu tanau ca nuḥ 
AVy_2,2.251–2,2.253	 gītāt puṣpa phala avāptiḥ sparśāt kārśyam rasāt sthitiḥ api vṛkṣasya dṛśyante iti nānā ātma tā bhavet evañca ātmākārtsnyam iti tatas eva āha veda vid sarvajña tva ādikaiḥ sarvaiḥ guṇaiḥ yuktam sadāśivam jagat vicitra racanā kartāram doṣa varjitam āhuḥ pāśupatāḥ tat ca bahu śruti virodhataḥ na upādeyam matam hi asya devasya stuhi garta gam 
AVy_2,2.254–2,2.257	 utpipeṣa śiraḥ tasya gṛṇīṣe sat patim padam yat viṣṇoḥ upamam hantum rudram ākṛṣṭate mayā dhanuryam kāmaye tam tam ugram mā śiśna devatāḥ ghnan śiśna devān ekaḥ asau= āsīt nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ tasmāt rudraḥ samprasādaḥ ca abhūtām vaiṣṇavam makham yajñena yajña maya janta abadhnan puruṣam paśum yaḥ bhūtānām adhipatiḥ rudraḥ tanti caraḥ vṛṣā ityādi śruti sāmarthyāt pāratantryam janiḥ mṛtiḥ 
AVy_2,2.258–2,2.260	 para adhīna para prāpti ḥ ajña tvam praaye abhavaḥ pratīyante sa doṣa tvāt na īśaḥ paśupatiḥ tatas aśarīra tvataḥ tasya sambandhaḥ jagatā kvacid kartṛ tvena na yujyeta dehinaḥ jñāna dṛṣṭitaḥ na ca deha ādi vat viśvam asya syāt bhoga sambhavāt adhiṣṭhāne sthitaḥ kartā kāryam kurvan pratīyate na asya adhiṣṭhāna yogaḥ asti bhūtānām praaye tadā 
AVy_2,2.261–2,2.264	 adehaḥ ced asārvajñaḥ śilā kāṣṭha ādi vat sadā dehī ced antavān eva yajñadatta nidarśanāt naca etat akhilam viṣṇau śruti prāmāṇya gauravāt manaḥ buddhayaṅgitām viṣṇoḥ lakṣayāmaḥ yaḥ eva saḥ saḥ eva dehaḥ vijñānam aiśvaryam śaktiḥ ūrjitāḥ dehaḥ viṣṇoḥ na te viṣṇo vāsudevaḥ agratas abhavat ekaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tu āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ ajasya nābhau= adhi ekam arpitam mātrayā paraḥ 
AVy_2,2.265–2,2.268	 sat dehaḥ sukha gandhaḥ ca jñāna bhās sat parākramaḥ jñāna jñānaḥ sukha sukhaḥ sa viṣṇuḥ parama akṣaraḥ ānandaḥ ekaḥ eva agre āsīt nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ priyam tasya śire moda pramodau ca bhujau hareḥ ānandaḥ madhyatas brahma puccham na anyat abhūt kvacid manasaḥ asya abhavat brahmā lalāṭāt api śaṅkaraḥ pakṣayoḥ garuḍaḥ śeṣaḥ mukhāt āsa sarasvatī sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapād 
AVy_2,2.269–2,2.272	 iti ādi śruti sandarbha balāt nitya guṇa ātmanaḥ viṣṇoḥ dehāt jagat sarvam āvirāsīt itīyate mānavat tvāt virodhaḥ kaḥ nāmānam kvacid iṣyate avirodhaḥ virodhaḥ ca mānena eva hi gamyate atas uktam samastam ca vāsudevasya yujyate śiva ādi nām a yuktāḥ ca śrutayaḥ viṣṇu vācakāḥ nāmāni sarvāṇi ca yam ekaḥ yaḥ deva nāmadhāḥ viṣṇu nāmāni na anyasya sarva nāmā hariḥ svayam 
AVy_2,2.273–2,2.276	 na nārāyaṇa nāmāni tad anyeṣu apare harau iti ādi śrutayaḥ tatra mānam ca uktaḥ samanvayaḥ purāṇāni purāṇa ādyaiḥ viruddha tvāt na tat pramā tad viruddheṣu naḥ mānam pūrva apara virodhataḥ sama brāhma virodhāt ca niyamāt vaiṣṇaveṣu api moha artha m uktitaḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ ekaḥ guṇa arṇavaḥ skanda sūrya gaṇa īśa ādi matāni nyāyataḥ amutas nirākṛtāni aśeṣeṇa siddhāntasya aviśeṣataḥ 
AVy_2,2.277–2,2.279	 nirākṛtau viśeṣasya bhāvāt śakti matam pṛthak dūṣyate mahatī devī hrīṅkarī sarva kāraṇam tripurābhairavi iti ādi nāmabhiḥ sā abhidhīyate tasyāḥ sadāśiva ādyāḥ ca jāyante deva mānuṣāḥ bhūta bhautikam api etat iti tat na upapadyate dṛṣṭā pumbhyaḥ sadā sṛṣṭiḥ strī pumbhyaḥ vā viśeṣataḥ kevalābhyaḥ na hi strībhyaḥ tatas utpatti asambhavāt 
AVy_2,2.280–2,2.283	 na arcyam mahā vāma matam vāmaiḥ anyat udīryate śiva upasarjanā śaktiḥ sasarja idam samantataḥ iti tat ca upapannam na śivasya akaraṇa tvataḥ adeha tvāt api hi anye brūyuḥ sarvajñam īśvaram aṇu vāmā na tat yuktam īśavāda praveśanāt sārvajñi ādi guṇaiḥ yuktam guru kalpanayā dvayam na yujyate hi atas tu īśaḥ ekaḥ eva prayojakaḥ ukta doṣaḥ ca tad pakṣaḥ iti na eva atra dūṣyate 
AVy_2,2.284–2,2.287	 śruti smṛti itihāsānām sāmastyena virodhataḥ satām jugupsita tvāt ca na aṅgīkāryam hi tat matam pañca rātra niṣedha artham etāni ācakṣate yadi sūtrāṇi ati viruddham tat yatas āha sa bhārate pañca rātrasya kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam jñāneṣu eteṣu rāja indra sarveṣu etat viśiṣṭate pañca rātra vidaḥ ye tu yathā krama parāḥ nṛpa ekānta bhāva upagatāḥ vāsudevam viśanti te 
AVy_2,2.288–2,2.291	 iti gītā ca tad śāstra saṅkṣepaḥ iti hīritam vedena pañca rātreṇa bhaktayā yajñena ca eva hi dṛśyaḥ aham na anyathā dṛśyaḥ varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api iti vārāha vacanam ślokāḥ iti vacaḥ śrutau vedaiḥ ca pañca rātraiḥ ca dhyeyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ pañca rātram ca vedāḥ ca vidyā ekā eva dvi dheyate iti ādi veda vacanaiḥ pañca rātram apodyate katham eva atra doṣaḥ kaḥ utpattiḥ jñaḥ atas iti api 
AVy_2,2.292–2,2.295	 iha eva uktā nacābhūta bhāvaḥ tatra api kathyate anādi karmaṇā baddhaḥ jīvaḥ saṃsāra maṇḍale vāsudeva icchayā nityam bhramati iti hi tad vacaḥ na hi saṃsāra sādi tvam pañca rātra uditam kvacid jīva abhimāni śeṣasya nāmnā saṅkarṣaṇasya tu vāsudevāt janiḥ proktā pradyumnasya tatas tathā manaḥ abhimāninaḥ kāmasya evam sākṣāt hareḥ kvacid saṅkarṣaṇa ādi nām nā eva nitya acintya uru śaktitaḥ vyūhaḥ uktaḥ anyathā ānūdya katham duṣṭa tvam ucyate 
AVy_2,2.296–2,2.300	 yadi vidyāt catur vedān iti vat veda pūraṇam pañca rātrāt iti kutas dveṣaḥ śāṇḍilya vartane atas parama śāstrorudveṣāt uditam āsuraiḥ dūṣaṇam pañca rātrasya vīkṣāyām api na kṣamam atas aśeṣa jagat dhātā nirdoṣa uru guṇa arṇavaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ śruti gaṇa tātparyāt avasīyate andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye tu avidyām upāsate tatas bhūyas iva āpsyanti ye tasyāḥ na eva nindakāḥ tatas vidyām avidyām ca yaḥ jānāti ubhayam saha doṣa jñānāt atītya etān vidyayā amṛtam aśnute 
AVy_2,3.1–2,3.4	 atha aśeṣa samāmnāya virodha apākṛtim prabhuḥ kariṣyan= adhidaiva adhibhūta jīva para ātmanām svarūpa nirṇayāya eva vacanānām parasparam pādena anena avirodham darśayati amita dyutiḥ anubhūti yukti bahu vāc vailomyam ca tatas adhikam etat sarvam sataḥ sāmyam dvāra vaiyarthyam eva ca dṛṣṭa yuktayanu sāri tva muktā anyārtha avirodhataḥ prasiddha nāma svīkāre bahu vākya anuvatiḥ tā 
AVy_2,3.5–2,3.8	 loka dṛṣṭa anusāri tvam jīva sāmyam anāditā tatra tatra parijñānam guṇa sāmya śrutī tathā utpattimat tvam sva guṇān anubhūti alpa kalpane nānā śrutiḥ ca vaicitṛyam yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣa gāḥ vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ca svātantryam anusāritāḥ mukhya tā śaktimat tvam ca vairūpyam sarva saṅgrahaḥ gati ādiḥ īśa śaktiḥ ca sarva māna virodhitāḥ abhīṣya asiddhi suvyaktī śāstra siddhi virparyayaḥ viśeṣa kāraṇam ca iti siddhāntasya eva sādhakāḥ 
AVy_2,3.9–2,3.11	 prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālaḥ devāḥ tad abhimāninaḥ mahat ādyāḥ ca jāyante para adhīna viśeṣitā idam sarvam sasarja iti janimat tvam iha uditam avakāśa mātram ākāśaḥ katham utpadyate anyathā yadi anākāśa tā pūrvam kim mūrta nibiḍam jagat mūtarsampūrṇa tā ca eva yadi anākāśa tā bhavet mūrta dravyāṇi ca ākāśe sthitāni eva hi sarvadā 
AVy_2,3.12–2,3.14	 atas ākāśa śabda uktaḥ tat devaḥ atra vināyakaḥ deha utpattyā samutpannaḥ iti śrutyā abhidhīyate bhūtam api asitam divya dṛṣṭi gocaram eva tu utpadyate avyākṛtam hi gaganam sākṣi gocaram pradeśaḥ iti vijñeyam nityam na utpadyate hi tat tathā api pūrva sambandha paratantra viśeṣa yuj kham eva utpattimat nāma śruti śabda vivakṣitam 
AVy_2,3.15–2,3.18	 prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālaḥ iti ete ca samastaśas īśa adhīna viśeṣeṇa janyāḥ iti eva kīrtitāḥ kāla pravāhaḥ eva ekaḥ nityaḥ na tu viśeṣavān puruṣa avyakta kālānām rama eva eka abhimāninī sisṛkṣu tva viśeṣam tat sākṣāt bhagavat icchayā prāptā eva sṛṣṭā iti uditā pradhānam vikṛteḥ api pumāṃsaḥ deha sambandhāt sṛṣṭimantaḥ iti īritāḥ evam praaya kāle api pratibhāta parāvaraḥ 
AVy_2,3.19–2,3.22	 mukhyau= āyuḥ nitya samaḥ śarīra utpatti kāraṇāt para adhīna viśeṣeṇa janimān eva śabditaḥ na eva kiñcid tatas janma varjitam paramāt ṛte para adhīna viśeṣa tve janmanaḥ sthūla tā bhavaḥ pūrva śabda vilopaḥ ca yadi janma iti kīrtyate ramāyāḥ na eva janma asti caitanyasya api kevalam pradhanasya ca vedasya vedasya api īśvara icchayā vyaktiḥ nāma viśeṣaḥ asti tasmāt tad vaśatā eva hi 
AVy_2,3.23–2,3.25	 utpattiḥ atra kathitā svatantra tvāt para ātmanaḥ na eva utpattiḥ katham api na svatantram tatas aparam acchedyasya api jīvasya vibhāgam bahudhā hariḥ kṛtvā bhogān pradāya eva ca aikyam āpādayet punar atas īśa vaśam sarvam cetana acetanam jagat avibhāgam vibhāgāya yadā nayati keśavaḥ kim aśakyam para īśasya tadā iti hi abhidhīyate 
AVy_2,3.26–2,3.28	 evam sthite api jīva aikyam kecid āhuḥ para ātmanā tat yaḥ aham iti pūrvābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ ca anumābalāt na tat yuktam yatas viṣṇuḥ pṛthak eva abhidhīyate prajñā netraḥ alokaḥ iti muktau bhedaḥ abhidhīyate etam ānandam iti anyā paramam sāmyam iti api idam jñānam apāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ sarge api na upajāyante praaye na vyathanti ca 
AVy_2,3.29–2,3.32	 upasampadya tat jyotiḥ sva rūpeṇa abhipadyate tatra paryeti jakṣan= ca krīḍan= api sadā sukhī ācakṣva me mokṣam dhīrāḥ yam pravadanti tam iti aktaḥ āha vāgdevī param mokṣam prajāpateḥ śākhām śākhām mahā nadyaḥ saṃyānti paritas sravāḥ dhānā pūpāḥ māṃsa kāmāḥ sadā pāyasa kardamāḥ yasmin= agni mukhāḥ devāḥ sa indrāḥ saha marut gaṇāḥ ījire kratubhiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ tat akṣaram upāsate 
AVy_2,3.33–2,3.36	 praviśanti param devam muktāḥ tatra eva bhoginaḥ nirgacchanti yathākāmam pareśena eva coditāḥ bheda dṛṣṭayā abhimānena niḥsaṅgena api kamarṇāḥ kartṛ tvāt sa guṇam brahma puruṣam puruṣa ṛṣabham sa saṅgatya punar kāle kālena īśvara mūrtitā jāte aguṇa vyatikare yathāpūrvam prajāyate ṛcām tvaḥ poṣam āste ca pareṇa preritāḥ sadā yat kāmaḥ tat sṛjati addhaiṣā ātmanā tat sṛjati api 
AVy_2,3.37–2,3.39	 saha eva brahmaṇā kāmān bhuṅkate nistīrṇa tad guṇaḥ duḥkha ādīn= ca parityajya jagat vaya āpāra varjitaḥ bhuṅkte bhogān saha eva uccān itya ādi āgama mānataḥ muktasya bheda avagateḥ katham eva hi abhinnatā jīveśayoḥ na anumā ca tad abhedam pramāpayet mithyā eva bhedaḥ vimataḥ bheda tvāt candrabheda vat iti ced sādhya dharmaḥ ayam sannasan vā nava ubhayam 
AVy_2,3.40–2,3.43	 yadi san= apa siddhāntaḥ saḥ eva āsanniti īrite na ubhayam ced na siddham tat iti mānasya dūṣaṇam na ca māna antareṇa etat śakyam sādhayitum kvacid anumānena ced sā eva hi anavasthā bhaviṣyati naca āgamaḥ tad arthaḥ asti na asat āsīt na tat vadet pariśeṣāt anirvācyam yadi siddhayet para ātmanaḥ anirvācya tvam eva syāt pariśiṣṭaḥ hi asau tadā naca anyaḥ āgamaḥ tatra sat asat pratiyogini 
AVy_2,3.44–2,3.46	 na ca pratyakṣa mātrā asti naca artha āpattiḥ iṣyate bādhā yogāt sataḥ iti bādhā bhāvataḥ eva hi viṣayasya kutas bādhaḥ vidyamānam hi bādhyate na hi vandhyā sutaḥ vadhyaḥ yajñadattaḥ hi vadhyate bādhā yogaḥ sataḥ iti vyāptiḥ eṣā kva dṛśyate kaḥ ca ayam bādhaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ na hi nāśaḥ asataḥ bhavet nivṛttiḥ ca apravṛttasya katham eva upapadyate 
AVy_2,3.47–2,3.50	 na āsīt asti bhaviṣyat ca tat iti jñānam eya tā yadi bādhaḥ tadā sattvam tena eva aṅgīkṛtam punar pratītiḥ na asataḥ iti vadan= aṅgīkaroti tām niṣedhaḥ hi apratītasya kathañcid na upapadyate na ca upamā bhavet atra pratyakṣāt sattvam eva ca śāstra gamya para īśānāt bhedaḥ sva ātmanaḥ īyate anubhūti virodhena katham ekatvam ucyate kiñcid kartā ca duḥkhī iti sarvaiḥ eva anubhūyate 
AVy_2,3.51–2,3.54	 sarvajñaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva śaktiḥ iti śrutaḥ anubhūtāt hi bhedena śrutiḥ eṣā vadati amum upajīvya viruddham tu katham aikyam śrutiḥ vadet aprāmāṇyam yadā bheda vācakasya bhaviṣyati saḥ eva dharmiṇaḥ grāhī tad abhedaḥ katham bhavet yat sva rūpa grahe mānam tad dharme na katham bhavet eka vijñāna vijñaptyā dvayam mānam bhaviṣyati na ced ekam amānam tat dvayam api atra naḥ bhavet 
AVy_2,3.55–2,3.58	 dharmi grāhi virodhaḥ tu tasmāt mānasya dūṣaṇam na upajīvyaḥ hi abhedaḥ atra kvacid bheda śruteḥ balāt na ca māna antara upeyam brahma tat bhavati kvacid yena mānena ca apeyam bhedaḥ tena avagamyate sarva jñāna maya eva īśaḥ yadi upeyaḥ kathañcana sarvajñathva guṇena eva tayā bhedaḥ avagamyate na duḥkha anubhavaḥ kvāpi mithyā anubhava tām vrajet na hi bādhaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ duḥkha ādi anubhavasya tu 
AVy_2,3.59–2,3.62	 yadi duḥkha anubhūtiḥ ca bhrāntiḥ iti avasīyate aduḥkhita aśrutiḥ kena na bhrāntiḥ iti gamyate śruti svarūpam arthaḥ ca mānena eva avasīyate tat ced mānam gṛhītam te kim duḥkha anubhave bhramaḥ na ca bādha viśeṣaḥ asti yat abādhitam eva tat bādhaḥ yadi anubhūte arthe katham nirṇayaḥ īyate kaḥ api hi arthaḥ na niścetum śakyate bhrama vādinā bhrama tvam abhramatvam ca yadā eva anubhava upagam ekasya bhramatā tatra parasya abhramatā kutas 
AVy_2,3.63–2,3.65	 bhrama tvam abhramatvam ca sarvam vedyam hi sākṣiṇā sa ced sākṣī kvacid duṣyaḥ katham nirṇayaḥ īyate viśeṣā sarve eva ete sākṣi pratyaya gocarāḥ ūrīkṛtya ca tān sarvān vyavahāraḥ pravartate sākṣiṇaḥ vyavasāyī tu vyavahāraḥ abhidhīyate tasmāt sarva prasiddhasya vyavahārasya siddhaye sākṣī nirdoṣaḥ eva ekaḥ sadā aṅgī kāryaḥ eva naḥ 
AVy_2,3.66–2,3.68	 śuddhaḥ sākṣī yadā siddhaḥ duḥkhi tvam vāryate katham upajīvya pramāṇam tat bheda grāhakam eva hi atas jīva īśayoḥ bhedaḥ śruti sāmarthya su sthiraḥ tathā api tu cit ānanda pūrvāḥ tad sadṛśāḥ guṇāḥ sāra sva rūpam asya api muktau= api avaśiṣyate atas abheda vat eva etāḥ śrutayaḥ pravadanti hi paurāṇāni ca vākyāni sādṛśya abheda saṃśrayāt 
AVy_2,3.69–2,3.71	 sādṛśyāt ca pradhāna tvāt svātantryāt apicā abhidām āhuḥ īśena jīvasya na svarūpa abhidām kvacid sthāna aikyam aikamatyam ca muktasya tu viśiṣṭate sādṛśyam ca viśeṣeṇa jaḍānām dvayam eva tu bhavet sādṛśyam ati alpam tṛtīyam paramātmanā īśa rūpa kriyāṇām ca guṇānām api sarvaśas tathā eva avayavānām tad svarūpa aikyam tu mukhyatas 
AVy_2,3.72–2,3.74	 yathā udakam durge vṛṣṭam parvateṣu vidhāvati evam dharmān pṛthak paśyan= tān eva anuvidhāvati iti śruteḥ na ubhayam ca bheda abheda ākhyam iṣyate ekam eva advitīyam na iha nānā asti kiñcana mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti śrutau= iva iti asmāt bheda abheda nirākṛtiḥ iva ubhaye ca sādṛśyaḥ iti vāc śabda nirṇaye 
AVy_2,3.75–2,3.77	 bhedasya muktau vacanāt api tad pakṣa nigrahaḥ cetana tva ādi sādṛśyam yadi abheda iti iṣyate aṅgīkṛtam tat asmābhiḥ na sva rūpa eka tā kvacid na kenacid abhedaḥ asti bheda abhedaḥ api vā kvacid samudāya m ṛte viṣṇoḥ sva guṇa ādīn vinā api vā iti śruteḥ na tasya asti bheda abhedaḥ api kenacid abheda śrutayaḥ a ṃśa tvāt sādṛśyam ca aṃśatā asya tu 
AVy_2,3.78–2,3.81	 aṃśaḥ tu dvividhaḥ jñeyaḥ svarūpa aṃśaḥ anyaḥ eva ca vibhinna aṃśaḥ alpa śaktiḥ syāt kiñcid sādṛśya mātra yuj aṃśinaḥ yat tu sāmarthyam yat svarūpam yathā sthitiḥ saḥ eva ced svarūpa aṃśaḥ prādurbhāvāḥ hareḥ yathā sūrya maṇḍala mānī ekaḥ tad prakāśa abhimānavān sūryaḥ atha saptama abdheḥ ca bāhya udasya ca vāripaḥ kaṭhina tvena meru ādeḥ pṛthivyāḥ api devatāḥ dharā devī evam eva ekaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ nānā avatāra rūpeṇa sthitaḥ pūrṇa guṇaḥ sadā 
AVy_2,3.82–2,3.85	 viṣ mūtra akṣi ādi māninyaḥ yathā apabhraṣṭa devatāḥ sūrya ādibhyaḥ tathā eva ayam saṃsārī paramāt pṛthak deha doṣaiḥ ca duṣṭa tvāt apabhraṣṭa ākhya devatāḥ anyāḥ sūrya ādi devebhyaḥ hi anugrāhyāḥ ca taiḥ sadā evam eva parāt viṣṇoḥ pṛthak saṃsāriṇaḥ matāḥ anugrāhyāḥ ca tena eva tad prasādāt ca mokṣiṇaḥ na tu matsya ādi rūpāṇām anugrāhya tvam iṣyate guṇaiḥ aśeṣaiḥ pūrṇa tvāt mukhyā bhedaḥ aparaiḥ naca 
AVy_2,3.86–2,3.88	 aṃśa ābhāsāḥ ca sarve api parasya aṃśāḥ na mukhyatas yathā eṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasmin= etat ātatam na tu pumpāda vat pādāḥ jīvāḥ ete para ātmanaḥ pūrṇāḥ tasya guṇāḥ eva prādurbhāva tayā sthitāḥ evam jagāda parama śrutiḥ nārāyaṇam param akṣayaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ lakṣmyāvāsaḥ laye sthitaḥ muktaiḥ sadā cintyamānaḥ brahma ādyaiḥ tāratamya gaiḥ 
AVy_2,3.89–2,3.94	 prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālaḥ vedāḥ ca iti catuṣyayam nityam svarūpataḥ viṣṇoḥ viśeṣa avāpti mātrataḥ utpattimāt iti proktam lakṣmīḥ tad abhimāninī tatas jātaḥ pumān nāma brahmā asyām vāsudevataḥ sūtra ātmā prāṇa nāmā ca devyau prakṛti māninī tatas rūpam mahān nāma brahmaṇaḥ ahaṅkṛtiḥ śivaḥ brahmaṇaḥ buddhi nāmnā umā tatas indraḥ manaḥ abhidhas skandaḥ ca tatas eva anye sarve devāḥ prajajñire tatra pūrvatanaḥ śreyān guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samastaśas tebhyaḥ ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ tad adhīnāḥ ime sadā janma sthiti laya ajñāna niyati jñāna saṃsṛtiḥ mokṣaḥ ca tad adhīna tvam eteṣām na eva hīyate muktau= api saḥ eva ekaḥ svatantraḥ pūrṇa sat guṇaḥ iti śruti upapattibhyām pāde asmin prabhuṇā uditam 
AVy_2,4.1–2,4.3	 śruti arthaḥ śruti yuktibhyām viruddhaḥ iva dṛśyate yatra tat nirṇayam devaḥ su viśiṣṭa upapattibhiḥ karoti anena pādena tatra spaṣṭa artha vat śrutiḥ viśeṣa śruti vairūpyam māhātmyam vyakta sat guṇāḥ dṛṣṭa āyuktiḥ samāna tvam kartṛ śaktiḥ vimiśratā yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣeṣu sunirṇīta asatu tādṛśāḥ yuktayaḥ nirṇayasya eva svayam bhagavatā uditāḥ 
AVy_3,1.1–3,1.4	 svābhāvikānyathānāma sahābhāvāni athoktayaḥ aviśeṣaḥ viśeṣau ca sahabhāvaḥ vimiśratā viruddha uktiḥ saha sthānam vaiyarthyam ca anyathāgatiḥ yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣasya guṇa ādhikya arthatā ubhavau upapattiḥ dvi rūpa tvam ādhikyam anurūpa tā yogya tā prabala tvam ca vibhāgaḥ kāraṇa abhavaḥ kptiḥ anyā gatiḥ ca eva siddhāntasya eva sādhakāḥ bījā pūruṣa yonīnām saṅga ati niyama ujkhitim athaśabdena bhagavān āha kāraṇataḥ ca tām 
AVy_3,2.1–3,2.4	 paścāt adṛṣṭayavijñāna kāla duḥkha pṛthak bhavāḥ sthāna bhedaḥ viruddha tvam nyāya sāmyam svatobhavaḥ guṇa sāmyam ayogaḥ ca tarka bādhaḥ viloma tā nānābhāvaḥ pralobhaḥ ca pūrva pakṣa gāḥ aśakya kartṛ tā śaktiḥ svatas abodhaḥ tat eva ca amāna kpti sanmāna vyavasthā ati alpatā bhavāḥ viśeṣa dṛṣṭi vākye ca puṃśaktiḥ su nidarśanam alaukika tvam ādhikyam svātantryam nirṇaya pramāḥ 
AVy_3,2.5–3,2.8	 vāsanāḥ sarva vastūnām anādi anubhava āgatāḥ santi eva aśeṣa jīvānām anādi manasi sthitāḥ triguṇa ātmakam manaḥ asti eva yāvat muktiḥ sadātanam tatra eva aśeṣa saṃskārāḥ sañcīyante sadā eva ca sūkṣma tvena laye sat ca prākṛtaiḥ upacīyate sṛṣṭi kāle yadā tat na kutas saṃsāra saṃsthitiḥ saṃskāraiḥ bhagavān eva sṛṣṭvā nānāvidham jagat svapna kāle darśayati bhrāntiḥ jāgrat tvam eva hi 
AVy_3,2.9–3,2.12	 adṛṣṭe ca aśrute bhāve na bhāvaḥ upajāyate adṛṣṭāt aśrutāt bhāvāt na bhāvaḥ upajāyate iti śruti purāṇa uktiḥ anādi tvāt tu yujyate kadācid darśana ayogyam yat tatra api vibhāgataḥ dṛṣṭam samāna adhikaraṇam dṛśyate ca sa ca bhramaḥ vāsanā mātra mūla tvāt jāgradvat spaṣṭa tā na ca bhedaḥ abhedaḥ athavā dvandvam iti praśnaḥ na yujyate draṣṭuḥ svapnasya dṛṣṭa tvāt bhedasya eva akhilaiḥ janaiḥ 
AVy_3,2.13–3,2.15	 praśna doṣā hi catvāraḥ sva vyāhatiḥ asaṅgatiḥ siddhārtha tā ca vaiphalyam na taiḥ syāt tattva nirṇayaḥ tattva nirṇaya vailomyam syāt vāde api hi nigrahaḥ udbhāvanīyam eva syāt na kathā avasitiḥ bhavet vijigīṣu kathāyām tu kathā avasiti kāraṇam parihāre api siddha tvam dūṣaṇam prativādinaḥ pratijñāyām tad anyasya siddha tā eva hi sādhakāḥ 
AVy_3,2.16–3,2.19	 āśraya vyāśraya asiddhī sādhya siddhiḥ ca dūṣaṇam keṣāñcid na ca te doṣāḥ vyāptau satyām kathañcana doṣaḥ vyāhatiḥ eva asti nṛśṛṅga astitva sādhane yatra vyāhata tā na asti kaḥ ati saṅgaḥ asya sādhane pratyakṣa āgama mūlāḥ tu nyāyāḥ sarve bhavanti hi nyāya ābhāsāḥ amūlāḥ syuḥ nyāyasya anyasya tau punar adṛṣṭe vyabhicāre tu sādhakam tat iti sphuṭam jñāyate sākṣiṇā eva at vā māna bādhe na tat bhavet 
AVy_3,2.20–3,2.23	 yat sākṣiṇā eva māna tvam mānānām avasīyate amānasya tu māna tvam mānasa tvāt calam bhavet utsargataḥ api yat prāptam apavāda vivarjitam vyabhicārya pavādena mānam eva bhaviṣyati atas hi bhojana ādīnām iṣṭa sādhana tā anumā mānam vyavahṛtau nityam vyabhicāraḥ hi tatra ca vyāpta tve vyāśraya tvam tu katham eva hi dūṣaṇam rohiṇī udayaḥ āsannaḥ kṛttikā abhyuditāḥ yatas iti ukte sādhanam no kim na hi ājñā eva atra sādhakāḥ 
AVy_3,2.24–3,2.26	 anyat sat asatoḥ viśvam iti ca vyāhateramā asiddha sādhane doṣaḥ kaḥ vyāptiḥ yadi vidyate vyāptiḥ ca vyatirekeṇa tatra taiḥ ca eva gamyate aprasiddhasya sādhyasya sādhaka tvam yat eṣyate liṅgasya uktau viśeṣaḥ ayam kena mānena gamyate sādhanam paramāṇu ādeḥ yadā siddhasya ca iṣyate yathā anubhavam eva etat na aṅgīkāryam kutas tadā 
AVy_3,2.27–3,2.29	 yatra na ati prasaṅgaḥ asti mānam na ca viparyate kliṣṭa kalpanayā eva atra sādhyam iti ati durvacaḥ pariśeṣaḥ mithas siddhiḥ cakraka sva āśraya ādayaḥ asiddha sādhaka tvena pañca avayava tām vinā aṅgīkāryāḥ samastaiḥ tad niyamaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ sidda sa adhana tāyām ca na kathā avasitiḥ bhavet vyabhicāraḥ hetu asiddhiḥ eka pakṣe api dūṣaṇam 
AVy_3,2.30–3,2.33	 sādhya sādhana vaikalyam dṛṣṭāntasya viśeṣaṇe vaiyathyarmekā siddhau ca viśiṣṭa asiddhiḥ eva hi aprayojaka tā tatra prathama praśna dūṣaṇam siddha praśna ādikam yat tad ādhikya anta gartam bhavet arthāpatti upama abhāvāḥ anumā antargatāḥ kvacid pratyakṣa antargataḥ abhāvaḥ sukha ādeḥ niyamena ca anyatra khaḍiti prāptaḥ prārambha ādyāḥ ca yuktayaḥ āgama artha a= asiti arthāḥ niyata vyāptayaḥ akhilāḥ 
AVy_3,2.34–3,2.36	 vākyam prakaraṇam sthānam samākhyā ca tathāvidhāḥ kuru pāṇḍava vat teṣām upapatteḥ pṛthak vacaḥ sva nyāyaiḥ sādhanam kāryam para nyāyaiḥ tu dūṣaṇam sva nyāyaiḥ dūṣaṇam ca syāt sādhitaiḥ prativādinaḥ prasaṅga artha tayā proktāḥ na siddhāntasya dūṣakāḥ chalam jātiḥ iti dvedhā vyāhati antaram iṣyate jātiḥ sva vyāhatiḥ jñeyā chalam artha antara uttaram 
AVy_3,2.37–3,2.40	 evam saṃśodhita nyāya sat āgama virodhataḥ na anirvācyam iha proktam māyā mātra padena hi vilakṣaṇam sat asatoḥ iti hi vyāhatam svatas pratiyogi tvam api asya brahmaṇaḥ aṅgīkṛtam bhavet mithyā ced pratiyogi tvam vailakṣaṇyam tatas na hi avilakṣaṇa tvam satyam syāt mithyātvam brahmaṇaḥ tatas anirvācyasya sattvam vā yadi dharmāḥ na kecana brahmaṇaḥ na eva jijñāsyam jijñāsā dharma nirṇayaḥ 
AVy_3,2.41–3,2.44	 idam ittham iti jñānam jijñāsāyāḥ prayojanam ittham bhāvaḥ hi dharmaḥ asya na ced na pratiyogitā ittham bhāva ātmakān dharmān āhuḥ ca śrutayaḥ akhilāḥ adṛśya tva ādayaḥ api asya guṇāḥ hi prabhuṇā uditāḥ yadi syuḥ tādṛśāḥ dharmāḥ sarvajña tva ādayaḥ na kim anya apekṣā yadi syuṣṭe sattā evam deśa kāla gā deśa kāla anapekṣā hi na sattā kvāpi dṛśyate sarva dharma ujjñitasya asya kim śāstreṇa adhigamyate 
AVy_3,2.45–3,2.48	 mithyā dharma vidhātuḥ ca vedasya eva apramāṇa tā aprāptām bhrāntim āpādya kim vedaḥ mānatām vrajet na hi vedam vinā brahma vedyam dharmāḥ ca tad gatāḥ veda vedyasya mithyātvam yadi na aikyasya tat katham dharma āropaḥ api sāmānya dharma ādīnām hi daśarne idantat ādi dharmi tve dharmaḥ anyaḥ kalpyate atra hi sarva dharma vihīnasya dharma āropaḥ kva dṛśyate tad artham yadi dharmāṇām āropaḥ sānavasthitiḥ 
AVy_3,2.49–3,2.52	 īśa tad jñāna veda akṣa ja anumā mātṛ pūrviṇaḥ bhrāntiḥ viśvasya yena eva māna ābhāsena kalpyate atra hi tanmātrasya anyathā bhāvāt kim na syāt viśva satya tā yena idam kalpyate bhrāntam bhrāntiḥ tasya eva kim na sā bhrānta tve tasya viśva ādeḥ īśādya bhrāntam eva hi bhaveyuḥ bhrāntayaḥ nṛṇām naiva īśa ādeḥ kathañcana satya tvam akṣaja prāptam yadi bhrāntam iti iṣyate prāmāṇyam āgamasya api pratyakṣāt anyatas kutas 
AVy_3,2.53–3,2.55	 sākṣi pratyakṣataḥ hi eva mānānām mānateyate sākṣiṇaḥ sva prakāśa tvam anavasthā tatas na hi tātkālikam pramāṇa tvam akṣajasya yadā bhavet aikya āgamasya kim na syāt tasya api etādṛśam yadi aikya prāmāṇya mithyā tvam yadā viśvasya satya tā aikya āgamasya māna tvam yadi abādhyam iti iṣyate akṣajasya api māna tvam na abādhyam kim iti iṣyate 
AVy_3,2.56–3,2.59	 advaita hāni sāmānyāt na viśeṣaḥ ca kaścana yadi svatas tvam prāmāṇye viśva sattā katham na te prāmāṇyasya ca maryādā kālataḥ vyāhatā bhavet kāla antare apyamānam ced idānīm mānatā kutas mithyā tva mānam mokṣe api mānam kim na iti bhaṇya tām māna tve advaita hāniḥ syāt amāna tve api amokṣa tā viśvasya punar āpattiḥ mithyāmānam yadā na mā asti ced mukta yavasthā ca dvaitāpattiḥ atas anyathā 
AVy_3,2.60–3,2.62	 amukta tvam tathā kāle kāla adhīnā hi mukta tā kālaḥ eva āgamaḥ api āha muktim kāla nivartane mukteḥ api nivṛttiḥ syāt saṃsāri tvam atas bhavet kva ca pratyakṣatas prāptam anumāgama bādhitam deha ātma tvam yadi na tat prāptam pratyakṣatas kvacid mama dehaḥ iti hi eva na dehaḥ aham iti pramā upacāraḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ aham iti kardama lepane vastrasya yadvat evam syāt yadi upādhi kṛtam tadā svatas śukla tva vat kārṣṇyam na mama iti pratīyate 
AVy_3,2.63–3,2.65	 katham ca bhedaḥ deha ādeḥ ātmanaḥ na pramīyate jāta mātrāḥ mṛgāḥ gāvaḥ hastinaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ khaṣāḥ bhaya abhaya sva bhoga ādau kāraṇāni vijānate asmṛtau pūrva dehasya vijñānam tat katham bhavet anvaya vyatireka ādeḥ anusandhāna vismṛtau yadā deha antara jñānam deha aikyau= asitiḥ kutas vyāpta tvāt ātmanaḥ dehe vyavahāreṣu apāṭavāt 
AVy_3,2.66–3,2.69	 bheda jñāne api ca aṅgāra vahni vat svāvivikta vat bhavanti vyavahārāḥ ca na hi pratyakṣa gān api arthān yathā anubhavataḥ pratipādayitum kṣamāḥ lokāḥ tatas hi pratyakṣa siddham na anyena kenacid śakyam vārayitum kvāpi tat ced na uttara gocaram katham eva uttaraḥ kālaḥ tad gaḥ mokṣaḥ ca gamyate āgamaḥ api hi sāmānye siddhe pratyakṣatas punar viśeṣam gamayet eva katham śakti grahaḥ anyathā 
AVy_3,2.70–3,2.73	 atīta anāgata artheṣu jāte śakti grahe akhilam viśeṣam jñāpayet vākyam na tad ajñāta śaktike śaktiḥ ced vartamāne syāt na atīta anāgatam vadet yadi śakti grahaḥ anyatra katham sa syāt tad agrahe sāmānyam dṛṣṭam eva asau= anyatra gamayet yadi sāmānya varjitam vastu svarūpam gamayet katham na svarūpa tva sāmānyam kena api aṅgīkṛtam kvacid svarūpam ced anugatam vyāvṛttam tatra kim bhavet 
AVy_3,2.74–3,2.76	 sarva anugata dharmāṇām ante hi sva tvam iṣyate kim vyāvṛttam iti praśne svarūpam iti kevalam syāt uttaram tatas anyat ced tat eva svayam eva naḥ evam vyāvṛtta rūpe api yadā śakti grahaḥ bhavet tasya sāmānyatas jñānam vinā sa ca bhavet kutas atas viśeṣa sāmānya rūpam sarvam api iṣyate vyāvṛttam yat ca sāmānyam tat eva syāt viśeṣataḥ 
AVy_3,2.77–3,2.80	 naca eka dharmatā tena padārthānām parasparam dharmāṇām bheda dṛṣṭayā eva tad sādṛśyasya darśanāt atas sarva padārthāḥ ca sāmānyāt sākṣi gocarāḥ sarvam iti eva vijñānam sarveṣām katham anyathā kiñcid sādṛśya vijñānāt akhilasya api vastunaḥ śabda śakti grahaḥ ca syāt tad tad sādṛśyamānataḥ pratyakṣam mānasam ca eva yadā atīta artha gocaram tadā smṛti pramāṇa tvam atīta tva viśeṣitam 
AVy_3,2.81–3,2.84	 ādhikyam anubhūtāt tu yadā atīta tvam iṣyate mānatā ca katham na syāt smṛteḥ bādhaḥ ca na atra hi māna tvam pratyabhijñāyāḥ api sarva anubhūti gam atīta vartamāna tva dharmiṇī sā ca dṛśyate na ca sā smṛti mātra ardhā tat idantu agraha ekatas atas na vatarmāna eka niyamaḥ syāt grahe akṣa je na ca pramāṇataḥ anyā syāt pramitiḥ nāma kutracid māna abhāvāt gauravāt ca kalpanāyāḥ kim etayā 
AVy_3,2.85–3,2.88	 mayā etat jñātam iti tu sākṣi gam jñāna gocaram jñānam eva tatas anyā na pramitiḥ nāma dṛśyate māna amātṛ prameyāṇām tad ucchittiḥ na hi kvacid svapnānām api ca eteṣām na bādhaḥ dṛśyate kvacid jāgrat tva mātram atra ekam anyathā dṛśyate sphuṭam atas mithyā na ca svapnaḥ jāgrat vat ja agradeva ca ātma vat kvacid ātmā ca syāt eva bhrama gocaraḥ etāvatā na mithyā asau svapne jāgarite tathā 
AVy_3,2.89–3,2.91	 yadi ātmani anyathā dṛśyam bhrāntam atra api tat bhavet abādhita anuvṛtteḥ tu svapna ādeḥ bhrānta tā kutas na ca kācid pramā viśva bhrānta tve sarvam eva ca abhrānta tve pramāṇam tu katham tat bhrāntitā bhavet kiñca bhrānta tva vādī sa bhrānta tvam sva matasya ca aṅgīkaroti niyatam tatra sampratipanna tā vādinoḥ tena ca abhrāntam viśvam eva bhaviṣyati 
AVy_3,2.92–3,2.95	 bhrānti tva bhrānta tā ced syāt katham na abhrānti satya tā aśeṣa doṣa duṣyam tat matam heyam bubhūṣibhiḥ yena sva mata heya tvam svayam aṅgīkṛtam sadā bhrānti tvāt durghaṭa tvasya bhūṣaṇa tvāt ca kevalam unmattaḥ api katham tasya matam svīkartum icchati īśa śakteḥ acintya tvāt mahā unmattaiḥ pravartitam atas prajñā atra māyā uktā jaivī upādānam eva sā nimittam aiśvarī mukhyam nirmitam trātam eva ca 
AVy_3,2.96–3,2.99	 tābhyām saha pṛthak ca eva māyā mātram iti īryate ubhābhyām mātam aiśvaryā trātam saha pṛthak tatas prajñā ātmakam manaḥ yena manaḥ rūpāḥ ca vāsanāḥ dhīḥ bhīḥ iti manaḥ tu ā iva iti āha ca śrutirañjasā cit acit miśram eva etat manaḥ yāvat ca saṃsṛtiḥ tena avasthāḥ imāḥ sarvāḥ jīvaḥ paśyati sarvadā manaḥ vikārāḥ viṣayāḥ svāpnāḥ yat bahya vat na te sthūlāḥ bhavanti atas teṣām spaṣṭa tā na tathā kvacid 
AVy_3,2.100–3,2.103	 kvacid spaṣṭāḥ api syuṣye vāsanā mānasī ca sā īśa icchayā antardadhāti vyajyate ca punar tayā sṛṣṭvā eva vāsānabhiḥ ca prapañcam svāpnam īśvaraḥ vāsanā mātra tām tasya nītvā antardhāpayati ajaḥ suṣupti moha bodhān= ca svavaśaḥ tad vaśam sadā jīvam nayati deveśaḥ na anyaḥ kartā asya kaścana na sthāna bhedataḥ api asya bhedaḥ kaścid pareśituḥ sarvatra aśeṣa doṣa ujkha pūrṇa kalyāṇa cit guṇaḥ 
AVy_3,2.104–3,2.107	 tad viruddham tu yat tatra mānam na eva bhavet kvacid mahātātparya rodhena katham tat mānam atra tu duḥkha apyaya sukhau= āpti hetu tvena eva veda vāc bhavet mānam tad īśānāt prasannāt eva na anyathā prasanna tā guṇa utkarṣa jñānāt eva hi kevalam nirdoṣa tā parijñānāt api na anyena kenacid yaḥ mām aśeṣa doṣa ujkham guṇa sarva sva bṛṃhitam jānāti asmai prasannaḥ aham dadyām muktim naca anyathā 
AVy_3,2.108–3,2.111	 yaḥ mām aśeṣa abhyadhikam vijānāti saḥ eva mām vijānāti akhilān= tasya dadyām kāmān param padam yaḥ mām evam asammūḍhaḥ kim mā nindanti śatravaḥ ityādi veda smṛti gavākyaiḥ eva avasīyate lokataḥ ca prasādena muktiḥ sa guṇa vedanāt mahātātparya mukhyasya virodhāt atas eva hi doṣi tva nirguṇa tva alpa guṇa tva ādi kathañcana na arthaḥ śruti purāṇa ādeḥ tat viruddhaḥ akhilasya ca arthaḥ svayam vinirṇītaḥ vāsudevena sa ādaram 
AVy_3,2.112–3,2.115	 iti guhyatamam śāstram idam uktam mayā anagha etat buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārata iti atas akhila sat śāstra viruddha tvena na anumā vartate tatra tena īśaḥ nirṇītaḥ akhila sat guṇaḥ na ca cit tvāt abhinna tvam jīvasya īśa vat āpyate yatas ābhāsatām eva śrutiḥ asya vadati alam yathā eṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasmin= etat ātatam chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśā pumā adhīnā ca dṛśyate evam eva ātmakāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ 
AVy_3,2.116–3,2.119	 sattā pratīti kāryeṣu pum a dhīnaḥ yatheyate ābhāsaḥ eva puruṣāḥ muktāḥ ca paramātmanaḥ chāyā viṣṇo ramā tasyāḥ chāyā dhātā viśeṣakau tasya indra kāmau ca tayoḥ tayoḥ anye akhilāḥ api hareḥ brahma asya gīḥ tasyāḥ viśeṣau= indraḥ etayoḥ māraḥ ca ābhāsakāḥ sarve etayoḥ tad adhīnataḥ sarve alpa śaktayaḥ ca eva pūrṇa śaktiḥ paraḥ hariḥ cetana tve api bhinnāḥ te tasmāt etena sarvadā ityādi śruti vākyebhyaḥ jñāyate bhedaḥ eva hi 
AVy_3,2.120–3,2.123	 ābhāsa tvam hi nirṇītam jīvasya paramātmanaḥ tat na yuktam yad ābhāse upādhyāyattaḥ īyate upādhi āyatta tā bhāvāt ābhāsa tva virodhataḥ cetana tvena ca aṃśa tvāt samudāya aikyam āpatet atas pṛthaktavam uditam samudāya aṃśayoḥ bhavet īśā ākhyā samudāye syāt īśa rūpeṣu iva uditā atas deha ādi upādhīnām apāye sama tā bhavet īśa rūpaiḥ atha ābhāsāḥ mukhyatas sūryaka ādi vat 
AVy_3,2.124–3,2.126	 yadā tadā upādhi āyatta rūpāṇām nāśitā bhavet iti āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham āha veda adhipaḥ prabhuḥ atas eva upamā iti eva ca anya ābhāsa viśeṣitām yat uktam tat adhīna tvam sarva avasthāsu aśeṣataḥ jīvasya sadṛśa tvam ca cittva mātram na ca aparam tāvat mātreṇa ca ābhāsaḥ rūpam eṣām cit ātmanām na upādhi adhīnata ādyaiḥ ca na ati sāmyam nidarśane 
AVy_3,2.127–3,2.130	 kiñcid sukha ādi sādṛśyam api īśenesura anṛte tatas ābhāsate nityam tadvat ābhāsate api ca bhānam asti tvam apica eva asamantāt yatas tatas jīvaḥ ābhāsaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ sadā eva paramātmanaḥ na jala āyatta sūrya ādi pratibimba upama tvataḥ tad adhīna tvam eva iti kiñcid sādṛśyam eva ca samprakāśayataḥ sūtra gatau= akhila mānataḥ jīveśa bheda dṛṣṭayā eva samudāya eka tā kutas aśeṣa doṣa rāhityam sarva śakti tvataḥ hareḥ 
AVy_3,2.131–3,2.134	 sarva upeta iti kathitam atas aikyam kva doṣiṇā aśeṣa śakti yuktaḥ ced svātantryāt doṣavān katham anusandhāna rahitam aikyam ced ekatā na tat cetanā aikye anusandhānam pramāṇam na eva ca aparam anusandhāna rahita samudāya aikyam eva ced cetaneṣu astu tad nāma mātram eva yatas tatas muktau syāt anusandhānam ced mithyā jñānitā bhavet sarvajñaḥ eka tām na anusandhatte na eva sā yatas 
AVy_3,2.135–3,2.138	 paścāt syāt anusandhānam ced mithyā jñānitā bhavet vidyamāna anusandhānam na ced ajña tvam āpatet asat aikyam bhavet paścāt yadi syāt saptamaḥ rasaḥ samudāya aikyam etasmāt dūratas apākṛtam sadā atas aśeṣa guṇa unnaddham nirdoṣam yāvat eva hi tāvat eva īśvaraḥ nāma tatra bhedaḥ api na kvacid na iha nānā asti kim api harayaḥ ayam ayam hi saḥ ityādi śruti mānena jīva aṃśāḥ sarve eva ca 
AVy_3,2.139–3,2.141	 niyamena anusandhānavantaḥ yadi ekatā svatas aṃśinaḥ aśeṣa sandhānam ati alpasya api vidyate bhuvi jātena ca aṃśena sukha duḥkha ādi tad gatam anubhūyate viśeṣaḥ tu kaścid īśa kṛtaḥ bhavet īśasya acintya śakti tvāt na aśakyam kvāpi vidyate sa īśata anupapannā eva yadi jīva eka tā asya hi anīśasya īśata iti eva viruddham sarva mānataḥ 
AVy_3,2.142–3,2.145	 īśa tvena eva vijñātam anīśa tvena ced śrutiḥ anīśa tvena vijñātam īśa tvena athavā diśet upajīvya virodhena na eva māna tvam eṣyati atas eva īśata asiddheḥ na kiñcid śakyam asya ca īśa tve anīśa bhedena śrutyā samyak prakāśite ayuktam api ca anyatra yuktam bhavati tad balāt atas anyatra api yat dṛṣṭam tat īśena eva kalpyate śruti ābhāsa āptam api na hi īśa tva paripanthi yat 
AVy_3,2.146–3,2.149	 īśaḥ anīśaḥ jagat mithyā duḥkhī muktaḥ bhidā na hi iti pratijñā vyāghātaḥ sarva doṣa adhika adhikaḥ iti hi brahma tarka uktiḥ ati heyam atas akhilaiḥ bubhūṣubhiḥ matam idam jīva īśā bheda vādinaḥ na ayuktam īśituḥ kiñcid īśa tvasya avirodhi yat yadi īśitva virodhi syāt tat eva ayuktam añjasā īśitvasya avirodhena yojayitvā akhilāḥ pramāḥ siddha īśi tvena ca ayuktam api hi īśe na yojayet 
AVy_3,2.150–3,2.152	 mānataḥ prāptam akhilam nāmānam yojayet kvacid iti hi brahma tarka ukti ḥ atas yuktam iha uditam sa ca aprākṛta rūpa tvāt arūpaḥ sva guṇa śatmakam rūpam asya śiraḥ pāṇi pāda ādi ātmakam iṣyate atas na anitya tā na eva śruti dvaya virodhitā yathā hi taijasasya eva prakāśasya ujkhitau= api ātmā eva jyotiḥ iti āha jīvasya īśam śrutiḥ tathā 
AVy_3,2.153–3,2.156	 tad bhakti tāratamyena tāratamyam vimukti gam brahma ādīnām ca sarveṣām ānanda ādeḥ yathākramam pratibimba vat api eṣām ānandaḥ anya guṇāḥ yathā nārāyaṇa guṇa adhīnaḥ ca ati alpaḥ tad apekṣayā tasmāt bhinnaḥ ca satatam anyat jñānam parasya ca anyat jñānam tu jīvānām anyaḥ ānanda īśatā mukhyeśatā para īśasya gauṇī jīvasya sā yatas iti śruteḥ sṛṣṭi nāśau tad adhīna aviti īrite svabhāva tvāt sthiteḥ na etat apekṣā iti na yujyate 
AVy_3,2.157–3,2.160	 yatas svabhāvaḥ akhilaḥ īśa āyattaḥ akhilasya ca avyaktaḥ api svaktayā eva bhaktānām dṛśyate hariḥ tad abhinnāḥ guṇāḥ nityam api sarve viśeṣataḥ guṇa tvena guṇi tvena bhoktṛ bhogya tayā sthitāḥ viśeṣa ātma tayā teṣām nitya śaktayā ātmanā tathā nitya sthiteḥ na dharmāṇām kriyā ādīnām anitya tā na viśeṣa ātma tā ca iyam anityā śakti rūpa tā sā eva yat sa viśeṣā syāt viśeṣaḥ anyaḥ na ca api ayam 
AVy_3,2.161–3,2.164	 sva nirvāha ka tā hetoḥ tathā api syāt viśeṣataḥ viśeṣa tvena vijñāteḥ pramāṇaiḥ akhilaiḥ api sasarja sañjahāra iti viśeṣaḥ hi avagamyate śrutyā eva sa saḥ eva iti tad abhedaḥ ca gamyate bhedaḥ yadi viśeṣasya sa bhedaḥ bhedinā katham bhinnaḥ ced anavasthā syāt abhinnaḥ ced purā na kim viśeṣaḥ abhinnaḥ eva iti tena na abhyupagamyate abhinnaḥ nivirśeṣaḥ ced bhedaḥ tad bheda tā kutas 
AVy_3,2.165–3,2.168	 anena anena bhinnaḥ ayam iti yat sa viśeṣataḥ bhedaḥ eva eṣa bahudhā dṛśyate tat kim uttaram abheda bhedayoḥ ca eva svarūpa tvam hi bhedinā tayoḥ api aviśeṣa tve paryāya tvam hi śabdayoḥ abheda bheda śabdau ca paryāyau= iti kaḥ vadet bhedaḥ anyonyam abhedaḥ ca bhedinā ced viśeṣa tā nirviśeṣe katham bhedaḥ bhedinā ekaḥ tathā abhidā punar tayoḥ vibhedaḥ ca bhedi mātra tvataḥ bhavet 
AVy_3,2.169–3,2.172	 bhedinaḥ ca eva bhedasya viśeṣaḥ yadi gamyate abheda abhedinoḥ ca eva kim bhedaḥ abheda bhedayoḥ viśeṣeṇa eva sarvatra yadi vyavahṛtiḥ bhavet kalpanā gauravāya eva kim bhedaḥ kalpyate tadā aikya pratītyabhāvena bhedaḥ eva gavaśvayoḥ saḥ eva iti pratītau hi viśeṣaḥ nāma bhaṇyate saccit ādera paryāya siddhayartham māyinā api hi aṅgīkāryaḥ viśeṣaḥ ayam yadi asati aviśeṣaṇam pṛthak pṛthak vārayitum śabda antaram iti iṣyate 
AVy_3,2.173–3,2.176	 māyā viśeṣa rāhitya viśeṣeṇa viśeṣitā satyasya api bhavet sā ca tathā ced anavasthitiḥ yadi satye viśeṣaḥ na na tad uktiḥ bhavet tadā lakṣyate ced tena lakṣyam iti api syāt viśeṣitā punar punar lakṣaṇāyām api syāt anavasthitiḥ yadi abhāva viśeṣi tvam syāt aṅgīkṛtam eva te asārvajñyādirāhityam api evam te bhaviṣyati tadā sārvajñyam eva syāt bhāva artha tvāt nañoḥ dvayoḥ 
AVy_3,2.177–3,2.180	 yadi na etādṛśam grāhyam asukha tva anivartanāt asattva jñāna tā ādeḥ ca syāt asattva ādikam tadā anṛta ādi virodhi tvam yadi asya abhyupagamyate anaiśvarya virodhi tvam api evam kim nivāryate akhaṇḍa khaṇḍanāt evam viśeṣaḥ akhaṇḍa vādinā khaṇḍitena api manasā svīkāryaḥ ananyathāgateḥ akhaṇḍa khaṇḍa vādibhyām khaṇḍākhaṇḍena ca eva tat mahādareṇa śirasi viśeṣaḥ dhāryaḥ eva hi 
AVy_3,2.181–3,2.183	 nidarśana trayeṇa atas bhagavān atyabhinna tām guṇānām ādareṇa āha tat ca na abhihita anvayaḥ yadā aśeṣa viśeṣāṇa muktiḥ sāmānyatas bhavet pada ekena api uttareṇa viśeṣa avagatiḥ bhavet yatas aśeṣa viśeṣāṇām vastunā asti eva ca ekatā atas sāmānyatas jñātaḥ pada antara balāt punar bhavet viśeṣataḥ jñānaḥ tena syāt anvita uktitā 
AVy_3,2.184–3,2.187	 sva arthaḥ eva anvitaḥ yasmāt kenacid tad viśeṣataḥ anena iti tad uktayā eva jñāyate anubhavena hi yadi ananvitam eva etat padam sva artham vadet iha tathā anyāni api sarvāṇi kaḥ kuryāt anvayam punar vyāpāraḥ na hi śabdasya paraḥ sva artha prakāśanāt pumān api eka vāra uktayā kṛtakṛtyaḥ yadā bhavet anvayasya katham jñānam śabda artha tvam yadā asya na yadā eva ananvita arthasya vacanam taiḥ padaibharvet 
AVy_3,2.188–3,2.191	 ananvitaḥ syāt śabda arthaḥ na tad arthaḥ hi saḥ anvayaḥ nirākāṅkṣa padāni eva vākyam iti ucyate budhaiḥ tat tad artha abhidhānena syāt nirākāṅkṣa tā ca sā apūrteḥ tāvat arthānām ākāṅkṣā pūrvam iṣyate karma kartṛ kriyāṇām tu pūrtau kaḥ anyaḥ anvayaḥ bhavet apūrtiḥ ced padaiḥ uktaiḥ kim nṛśṛṅgeṇa pūryate vyāpāraḥ ced punar teṣām anuktau= api kim na saḥ 
AVy_3,2.192–3,2.194	 ukte buddhi sthatā hetoḥ yadi vyāpāraḥ iṣyate buddhi stha tvāya yatnam na katham kuryuḥ purā eva ca puruṣa adhīna tā teṣām yadi paścāt ca sā samāḥ pumān eva anvayāya eṣām paścāt yadi viceṣyate ananvita abhidhānānām saḥ eva artha antara uktiṣu yatatām śabda śaktiḥ ced tatra na eva anvaye katham tad kalpanā guru tva ādi doṣa itaḥ abhihita anvayaḥ anubhūti viruddhaḥ ca tyājyaḥ eva manīṣibhiḥ 
AVy_3,2.195–3,2.198	 kartṛ śabde hi abhihite dharma sāmānya vedanāt viśeṣa dharmam anvicchan kim iti eva hi pṛcchati guṇa kriyā ādi dharmāṇām viśeṣe kathite punar nirākāṅkṣaḥ bhavet yasmāt śabdāḥ anvita vācakāḥ atas ananta guṇa ātmā ekaḥ bhagavān ekaḥ eva tu ucyate sarva vedaiḥ ca te ca akhila vilakṣaṇāḥ sarve sarva guṇa ātmānaḥ sarva kartāraḥ eva ca tathā api sa viśeṣāḥ ca vidvadi vutpattitaḥ api ca 
AVy_3,2.199–3,2.202	 taiḥ taiḥ śabdaiḥ ca bhaṇyante yujyate ca upadeśataḥ anya ānanda ādi sādṛśyam ānu kūlyādinā param pūrṇa tva ādi mahat teṣām vailakṣaṇyam śrutau śrutam pūrṇe aśeṣa niyantā ca sukhāt utamaḥ eka kalaḥ guṇa uru samudāyaḥ ayam vāsudevaḥ sa niṣkaaḥ vāsudeva śrutiḥ sā eṣā guṇān vakti hareḥ parān saḥ eva aśeṣa jīva stha nissaṅkha yāna ādi kālikān dharma adharmān sadā paśyan sva icchayā bodhayati ajaḥ 
AVy_3,2.203–3,2.205	 kāṃścid teṣām phalam ca eva dadāti svayam acyutaḥ na te viśeṣam kam api preraṇa ādikam ucyate kuryuḥ kadāpi tena ayam svatantraḥ anupacārataḥ karmāṇi tāni ca pṛthak cetanāni eva sarvaśas acetana śarīrāṇi sva karma phala bhāñci ca pratyekam teṣu ca ananta karmāṇi evaṃvidhāni ca tāni ca evam iti īśasya nissīmā śaktiḥ uttamā 
AVy_3,2.206–3,2.209	 ekā eva brahmahatyā hi varāha hariṇā uditā brahmapāra stavena eva niṣkrāntāḥ rāja dehataḥ stotrasya tasya māhātmyāt vyādha tvam gamitā punar prāpya jñānam param ca apa tathā anyāni api sarvadā anantāni uditāni evam prabhuṇā kapilena hi saṃsāre pacyamānāni karmāṇi api pṛthak pṛthak tasmāt ananta māhātmya guṇa pūgaḥ janārdanaḥ bhaktyā para mayā arādhyaḥ iti pāda arthaḥ īryate 
AVy_3,3.1–3,3.4	 vairāgyataḥ bhakti dārḍhyam tena upāsā yadā bhavet āparokṣyam bhavet viṣṇoḥ iti pāda kramaḥ bhavet yuktitaḥ jñāta veda arthaḥ nirasya samayān parān paraspara virodham ca praṇudya aśeṣa vākya gam adhyātma praṇavaḥ bhūtvā tasya sannihita tvataḥ bahu yukti virodhānām bhānāt tad sahita śruteḥ virodham ca nirākṛtya śrutīnām prāṇataḥ tvagān parihṛtya virodhān= ca tad prasāda anurañjitaḥ 
AVy_3,3.5–3,3.8	 deha kartṛ tvam īśasya jñātvā tad pitṛtā smṛteḥ viśeṣa sneham āpādya sarva kartṛ tvataḥ adhikam niṣpādya bahu mānam ca tad anyatra ati duḥkhataḥ utpādya adhika vairāgyam tad guṇa ādhikya vedanāt sarvasya tad vaśa tvāt ca dārḍhyam bhakteḥ avāpya ca yateta upāsanāya eva viśiṣṭa ācārya sampadā kartavyā brahma jijñāsā iti ukte kim iti saṃśaye atas iti udite api asya viśeṣa anuktitaḥ punar 
AVy_3,3.9–3,3.11	 sṛṣṭi bandhana mokṣa ādi kartṛ tvasya śrutatvataḥ yatas mokṣa ādi dāta asauvataḥ jijñāsyaḥ eva vaḥ iti āha tat param brahma vyāsa ākhyam jñāna raśmimat yena eva bandha mokṣaḥ syāt sa ca jijñāsayā gataḥ su prasannaḥ bhavet īśaḥ jijñāsā ataḥ asya mukti dā mokṣāt idatvam īśasya katham eva avagamyate iti ced śāstra yoni tvāt śāstra gamyaḥ hi mokṣa daḥ 
AVy_3,3.12–3,3.15	 pratyakṣa avasitebhyaḥ syāt yadi mokṣaḥ kathañcana kim iti anādi saṃsāra magnāḥ sarvāḥ imāḥ prajāḥ yasmāt niyamataḥ duḥkha hāniḥ pratyakṣataḥ bhavet dhāvanti eva tam uddiśya rāja ādyam akhilāḥ prajāḥ anumāna gamyataḥ mokṣaḥ yadi tasya anumā eva hi dṛṣṭa pūruṣa vat mokṣa dātṛ tām vinivārayet tad śāstra gamyaḥ eva ekaḥ mokṣa daḥ bhavati dhruvam śāstra gamyaḥ ca na anyaḥ asti mokṣa da tvena keśavāt 
AVy_3,3.16–3,3.18	 mokṣa daḥ hi svatantraḥ syāt paratantraḥ svayam sṛtau vartamānaḥ katham śaktaḥ para mokṣāya kevalam anya āśrayeṇa yadi eṣa dadyāt mokṣam saḥ eva hi tena ananusṛtaḥ mokṣam na dadyāt anya vākyataḥ atas tad artham api sa jñeyaḥ viṣṇuḥ mumukṣibhiḥ yam eva eṣaḥ iti śrutyā tam eva iti ca sa ādaram śāstra yoni tvam asya eva jñāyate veda vādibhiḥ 
AVy_3,3.19–3,3.22	 yaḥ enam viduḥ a mṛtā iti uktaḥ tu samudra gaḥ tat eva brahma paramam iti śrutyā avadhāritaḥ yatas prasūtā iti tatas sṛṣṭim āha tatas hariḥ śāstra yoniḥ naca anyaḥ asti mukhyatas tu iti gamyate śāstra yoni tvam etasya jñāyate hi samanvayāt samiti hi upasargeṇa para mukhyāthaṛtā ucyate evam parama mukhya arthaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti śruteḥ nirdhāraṇāya na aśabdam iti veda patiḥ jagau 
AVy_3,3.23–3,3.25	 katham samanvayaḥ jñeyaḥ su alpa śākhā vidām nṛṇām vedāḥ hi anantāḥ iti hi śrutirāha api anantatām ananta veda nirṇītiḥ mahā praaya vāridheḥ uttāraṇa upamā iti asmān na jñeyaḥ atra samanvayaḥ iti śaṅkā apanoda artham saḥ āha karuṇā karaḥ aśakya uttaraṇa tve api hi āgama apāra vāridheḥ nirṇīyate mayā eva ayam romakūpalaya udinā 
AVy_3,3.26–3,3.29	 yadi api aśeṣa veda arthaḥ durgamaḥ akhila mānavaiḥ mad jñāna avyākṛta ākāśe prāpnoti parama aṇu tām iti prakāśayan viśvapatiḥ āha prameya tām nikhilasya api vedasya gati sāmānyam añjasā kaḥ nāma gati sāmānyam ananta āgama sampadaḥ jñāna sūryam ṛte brūyāt tam ekam bādarāyaṇam anyaḥ api alpa matiḥ śākhā catuṣpañca gatam vasu jānanna anumita tvena brūyāt tasya prasādataḥ 
AVy_3,3.30–3,3.33	 iti mukhya tayā aśeṣa gati sāmānya vid prabhuḥ pratijajñe dṛḍham yasmāt devānām api pūryate atas nikhila vedānām siddhaḥ evam samanvayaḥ iti su jñāpita arthaḥ api pṛthak ca āha samanvayam tatra prathamatas anyatra prasiddhānām samanvayaḥ śabdānām vācyaḥ eva atra mahā malleśa bhaṅga vat itas ati abhyadhika tve api turya pāda uditasya tu mahā samanvaye tasmin na adhikāraḥ akhilasya hi 
AVy_3,3.34–3,3.36	 brahma eva adhikṛtaḥ tatra mukhyatas anye yathākramam durgama tvāt ca na eva atra prāthamyena uditaḥ añjasā atas anyatra prasiddhānām śabdānām nirṇayāya tu pravṛttaḥ prathamam devaḥ tatra ānanda ādayaḥ guṇāḥ īśasya eva iti nirṇītāḥ śruti yukti samāśrayāt devatā antara gāḥ sarve śabda vṛtti nimittataḥ viṣṇum eva vadanti addhā tad saṅgāt upacārataḥ 
AVy_3,3.37–3,3.40	 anya devān vadanti iha viśeṣa guṇa vaktṛtaḥ viṣṇum eva param brūyuḥ evam anye api aśeṣatas iti anyatra prasiddha ūru śabda rāśeḥ aśeṣatas jñāte samanvaye viṣṇau liṅgaiḥ hi eṣa samanvayaḥ teṣām anya gata tve tu na syāt samyak samanvayaḥ iti eva aśeṣa liṅgānām brahmaṇi eva samanvayam āha ubhaya gata tvam ca syāt atas liṅga śabdayoḥ iti saṃśaya nutti artham ubhayatra pratītitaḥ 
AVy_3,3.41–3,3.44	 śabdānām vartamānānām sa liṅgānām viśeṣataḥ samanvayaḥ harau= eva yat na eva anyatra mukhyatas śabdāḥ liṅgāni ca yatas na eva anyatra svatantra tā asvatantreṣu śabdasya vṛtti hetuḥ na mukhyatas yatas atas yat adhīnāḥ te śabda artha tvam upāgatāḥ ati alpena eva śabdasya vṛtti hetu guṇena tu ayaḥ yathā dāhaka tvam saḥ eva īśaḥ svatantrataḥ mukhya śabda arthaḥ iti hi svīkartavyaḥ manīṣibhiḥ 
AVy_3,3.45–3,3.48	 iti āha evañca śabdānām nārāyaṇa samanvaye siddhe api aśeṣa śabdānām na kathañcana yujyate virodhau= avara tva ādeḥ api prāptiḥ yatas bhavet iti ced avara tva ādi dvividham hi upalabhyate parasya āvarata ahetuḥ yaḥ svayam paraḥ eva san saḥ api hi avara śabda arthaḥ yathā rājā jayī bhavet anyaḥ avaratvā anubhavī tayoḥ pūrvaḥ asti keśave dvitīyaḥ jīvaḥ eva asti svātantrān na ca dūṣaṇam 
AVy_3,3.49–3,3.51	 hareḥ evam aśeṣeṇa sarva śabda samanvaye ukte virodha hīnasya syāt samanvayatā yatas atas aśeṣa virodhānām kṛta īśena nirākṛtiḥ samanvaya avirodhābhyām san jāte vastu nirṇaye kim mayā kāryam iti eva syāt buddhiḥ adhikāriṇaḥ tatra bhakti vidhāna artham abhakta anartha santatau uktāyām bhakti dārḍhyāya prokte aśeṣa guṇa uccaye vaktavya upāsanāḥ nityam kartavyā iti ādareṇa hi 
AVy_3,3.52–3,3.55	 sa upāsanā ca dvividhā śāstra abhyāsa svarūpiṇī dhyāna rūpā parā ca eva tad aṅgam dhāraṇa ādikam tathā ubhaya ātmakam ca eva pāde asmin bādarāyaṇaḥ āha upāsana m addhava vistarāt śruti pūrvakam pṛthak dṛṣṭiḥ aśakya tvam anirṇītiḥ samuccayaḥ viśeṣa darśanam kārya lopaḥ nānā uktiḥ āśu tā vibhramaḥ apākṛtiḥ liṅgam anavasthā viśeṣitā aprayojana tā ca atiprasaṅgaḥ adūra saṃśrayaḥ 
AVy_3,3.56–3,3.59	 viśiṣṭa kāraṇam ca iṣyā dṛṣṭa vairūpyam unnatiḥ anuktiḥ aprayatna tvam dṛḍha bandha parābhavau puṃsāmyam prāpta santyāgaḥ kāraṇa anirṇayaḥ bhramaḥ viśeṣa darśitā alāpaḥ guṇa sāmyam pṛthak dṛśiḥ agamyavartma sandhānam iṣṭam phalam akalpanā śuddha vairūpyam aṅga tvam aviśeṣa dṛśiḥ kriyā yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣa sthāḥ su jñeya tvam vidhi kriyā māhātmyam alpa śakti tvam yathāyogya phalam bhavaḥ 
AVy_3,3.60–3,3.63	 phala sāmyam viśeṣaḥ ca guṇa ādhikyam pradhāna tā yathāśakti kriyā sandhiḥ pramāṇa balam ānatiḥ kāraṇam kārya vaiśeṣyam svabhāvaḥ vastu dūṣaṇam pratikriyā virodhaḥ ca pratisandhiḥ anūna tā saṃskāra pāṭavam sva icchā niyatiḥ vastu vaibhavam viśeṣa uktiramāna tvam prādhānyam prītiḥ āgamaḥ su sthira tvam kṛta prāptiḥ anādi guṇa vistaraḥ sādhana uttamatā nānā dṛṣṭiḥ śiṣṭiḥ anūna tā 
AVy_3,3.64–3,3.67	 avighna tva virodhau ca guṇa vaiśeṣyam āgamaḥ siddhānta nirṇaye hi etāḥ yuktayaḥ avyāhatāḥ sadā yathāśaktayakhilān vedān vijñāya upāsanam bhavet tatra akhilasya vijñaptiḥ samyak brahmaṇaḥ eva hi tad anyeṣām yathāyogyam akhila jñaptiḥ iṣyate tāvatā upāsane yogyaḥ bhavet eva akhilaḥ pumān mahat tvasya param pāram viditvā eva janārdanaḥ stoṣya tām eti tuṣṭa tvam iti na asti eva nārada 
AVy_3,3.68–3,3.71	 kintu niścalayā bhaktayā hi ātma jñāna anurūpataḥ yaḥ stoṣyati sadā bhaktaḥ tuṣyaḥ tasya sadā hariḥ ityādi vākya sandarbhāt yathāyogya akhila jña tā ātma jñāna anurūpa tvam yathāśakti vicāraṇāt vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ adhigantavyaḥ svādhyāya adhyayanam bhavet ityādi vākya vaiyarthyam anyathā na nivāryate adya api tena deva ādyāḥ śṛṇvate manvate sadā dhyāyanti ca yathāyogam tathā apyāḥ vastu nirṇayāt śravaṇam mananam ca eva kartavyam sarvathā eva hi 
AVy_3,3.72–3,3.75	 mati śruti dhyāna kāla viśeṣam guruḥ uttamaḥ vetti tasya ukti mārgeṇa kurvataḥ syāt hi darśanam śravaṇam dṛṣṭa tattvasya mananam dhyānam eva ca viśeṣa ānanda samprāptyā anyasya etāni dṛṣṭaye yadi tādṛś guruḥ na asti nirṇīta śravaṇa ādikam tad siddhānta anusāreṇa nirṇaya jñāt samācaret śravaṇa ādi vinā na eva kṣaṇam tiṣṭhet api kvacid atyaśakye tu nidrā ādau punar eva samārabhet 
AVy_3,3.76–3,3.79	 abhāve nirṇaya jñasya sat śāstrāṇi eva sarvadā śṛṇuyāt yadi sat jñāna prācuryam upalabhyate mahat bhayaḥ viṣṇu bhaktebhyaḥ yathāśakti ca saṃśayān chindyāt svatas adhika abhāve svayam eva samabhyaset aśeṣa guṇa pūrṇa tvam sarva doṣa samujkhitiḥ viṣṇoḥ anyat ca tat tantram iti samyak vinirṇayaḥ svatantra tvam sadā tasya tasya bhedaḥ ca sarvatas adoṣa tvasya siddhayartham yat abhede tad anvayaḥ 
AVy_3,3.80–3,3.82	 tat tantra tvam ca muktānām api tad guṇa pūrtaye muktānām api bhedaḥ ca na hi bhinnam abhinna tām gacchat dṛṣṭam kvacid tasya api abhāvaḥ anubhava upagaḥ pūrva abhede doṣavat tvam īśasya iti ati bhinna tā nārāyaṇena muktānām api samyak iti sthitiḥ bheda abhede api abhedena doṣāṇām api sambhavaḥ nirdoṣa tvam ramāyāḥ ca tad anantara tā tathā 
AVy_3,3.83–3,3.86	 brahmā sarasvatī vi indra śeṣa rudrāḥ ca tad sriyaḥ śakra kāmau tad anye ca kramāt muktau= api iti ca sat siddhāntaḥ iti jñeyaḥ nirṇītaḥ hariṇā svayam etat virodhi yat sarvam tamase andhāya kevalam andham tamaḥ viśanti iti prāha śruti ḥ ati sphuṭam iti eva śrutayaḥ aśeṣāḥ pañca rātram atha akhilam mūla rāmāyaṇam ca eva bhāratam smṛtayaḥ akhilāḥ vaiṣṇavāni purāṇāni sāṅkhaya yogau parau= api 
AVy_3,3.87–3,3.90	 brahmatarkaḥ ca mīmāṃsā iti anantaḥ śabda sāgaraḥ anantara yuktayaḥ ca eva pratyakṣa āgama mūlakāḥ pratyakṣam aiśvaram ca eva rama ādīnām aśeṣatas muktānām api amuktānām etam eva artham uttamam anya avakāśa rahitam prakāśayati sādaram etat eva ca sat śāstram duḥśāstram tu tatas param sat śāstram abhyaset nityam duḥśāstram ca parityajet asaṃśayena tattvasya nirṇaye brahma darśanam 
AVy_3,3.91–3,3.94	 samyak viṣama vijñāna tāratamya anusārataḥ phalam bhavet tāratamyāt sukha duḥkha ātmakam nṛṇām samyak ca adhika vijñānāt sukha ādhikyam bhavet nṛṇām atas yathā ātma śaktayā eva śravaṇam mananam tathā viṣayeṣu ca saṃsargāt śāśvatasya ca saṃśayāt manasā ca anyat ākāṅkṣāt param na pratipādyate iti bhārata vākyam hi tena etad doṣa varjitaḥ sadā upāsanayā yuktaḥ vāsudevam prapaśyati 
AVy_3,3.95–3,3.97	 doṣāḥ anādi sambaddhāḥ te mukti paripanthinaḥ santi eva prāyaśas puṃsu tena mokṣaḥ na jāyate sarve te ete jīveṣu dṛśyante tāratamyataḥ ṛjūnām ekaḥ eva asti parama utsāha varjanam sa guṇa alpa tva mātra tvāt narja tvena viruddhayate atas viṣṇau parā bhaktiḥ tad bhakteṣu rama ādiṣu tāratamyena kartavyā puruṣa artham abhīpsitā 
AVy_3,3.98–3,3.101	 svādaraḥ sarva jantūnām saṃsiddhaḥ hi svabhāvataḥ tatas adhikaḥ sva uttameṣu tad ādhikya anusārataḥ kartavyaḥ vāsudeva antam sarvathā śubham icchatā na kadācid tyajet tam ca krameṇa enam vivardhayet sameṣu sva ātma vat snehaḥ satsu anyatra tatas dayā kāryā evam āparokṣyeṇa dṛśyate kṣipram īśvaraḥ tat tamaḥ andham vrajet viṣṇu sama tvam yaḥ anupaśyati ramā brahma śiva ādīnām api muktau kathañcana 
AVy_3,3.102–3,3.104	 kim uta ādhikya dṛṣṭeḥ tat guṇa abhāva mateḥ api doṣa vettuḥ abhedasya draṣṭuḥ draṣṭuḥ tathā ubhayoḥ iti āha sat śrutiḥ tena samprokta guṇa saṃyutam upāsīta harim dṛṣṭvā muktiḥ tena eva jāyate dveṣāt yat mukti kathanam śruti vākya virodhi yat ripavaḥ ye tu rāmasya vimukha tvāt nirāmiṇaḥ abhidroha pade nityam andhe tamasi te sthitāḥ 
AVy_3,3.105–3,3.107	 haridviṣaḥ tamaḥ yānti ye ca eva tad abhedinaḥ tat nirguṇa tva vettāraḥ tasya doṣa vidaḥ api ca ityādi śruti sandarbhāt dveṣiṇaḥ tamaḥ īyate hiraṇyakaśipuḥ ca api bhagavat nindayā tamaḥ vidhi kṣuḥ ati agāt sūno prahlādasya anubhāvataḥ yat anindat pitā mahyam tvad bhakte mayi ca āghavān tasmāt pitā me pūyeta durantāt dustarāt aghāt 
AVy_3,3.108–3,3.111	 nindām bhagavataḥ śṛṇvan= tatparasya janasya vā tatas na apaiti yaḥ saḥ api yāti aghaḥ sukṛtāt cyutaḥ avajānanti mām mūḍhāḥ mānuṣīm tanum āśritam param bhāvam ajānantaḥ mama bhūta maheśvaram mogha āśāḥ mogha karmāṇaḥ mogha jñānāḥ vicetasaḥ rākṣasīm āsurīm ca eva prakṛtim mohanīm śritāḥ mām ātma para deheṣu pradviṣantaḥ abhyasūyakāḥ tān aham dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu nara adhamān kṣipāmi ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu 
AVy_3,3.112–3,3.114	 āsurīm yonim āpannāḥ mūḍhāḥ janmani janmani mām aprāpya eva kaunteya tatas yānti adhamām gatim yaḥ dviṣṭāt vibudha śreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam prabhum katham sa na bhavet dveṣyaḥ āloka antasya kasyacid yaḥ dviṣṭāt vibudha śreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam prabhum majjanti pitaraḥ tasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ityādi vākya sandohāt dveṣiṇaḥ tamaḥ eva tu 
AVy_3,3.115–3,3.118	 na eva mokṣaḥ iti prāhuḥ lokāyata mate sthitāḥ bhogaḥ śarīra paryantam bhasmībhāvaḥ tatas bhavet iti tat kena mānena dṛṣṭam pratyakṣa vādinā na hi pratyakṣa mānena mokṣa abhāvaḥ avasīyate ghaṭate mukti dṛṣṭiḥ tu puruṣeṇa mahīyasā na iti vaktuḥ mahat tvam tu kathañcana na vidyate sādhayan sarva sāmānyam katham eva viśeṣavān dṛśyante puruṣāḥ loke parāvara vidaḥ api ca 
AVy_3,3.119–3,3.122	 aparokṣa dṛśaḥ yoga niṣṭhāḥ ca amala cakṣuṣaḥ pratyakṣam devatām dṛṣṭvā tad prasāda āpta bhūtayaḥ jñāna vijñāna pāra jñāḥ niṣiddhayante katham nṛbhiḥ dṛśyate ca ati māhātmyam teṣām ati mahā ojasām yadi te api niṣiddhayante kim na uktiḥ te niṣiddhayate yat ukta vākya prāmāṇyam pratyakṣeṇa upalabhyate vara ādayaḥ api tad dattāḥ sadā satyāḥ bhavanti hi aprāmāṇyam tat ukteḥ ca vṛthā vācā vasīyate 
AVy_3,3.123–3,3.125	 na hi prayojanam kiñcid para loka nivāraṇāt vṛthā vācam vṛthā hanyāt yadi tasya kim uttaram sva jīvana virodhāya vadan kim nāma buddhimān prāmāṇye saṃśayaḥ kim syāt tayoḥ puruṣayoḥ api sva jīvana viruddha ukti rajñaḥ dṛṣṭasya ca api saḥ yaḥ ca atīndriya deva ukti śrotāḥ dṛṣṭa parāvaraḥ atīta anāgatam sarvam lokānubhavam āpayan atas pratyakṣa gamya tvāt vedamātvasya ca sphuṭam 
AVy_3,3.126–3,3.128	 yadi āgamasya naḥ mātvam akṣajasya tathā bhavet yadi akṣa jasya mātvam syāt āgamasya katham na tat loka vākyāt viśeṣaḥ ca avyabhicāreṇa siddhayati asti mokṣaḥ api dharmeṇa yathā artha jñānataḥ api ca prāmāṇyam anumāyāḥ ca jinasya āptatva sādhane tad vākyāt dharma sat jñāna vijñaptiḥ bhavati iti ca dharmaḥ ahiṃsā paraḥ na anyaḥ jñānam pudgala darśanam 
AVy_3,3.129–3,3.131	 iti jaināḥ katham tat syāt pramāṇam anumānataḥ viṣayān prati sthitam hi akṣam pratyakṣam iti gīyate pratyakṣa śabda anusārāt anumā iti prakītiḥ tāḥ ā samantāt gamayati dharma adharmau param padam yat ca api atīndriyam tu anyat tena asau= āgamaḥ smṛtaḥ etena kāreṇena eva tat tad māna tvam iṣyate svarūpam hi tat eteṣām anyathā siddhi mānataḥ 
AVy_3,3.132–3,3.134	 atas anumā katham dharmam pudgalam ca api darśayet svarūpam pudgalasya uktāḥ doṣāḥ ānandam eva ca na manyate pudgalam sa duḥkha abhāvaḥ sukham tu iti mātrā bhoga atirekeṇa sukha ādhikyasya darśanāt sukhasya abhāva tā kena na ca syāt kim viparyayaḥ yadi bhāvaḥ api kaścid syāt tasya eva abhāva tā kutas yadi sarve api abhāvāḥ syuḥ anyonyam iti bhāvatā 
AVy_3,3.135–3,3.138	 abhāva abhāva tā yat syāt kim naḥ chinnam tadā bhavet bhāva tvam vidhi rūpa tvam niṣedha tvam abhāvatā niṣedhasya niṣedhaḥ api bhāvaḥ eva balāt bhavet prathama pratipattiḥ tu bhāva bhāva niyāmikā na ca pudgala vijñānam mokṣa dam bhavati kvacid asvātantryāt pudgalasya jñātaḥ api sukha daḥ na hi na hi duḥkhi parijñānāt duḥkhi tvam vinivartate yadi pudgala vijñānāt aduḥkhī syāt kathañcana dehavān api na aduḥkhī kim jñānāt uttaram sadā 
AVy_3,3.139–3,3.142	 īśa kpti anusāreṇa syāt kālādi īśa vādinaḥ karma hetu tvam api tu niścaitanyāt na hi kvacid aśeṣa duḥkha vilaye na idānīm kāraṇam yathā tathā uttaram ca na eva syāt dṛṣṭi pūrva anumā yatas śaktasya anyasya vijñānam tat prīti janakam yadi tayā eva bandha hāniḥ syāt iti kim nāma dūṣaṇam sva jñānāt bandha hāniḥ tu dṛśyate kasya kutracid ahiṃsāyāḥ ca dharma tvam kena mānena gamyate hiṃsāyāḥ eva dharma tvam iti ukte syāt kim uttaram 
AVy_3,3.143–3,3.146	 dharmasya sukha hetu tvam api kena avagamyate hatyayā mokṣa hetu tvam kutas mānāt nivāryate na ca śūnya parijñānāt śūnya bhāvanayā api ca mokṣaḥ kathañcana bhavet yadi idānīm katham na saḥ para prasādana icchoḥ tu viambaḥ nāma yujyate pum icchā adhīna tā no ced viambaḥ kiṅkṛtaḥ bhavet anyatra api viambāḥ tu syuḥ īśa icchā nimittataḥ anyathā kāraṇam ced syāt kim kāryam na upajāyate kāraṇe sati kāryasya bhāvaḥ su niyataḥ asya hi 
AVy_3,3.147–3,3.150	 vijñāna vādinaḥ ca eva vijñāna advaita vedanāt vijñāna bhāvanāt ca eva mokṣaḥ na ghaṭate kvacid antar jñānasya bāhye ca kṣaṇika tvasya vedanāt bhāvanāt ca ukta mārgeṇa māna abhāvāt na mucyate prakṛteḥ puruṣasya api vivekaḥ mukti sādhanam iti śaṅkayā na ca etasmin mānam īśa aprasādataḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ca eva yadi īśasya prasādataḥ vadanti niyamāt muktim tam ṛte atas kutas bhavet 
AVy_3,3.151–3,3.153	 kaṇāda yoga akṣa pādāḥ api īśasya prasādataḥ muktim bruvāṇāḥ api āhuḥ bhogāt eva ca karmaṇām kṣayam prāhuḥ kutas ca etat prasanne jagat īśvare bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi dṛṣṭaḥ eva ātmani īśvare iti śruti purāṇa ādi vacanebhyaḥ anyathāgateḥ 
AVy_3,3.154–3,3.157	 na ca pāśupatādyukta śiva ādīnām anugrahāt na anyaḥ panthāḥ iti hi uktam puruṣa jñānataḥ śrutau sarve nimeṣāḥ jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣāt atas evam puruṣa śabdaḥ ca prayuktaḥ abdhiśaye harau na tasya īśe kaścana tasya nāma mahat yaśaḥ iti ca adhipatiḥ tasya pratiṣiddhaḥ svayam śrutau viśvatas paramām nityam viśvam nārāyaṇam harim iti sarva adhika tva uktayā samaḥ api vinivāritaḥ samādhikasya rāhityāt na upacāra pumān asau 
AVy_3,3.158–3,3.161	 puruṣaḥ eva idam sarvam yat bhūtam yat ca bhavyam uta amṛta tvasya īśānaḥ yat annena atirohati muktā mukta para īśa tvam iti tasya āha sā śrutiḥ amṛta īśāna vacanāt sarvasya īśāna toditā yadi sarva tvam udita muta īśaḥ iti tat vṛthā uta śabdaḥ vadet eṣa hi īśa tvasya samuccayam puruṣeṇa idam vyāptam iti brāhmaṇam ca āha tam prati etāvān asya mahimā iti mahimnaḥ vacaḥ hi tat 
AVy_3,3.162–3,3.164	 saḥ amṛtasya abhayasya īśaḥ martyam annam yat atyagāt iti amukta ādhipatyam tu pūrva ardha uktam anūdya ca uta amṛtasya īśaḥ iti vidhatte mukti geśa tām atas viṣṇu parijñānāt eva muktiḥ naca anyatas tat yathā iti śruteḥ ca eva tatas karma kṣayaḥ bhavet yathā edhāṃsi samiddhaḥ agniḥ bhasmasāt kurute arjunaḥ jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā 
AVy_3,3.165–3,3.167	 sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ ityādi bhagavat vākyaiḥ ukta arthaḥ ca avasīyate nitya naimittikam karma kurvan= anyat parityajan mucyate saṃsṛteḥ ca etat api etena nirākṛtam vidyā eva iti imam eva artham svayam eva āha veda rāj vinā karma na mokṣaḥ syāt jñānena iti api sā śrutiḥ na anyaḥ panthāḥ iti hi eva nivārayati sa ādaram 
AVy_3,3.168–3,3.170	 anyathā upāsanam api tam evam iti vādinī nivārayati ādareṇa na pratīkaḥ iti prabhuḥ andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye avidyām upāsate iti śruti virodhāt ca na anyathā upāsanam bhavet na ca api eka tva vijñānāt ukta nyāyena mucyate iti sarvam pravijñāya sarvaiḥ tarka sat āgamaiḥ upāsīta harim nityam guṇaiḥ eva sva yogataḥ 
AVy_3,3.171–3,3.174	 brahmā sarvai guṇaiḥ ca eva kriyā sāmānyataḥ ca gīḥ guṇa sāmānyatas rudraḥ dravya sāmānyatas pare adhikāra viśeṣeṇa bhakti jñāna sukha ādibhiḥ viśeṣaḥ devatā ādīnām mokṣe ca eva viśeṣataḥ na tāvatā virodhaḥ asti nirdoṣa tvāt samastaśas ābhāsa tvāt pareṣām tad avarāṇām ca sarvaśas yatas avarāṇām sarve api guṇāḥ sarvāḥ kriyāḥ api niyamena eva pūrveṣām su prasāda nibandhanāḥ atas sat śiṣya vat teṣām na eva īrṣyādiḥ kathañcana 
AVy_3,3.175–3,3.177	 na ca saṃsāri devānām kāleyatta apare ime sūtre hi ārabdha mātrasya bhogena eva kṣayaḥ dhruvaḥ anārabdha kārye bhogena tu itare iti coditaḥ paunaruktayena tena ete ukta arthe iti niścayaḥ uṣāḥ svāhā ca parjanyaḥ mitraḥ agniḥ varuṇaḥ vidhuḥ pravahaḥ aniruddhaḥ indrome rudraḥ vāṇī ca mārutaḥ uttarottarataḥ tu ete guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ ca mukti gāḥ 
AVy_3,3.178–3,3.181	 sūrya dharmau yathā somaḥ manuḥ dakṣaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ śacī ratiḥ ca aniruddha samāḥ tārā ca mitra vat somavat śata rūpā tu prasūtiḥ vahni vat virāj parjanya vat vāruṇī ca tathā sañjñā ca rohiṇī dharmī ca mitravat tvena prāvahī parikīrtitā mitra pajarnya madhya sthau= aśvinau vighna vid tapau bhṛguḥ agni samaḥ mitra tad madhye brahma putrakāḥ varuṇa agni antarā tatra nāradaḥ prāyas indra vat 
AVy_3,3.182–3,3.184	 kāmaḥ suparṇī ca umā vat vi indraḥ rudra vat īritaḥ niṛtiḥ mitra sadṛśaḥ viśvāmitraḥ kasūnu vat vaivasvataḥ manuḥ ca aśvi paścāt anye tatas avarāḥ cyavanocathya vainyāḥ ca śaśabinduḥ ca haihayaḥ tadvat ca vipra rājanya viśeṣaḥ atra api kaścana tadvat priyavrataḥ ca api tad anyāḥ śata devatāḥ pajarnī amitra antarāe tad anye tu tatas avarāḥ 
AVy_3,3.185–3,3.187	 etebhyaḥ abhyadhikā śrīḥ astu sadā muktāḥ viśeṣataḥ tad samaḥ na asti paramaḥ hariḥ eva naca aparaḥ saṃhitāyām bṛhatyām tu svayam bhagavatā uditam tat etat akhilam prāṇaḥ āhaṅkārikaḥ eva ca indrāt anantaraḥ dṛṣṭiḥ api yogyā anusārataḥ samyak guru prasādaḥ ca mukhyatas dṛṣṭi kāraṇam śravaṇa ādi ca kartavyam na anyathā darśanam kvacid 
AVy_3,3.188–3,3.193	 guṇa adhikam gurum prāpya tat hīnam na āpnuyāt kvacid viparyayaḥ tu kartavyaḥ sarvathā muktim icchatā same vikalpaḥ eva syāt pūrva anujñā ca sarvathā tat uttama guru prāptyai pūrva anujñā na mṛgyate guru barrahma akhilānām ca vidyā ca eva sarasvatī devatāḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarveṣām aviśeṣatas tad prasādena muktiḥ syāt na anyathā tu kathañcana sva uttamāḥ tu krameṇa eva sarveṣām guravaḥ śrutāḥ upadeśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tu sarveṣām eva muktaye sādhanebhyaḥ adhikā bhaktiḥ na eva anyat tādṛśam kvacid bhaktiḥ ca eva harau= eva mukhyāni atra yathākramam sva adhikā tu eva sarvatra sva uttameṣu krameṇa ca anuvartate ca sā bhaktiḥ muktau= ānanda rūpiṇī tad pūrva ka upāsana evam kartavyāḥ muktaye guṇaiḥ 
AVy_3,4.1–3,4.4	 evam utpanna nirdoṣa bhagavat darśanāt sadā apekṣita phala prāptiḥ ārabdhasya anatikramāt deva ṛṣi mānuṣa ādīnām tat tad jāti anusārataḥ jaimini uktam mānuṣāṇām tad viśeṣāḥ ca kecana sāmānyam bhagavat proktam deva ādīnām viśeṣataḥ balavat virodhi sadbhāve jaiminyāt yuktiḥ iṣyate vikarma lepaḥ na eva asti samyak dṛṣṭimatām kvacid guṇa hāniḥ ca na eva asti brahmaṇaḥ tu avikarmataḥ 
AVy_3,4.5–3,4.7	 devānām api na prāyas kptasya tu kathañcana prāpta hrāsaḥ bhavet kvāpi mahatā tu vikarmaṇā tathā api tat kptam eva tasmāt na niyama ujkhitiḥ candra sugrīvayoḥ ca eva sva ucca dāra parigrahāt prāpta hāniḥ abhūt na eva kpta hāniḥ yathañcanaḥ hrāsaḥ api mānuṣa ādīnām ānandasya vikarmaṇā bhavet muktau viśeṣeṇa sva uccānām aparādhataḥ 
AVy_3,4.8–3,4.10	 jñāna uttarasya pāpasya caturthe alepaḥ ucyate aśuci tva ādikam tasya na bhavet iti tad phalam atra jñāna phalasya eva mukteḥ niyata tā ucyate prārabdha karma jasya eva viṣa bhakṣāt mṛteḥ iva prāptasya api anivartyasya kiñcid bhuktasya saṃvidā upamardaḥ iha proktaḥ deva ādīnām yathākramam sarva ātmanā tu abhogaḥ hi prārabdhasya eva karmaṇaḥ na brahma darśinaḥ api syāt phala hrāsaḥ tu vidyate 
AVy_3,4.11–3,4.13	 sarva ātmanā phala hrāsaḥ yadi na ārabdha karmaṇaḥ syāt kāmya vidhi vaiyarthyam iti ukta niyamaḥ bhavet evam adya api samproktam tantra bhāgavate sphuṭam tāratamyam phale no ced brahma ādīnām katham śrutiḥ avṛjinaḥ akāma hataḥ iti muktim nigadya ca ānanda tāratamyam ca teṣām brūyāt pṛthak pṛthak saṃsāraḥ eva ced etat tāratamyam na mukhyatas akāma hata śabda arthaḥ avṛjina tvam ca naḥ bhavet 
AVy_3,4.14–3,4.16	 kāmasya yatra āptāḥ kāmāḥ tatra mām amṛtam kṛdhi iti yat lakṣaṇam mukteḥ śrutiḥ āha balīyasī kāma āhatiḥ kutas anyatra prāpta kāmasya sā bhavet aprayatnena kāmānām avāptiḥ sā yadā bhavet tadā eva akāma hatatā kutas eva anyathā bhavet cetanasya tu asuptasya kutra dṛṣṭā hi akāma tā avyaktiḥ eva kāmānām na nāśaḥ moha suptayoḥ 
AVy_3,4.17–3,4.20	 yad kāmaḥ svāpam āpnoti tat eva utthāpitaḥ kutas avaśaḥ api vyāharati kutas supta avakāma tā sarva kāmān avāpnoti brahmaṇā saha mukti gaḥ paryeti tatra jakṣan= ca krīḍan ratim avāpnuvan kāmānnī kāmarūpī san= imān lokān= ca sañcaran āste gāyan sāma muktaḥ iti ādi śruti sat balāt akāmaḥ syāt katham muktaḥ kāmāḥ ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ iti antaḥkaraṇa sthānām kāmānām mokṣam eva hi āha śrutiḥ hṛdi iti eva na ced vyartham viśeṣaṇam 
AVy_3,4.21–3,4.24	 hṛdi eṣa teṣām śrayaṇam iti pakṣaḥ na bhāsate muktānām kāmitām āha pṛthak śākhāsu yat śrutiḥ atas akāma hata tvam tu muktānām eva mukhyatas mukhya arthasya vṛthā tyāgaḥ māyinām eva bhūṣaṇam apāpa tvam aduḥkha tvam ca āvṛjina tvam iha uditam apriyam vṛjinam duḥkhamakam todaḥ iti iya ṛte tad kāraṇa tvāt pāpam vā vṛjinam nāma kathyate iti uktaḥ svayam īśena nāma arthaḥ śabda nirṇaye 
AVy_3,4.25–3,4.28	 apāpa tvam ca na eva asti yāvat saṃsāram asya hi ārabdha pāpam asti eva duḥkham ca jñāninaḥ api hi tasmāt tasmāt akāma tvam iti ca aśruta kalpanā akāma hataḥ iti ukteḥ śruta hāniḥ api sphuṭāḥ kutracid kāminaḥ puṃsaḥ kāma abhāvāt kvacid kvacid indra ādi sukha bhogaḥ asti iti anubhūtiḥ hi kupyati tasmāt amukta sukha gam tāratamyam pṛthak pṛthak uktvā yaḥ ca iti muktānām tāratamyam sukhe śrutiḥ āha iti peśalam tat ca caśabdāt eva gamyate 
AVy_3,4.29–3,4.32	 rāddhaḥ saṃsiddhaḥ iti eva muktaḥ eva avagamyate sādhunā viṣṇunā yuktaḥ muktaḥ sādhu yuvā mataḥ yauvanam nityam etasya muktasya iti yuvā sa ca phalam adhyayanasya āptam tena adhyāyakaḥ īritaḥ nirhrāsa ānanda samprāptyā ca āśiṣṭaḥ iti gīyate sthitasya ananyathā prāpteḥ dṛḍhiṣṭhaḥ iti coditaḥ baliṣṭhaḥ ca svabhāvena muktaḥ bhavati kevalam tasya iyam pṛthivī ityādi pūrva bhāva vyapekṣayā 
AVy_3,4.33–3,4.36	 saḥ ekaḥ iti saṃsāra gata muktavā sukham punar śrotriyasya iti vadati muktāt śataguṇa ātma tām saṃsāra gāt ca saṃsāra gatasya eva śata adhikam muktān muktasya yuktam syāt śruti uktam abhivīkṣitaḥ yuktam ca sādhana ādhikyāt sādhya ādhikyam sura ādiṣu na ādhikyam yadi sādhye syāt prayatnaḥ sādhane kutas yatnaḥ ca dṛśyate teṣām mahān eva mahātmanām yatra sādhana bāhulyam sādhya bāhulyam atra ca dṛṣṭam niyamataḥ no ced na yatnam kurya rañjasā 
AVy_3,4.37–3,4.39	 kṛcchreṇa sādhanāt eva na mukta vat udīryate daśa kalpam tapaḥ cīrṇam rudreṇa lavaṇa arṇave tyaktavā sukhāni sarvāṇi kliṣṭena lavaṇa ambhasā śakreṇa varṣakoṭiḥ ca dhūmaḥ pītaḥ ati duḥkhataḥ varṣa ayutam ca sūryeṇa tapaḥ avākchirasā kṛtam su duḥkhena sukham tyaktavā dharmeṇa ākāśa śāyinā pītā mayīcayaḥ varṣa sāhasram ati sādaram 
AVy_3,4.40–3,4.42	 atikṛcchreṇa kurvanti yatnam brahma vidaḥ api hi iti etat akhilam mokṣa viśeṣa abhāvataḥ katham daivī sampad vimokṣāya nibandhāya āsurī matā iti mokṣa viśeṣaḥ ca svayam bhagavatā uditaḥ tam eva yūyam bhajata ātma vṛttibhiḥ manaḥ vacaḥ kāya guṇaiḥ sva karmabhiḥ amāyinaḥ kāmadughā aṅghri paṅkajam yathā adhikāra avasita artha siddhaye 
AVy_3,4.43–3,4.45	 akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyaḥ manojaveṣu asamāḥ babhūvuḥ ādaghnāsaḥ upakakṣāsaḥ u tve hradāḥ iva snātvā u tve dadṛśre ityādīni ca vākyāni tāratamyam vimukti gam vyaktam vadanti tat kena sāmyam mukteṣu gamyate duḥkha ādi a bhāva sāmyam ca sāmya vākya arthaḥ īyate bhaktayā ādi guṇa sadbhāve hi atulya tvam ca bhārate uktam sādhana vaiśeṣyam api sarvatra kathyate 
AVy_3,4.46–3,4.49	 durjñeyam ghora rūpasya trailokya dhvaṃsinaḥ prabhoḥ daivataiḥ munibhiḥ siddhaiḥ mahā yogibhiḥ eva ca nitya yuktaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ vimukta kleśa sādhvasaiḥ mahā utsāhaiḥ mahā dhairyaiḥ sattva sthaiḥ vyavasāyibhiḥ atīta anāgata jñāna prabhava apyaya vedibhiḥ śauca svādhyāya santoṣa tapassatya dayā anvitaiḥ kimu martyaiḥ bhaya bhrānti dhvaṃsa moha rujā anvitaiḥ alpa āyuḥ vīrya dhī sattva vyavasāya śruti vrataiḥ 
AVy_3,4.50–3,4.53	 kaḥ tam madāmadam devam mad anyaḥ jñātum arhati brahma eva kiñcid jānāti na tad anyaḥ hi kaścana muktānām api siddhānām nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ su durlabhaḥ praśānta ātmā koṭiṣu api mahāmate iyam visṛṣṭiḥ yatas ā babhūva yadi vā dadhe yadi vā na yaḥ asya adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman tsaḥ aṅga veda yadi vā na veda yaḥ sva ātma māyā vibhavam svayam gataḥ na aham nabhasvān= tam atha apare kutas brahmā api yam vetti na eva iha samyak anye kutas deva muni indra martyāḥ 
AVy_3,4.54–3,4.56	 namaḥ te amita tattvāya dharma ādīnām ca sūtaye nirguṇāya ca sat kāṣṭhām na aham veda apare kutas na aham parāyuḥ ṛṣayaḥ na marīci mukhyāḥ jānanti yat viracitam khalu sattva saṅgāḥ yat māyayā muṣita cetasaḥ īśa daitya martya ādayaḥ kim uta śaśvat abhadra vṛttāḥ aham mahā indraḥ nirṛtiḥ pracetāḥ somaḥ agniḥ īśaḥ pavanaḥ arkaḥ viriñcaḥ āditya viśve vasavaḥ atha sādhyāḥ marut gaṇāḥ rudra gaṇāḥ sa siddhāḥ 
AVy_3,4.57–3,4.59	 anye ca ye viśvasṛjaḥ amara īśāḥ bhṛgu ādayaḥ aspṛṣṭa rajaḥ tamaskāḥ yasya īhitam na viduḥ spṛṣṭṛ māyāḥ sattva pradhānāḥ api kim tatas anye sa varsya ādau smṛtaḥ brahmā tasmāt devāt anantaraḥ jānāti deva pravaram bhūyas ca atas adhikam nṛpa na tvām atiśayiṣyanti muktau= api kathañcana mad bhakti yogāt jñānāt ca sarvān atiśayiṣyasi 
AVy_3,4.60–3,4.63	 yathā bhakti viśeṣaḥ atra dṛśyate puruṣottame tathā mukti viśeṣaḥ api jñāninām liṅga bhedane sāyujyam samanuprāptāḥ api deva ādayaḥ akhilāḥ tāratamyāt hi tiṣṭhanti tāratamyam hi sādhane manuṣyāṇām sahasreṣu kaścid yatati siddhaye yatatām api siddhānām kaścid mām vetti tattvataḥ yaḥ imam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ 
AVy_3,4.64–3,4.67	 na ca tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me priya kṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmāt anyaḥ priyataraḥ bhuvi adhyeṣyate ca yaḥ imam dharmyam saṃvādam āvayoḥ jñāna yajñena tena aham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥ śraddhāvānana sūyuḥ ca śṛṇuyāt api yaḥ naraḥ saḥ api muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇya karmaṇām dhyānena ātmani paśyanti kecid ātmānam ātmanā anye sāṅkhayena yogena karma yogena ca apare 
AVy_3,4.68–3,4.71	 anye tu evam ajānantaḥ śrutvā anyebhyaḥ upāsate te api ca atitaranti eva mṛtyum śruti parāyaṇāḥ su sūkṣmaiḥ api aśeṣaiḥ ca viśeṣaiḥ saha paśyati sva ātmānam bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva rūpaḥ api sarvadā savartra ca anyat api evam tena adṛṣṭam na hi kvacid sarvatra sarva daiveśam paśyati eva ramā api tu na tu sarvaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ tam paśyanti api anyatas adhikam sva ātmānam anyat ca aśeṣam paśyati eva hi sarvadā 
AVy_3,4.72–3,4.74	 brahmā tu sarvagam paśyet guṇān api atas adhikam na tu sarveṣu kāleṣu tathā paśyati amukti gaḥ muktaḥ tu sarvadā paśyet sarva ga tvena ca api tu na ramā vat viśeṣāṇām darśanam śaknuyāt kvacid sva ātmānam anyat ca sadā viśeṣaiḥ akhilaiḥ api paśyanti añjaḥ tathā vāṇī viśoṣān= tāvataḥ na tu traiguṇyāt paratas paśyet vyāptam śataguṇam harim 
AVy_3,4.75–3,4.78	 giriśaḥ garuḍaḥ ca eva tamaḥ mātra gatam harim paśyet viśeṣān api hi vāṇī dṛṣṭān na paśyati umā suparṇī ca mahat tattvam yāvat prapaśyati rudra dṛṣṭān viśeṣān= ca na eva paśyet kadācana svarūpam anya rūpam ca muktāḥ devāḥ samastaśas jānanti indraḥ ca kāmaḥ ca brahma yāvat ahaṅkṛtiḥ paśyantaḥ manu dakṣa ādyāḥ buddhi tattva sthitam harim paśyanti soma sūryau tu mana stham parameśvaram 
AVy_3,4.79–3,4.81	 anye bhūta sthitam viṣṇum devāḥ paśyanti sarvadā bahu sāhasra varṣeṇa mahat tattve kvacid kvacid anye ca eva yathāyogya maṇḍa antar vartinam harim śvetadvīpa patim ca eva hṛdi eva anye tu kecana kadācid eva tatra api kecid paśyanti keśavam umā yāvat ananta aṃśān pūrva dṛṣṭebhyaḥ eva tu viśeṣān vāsudevasya paścāt uktāḥ vicakṣate 
AVy_3,4.82–3,4.84	 śakra kāma ādayaḥ ca eva viśeṣān brahmaṇi sthitān umā ādibhiḥ prabuddhebhyaḥ śata aṃśān eva cakṣate ityādi veda smṛti gavacanebhyaḥ yathārthataḥ tāratamyam vimuktānām sādhanānām ca dṛśyate sādhya sādhana vairūpyam adṛṣṭam kena kalpyate vaiṣamyam nirghṛṇa tvam ca tena syātām parasya ca sa apekṣa tvāt iti ca tau vidyā adhīśena vāritau 
AVy_3,4.85–3,4.87	 tāratamyāt sādhanānām sādhya tāt ṛktavam īśataḥ avaiṣamyādi hetuḥ syāt sadā eva parameśvare svātantrye vidyamāne api sādhana ādau pareśituḥ apekṣya anādi vaicitṛyam na doṣaḥ iti tad vacaḥ nānā ādi tvāt iti hi uktam upapadyate iti api apekṣya upāya vaiṣamyam upeyasya tathā sthitiḥ mayā kayā viruddhā syāt rāja ādau= api dṛśyate 
AVy_3,4.88–3,4.91	 tyāgaḥ dṛṣṭasya ca adṛṣṭa kalpanā iti su duṣkarau māyibhyaḥ anyena kena api tat kim anyaiḥ ca vādibhiḥ māyinaḥ atra anugamyante śruta hānya śruta grahau api atra māyinām liṅge tat ke doṣāḥ tatas adhikāḥ niśśeṣa gata doṣāṇām bahubhiḥ janmabhiḥ punar syāt āparokṣyam hi hareḥ dveṣa īrṣyādiḥ tatas kutas bhaveyuḥ yadi ca īrṣi ā ādyāḥ sameṣu api kutas na te tapyamānāḥ samān dṛṣṭvā dveṣa īrṣyā ādi yutāḥ api dṛśyante bahavaḥ loke doṣāḥ eva atra kāraṇam 
AVy_3,4.92–3,4.94	 yadi nirdoṣa tā tatra kimādhikyena dūṣyate yadi anya darśana abhāvādīrṣi ādiḥ vinivāryate adarśanāt arati ādiḥ katham tena nivāryate brahmaṇaḥ api aratiḥ dṛṣṭvā pūrvam ekākinaḥ śrutau na eva reme sa ca ekākī tasamān na ramate kvacid dvitīyam aicchat tena asau= iti śrutayaḥ ūdire yadi icchā tatra na eva asti iti eva tat kalpyate mṛṣā śruti ukta nirdoṣa tā eva kim na aṅgīkriyate svayam 
AVy_3,4.95–3,4.98	 tāratamyam ca kāmam ca śrutam eva atihāya tu aśrutā sama tā kena kalpyate yukti māninā kim tat mānam sama tve te muktānām upalabhyate vṛthā ayam āgrahaḥ kena śruta hānya śruta grahe mokṣe api tāratami a itas cetana tvāt purā yathā iti uktaḥ uttaram kim te kalpanā mātra vādinaḥ na ca duḥkha ādikam kalpyam nirduḥkha tva śruteḥ balāt śokam tarati ātma vettā tīrṇaḥ sarvān aduḥkha bhāj 
AVy_3,4.99–3,4.102	 yena ānandyā iva bhavati na śocati kadācana kilbiṣa spṛt pituṣaṇiḥ aram hitaḥ iha īśvaraḥ yam yamantam abhiprepsuḥ sa saṅkalpāt bhavet iha iti ādi śrutayaḥ mānam nirduḥkha tva ādi sampadi atas duḥkha ādi anumayā na avakāśaḥ atra labhyate tāratamya anumā tena bhavet na ati prasaṅginī śruti yukti balāt evam tāratamyam vibhāvyate muktau= api tatas ke atra virodham kartum īśate 
AVy_3,4.103–3,4.106	 anādi yogyatām ca eva kali vāṇi īśvara avadhim kaḥ nivārayitum śaktaḥ yuktayā āgama bala uddhatām brahmaṇaḥ anyatra ādhikya yuktaḥ kālaḥ vivādavān kālaḥ hi ayam yathā ityādi mā anumāmāninaḥ bhavet anya śabdaḥ hari śrī svasamebhyaḥ anya vivakṣayā prayuktaḥ na eva doṣāya rudra ādiṣu ca yuktitaḥ uttama tvam tu muktānām api na brahmaṇaḥ bhavet vyaktiḥ sukhasya tu bhavet natu ādhikyam sukhasya ca 
AVy_3,4.107–3,4.109	 bala jñāna adhika tvam ca tebhyaḥ hi brahmaṇaḥ sadā ādhikyasya tu anitya tve na kiñcid mānam īyate śṛṇve vīraḥ ugram ugram damāyan= anyam anyam atinenīyamānaḥ edhamāna dviu bhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśaḥ indraḥ manuṣyān parā pūrveṣām sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇaḥ aparebhiḥ eti anānubhūtīḥ ava dhūnvānaḥ pūrvītindraḥ śaradaḥ tartarī iti 
AVy_3,4.110–3,4.112	 divedive sadṛśīḥ anyam ardham kṛṣṇāḥ asedhat apa sadmanaḥ jāḥ ahan dāsāḥ vṛṣabhaḥ vasnayanta udavra je varcinam śambaram ca tam bhūtiḥ iti devāḥ upāsāñcakrire te babhūvuḥ tasmāt ha api etarhi suptaḥ bhūbhrūḥ iti eva praśvasiti abhūtiḥ iti asurāḥ te ha parābabhūvuḥ tat yathā peśaskarī peśasaḥ mātrām apādāya anyat navataram kalyāṇataram rūpam tanutaḥ evam eva ayam ātmā idam śarīram nihatya avidyām gamayitavān yat navataram kalyāṇataram rūpam kurute pitṛyam pitṛyam vā gāndharvam vā daivam vā prājāpatyam vā brāhmam vā anyeṣām vā bhūtānām 
AVy_3,4.113–3,4.115	 prayānti paramām siddhimaihikā muṣmikīm drutam yā na prāpya asuraiḥ sarvaiḥ akṣayā kleśa varjitāḥ na tām gatim prapadyante vinā bhāgavatāt narān avajānanti mām mūḍhāḥ mānuṣīm tanum āśritam param bhāvam ajānantaḥ mama bhūta maheśvaram mogha āśāḥ mogha karmāṇaḥ mogha jñānāḥ vicetasaḥ rākṣasīm āsurīm ca eva prakṛtim mohanīm śritāḥ 
AVy_3,4.116–3,4.119	 mahātmānaḥ tu mām pārtha daivīm prakṛtim āśritāḥ bhajanti ananya manasaḥ jñātvā bhūtādim avyayam abhayam sattva saṃśuddhiḥ jñāna yoga vyavasthitiḥ dānam damaḥ ca yajñaḥ ca svādhyāyaḥ tapaḥ ārjavam ahiṃsā satyam akrodhaḥ tyāgaḥ śāntiḥ apaiśunam dayā bhūteṣu alolu tvam mārdavam hrīḥ acāpalam tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adrohaḥ na ati mānitā bhavanti sampadam daivīm abhijātasya bhārata 
AVy_3,4.120–3,4.122	 ḍambhaḥ darpaḥ atimāḥ ca krodhaḥ pāruṣyam eva ca ajñānam ca abhijātasya pārtha sampadam āsurīm mām ātma para deheṣu pradviṣantaḥ abhyasūyakāḥ tān aham dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu nara adhamān kṣipāmi ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu āsurīm yonim āpannāḥ mūḍhāḥ janmani janmani mām aprāpya eva kaunteya tatas yānti adhamām gatim 
AVy_3,4.123–3,4.126	 dvividhaḥ bhūta sargaḥ atra daive āsuraḥ eva ca viṣṇu bhakti paraḥ daivaḥ viparītaḥ tathā asuraḥ devānām paramaḥ dharmaḥ sadā yajña ādikāḥ kriyāḥ svādhyāyaḥ tattva vedi tvam viṣṇu pūjā ratiḥ smṛtiḥ daityānām bāhuṣāi tvam mātsaryam yuddha satkriyā nīti śāstra praveditvam śiva pūjā ratiḥ smṛtiḥ varṇa āśrama ācāravat tvam svādhyāyaḥ bhaktiḥ acyute śive sūrye tathā devyām svabhāvaḥ mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVy_3,4.127–3,4.130	 anādi vaiṣṇavāḥ eva devatāḥ tu svabhāvataḥ viparītāḥ tatas daityāḥ sadā eva anādi kālataḥ mānuṣāḥ miśra matayaḥ vimiśra gatayaḥ api ca ityādi vākya sandarbhe jñāyate anādi yogya tā yadi anādiḥ viśeṣaḥ na sāmpratam katham eva saḥ adṛṣṭāt eva ca adṛṣṭam svīkṛtam sa varva ādibhiḥ ākasmikaḥ viśeṣaḥ ced adṛṣṭe kvacid iṣyate sarvatra ākasmika tvam syāt na adṛṣṭa apekṣatā bhavet adṛṣṭāḥ ced viśeṣaḥ ayam anādi tvam kutas na tat 
AVy_3,4.131–3,4.134	 naca anya bheda vat viṣṇau bhedaḥ tad darśinām api dṛśyate pratyabhijñā eva bahu rūpeṣu dṛśyate bahu tvam ca viśeṣeṇa na bhedena kathañcana pratyabhijñā ca yeṣām na te api tad muṣya dṛṣṭayaḥ bhedam na eva prapaśyanti bhedam anyebhyaḥ eva ca paśyanti evam hariḥ teṣām sandarśayati na anyathā evam bṛhatsaṃhitāyām vacanam na purāṇa gam loka darśana vādyā iva veda rodhāya śaknuyāt 
AVy_3,4.135–3,4.138	 aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ ca parīkṣā pūrva darśanam niṣeddhum śaknuvādi eva veda rodhāya śaknuyāt na ca niścita bhedasya darśane asti purāṇa gam vākyam kvacid hi sammugdha darśanam tatra gamyate aparīkṣitam eva atra vedha ādikam adhīśituḥ parīkṣā darśane na eva dṛśyate kenacid kvacid nirdoṣam eva tam brahmā dadarśa aśeṣa rūpiṇam nirdoṣam eva rudraḥ adrāk nirdoṣam tam purandaraḥ
