AVy_3,4.139–3,4.141	 nirdoṣāṇi asya rūpāṇi dṛṣṭāni evam sura uttamaiḥ anye sa doṣāḥ sarve api nirdoṣaḥ harirekalaḥ iti barku śruteḥ ca eva sa doṣam na asya darśanam aviddhaḥ viddha vat viṣṇuḥ ajātaḥ jāta vat mṛṣā abaddhaḥ baddha vat ca eva darśayati amita dyutiḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca eva prāha nirdoṣa tām hareḥ aparīkṣita dṛṣṭayā eva sa doṣaḥ dṛśyate hariḥ parīkṣā darśane na eva dṛśyaḥ doṣaḥ hareḥ kvacid iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca āha pramāṇam hi parīkṣitam 
AVy_3,4.142–3,4.144	 na parīkṣā anavasthā syāt sākṣi siddhe tu asaṃśayāt mānase darśane doṣāḥ syuḥ navai sākṣi darśane su dṛḍhaḥ nirṇayaḥ yatra jñeyam tat sākṣi darśanam icchā jñānam sukham duḥkha bhaya abhaya kṛpa ādayaḥ sākṣi siddhā na kaścid hi tatra saṃśayavān kvacid yat kvacid vyabhicārī syāt darśanam mānasam hi tat manaḥ cakṣuḥ darśana ādeḥ api yatra eva sākṣiṇā prāmāṇyam su gṛhītam syāt tat parīkṣita darśanam 
AVy_3,4.145–3,4.148	 na jñāna dṛṣṭi mātreṇa prāmāṇyam tasya dṛśyate niyamena sukha ādyeṣu prāmāṇyam sākṣi gocaram sva prāmāṇyam sadā sākṣī paśyati eva su niścayāt jñānasya grāhakeṇa eva sākṣiṇā mānatā amiteḥ doṣa abhāve pramāṇa tvam doṣa abhāvasya sākṣiṇā niścita tvam kvacid ca eva svatas prāmāṇyam iṣyate atas na sarva mānānām prāmāṇyam niścitam bhavet sākṣiṇā niścitam yatra tat prāmāṇya sva lakṣaṇam 
AVy_3,4.149–3,4.152	 na hi kaścid sukha ādyeṣu saṃśayam kurute janaḥ na ca eva akhila mānāni niścinoti akhilaḥ janaḥ tasmāt anubhava ārūḍham kim artham upalapyate doṣa abhāva ādikam ca eva sākṣī samyak prapaśyati tat parīkṣita mānena na doṣaḥ viṣṇavi kvacid aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ tu kasmin= arthe na vidyate tat pratyakṣa viruddha arthe na āgamasya api mānatā upajīvyam akṣa jam yatra tad anyatra viparyayaḥ 
AVy_3,4.153–3,4.156	 laukike vyavahāre atra pratyakṣasya upajīvyatā avatāra ādi daṣṭau syāt āgamasya upajīvyatā āgamena hi viṣṇu tvam jñātvā doṣaḥ atra kalpyate na ced syāt doṣavān anyaḥ śāstra siddham hi lakṣaṇam kasyacid doṣavat tvam syāt iti mātre akṣa jam bhavet na viṣṇoḥ deṣavat tve hi pratyakṣam vartate svatas kecid paśyanti doṣān iti atra api syāt na cākṣa jam paurāṇam vākyam eva atra tat śrutyā eva viruddhayate 
AVy_3,4.157–3,4.160	 purāṇasya upajīvyaḥ ca vedaḥ eva naca aparaḥ tad virodhe katham mānam tat tatra ca bhaviṣyati aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ ca katham eva akṣa jam bhavet yadi evam devadatta ādi bhramaḥ kim na akṣa jam bhavet yāvat śakti parīkṣāyām upajīvyasya bādhane doṣaḥ na aśodhite doṣaḥ upajīvya tvam asvalam bhrame api abhrama bhāgaḥ asti tanmātram upajīvya hi bādhaka jñāna vṛttiḥ syāt na ca evam su parīkṣite sarvam tat upajīvya eva pramāṇam vartate yatas 
AVy_3,4.161–3,4.164	 katham brahma iti tat jñeyam sarvajña tva ādi lakṣaṇam vihāya yasmāt kasmāccid svarūpasya eva ced yadi upajīvya tvam etasmāt vyāvṛttam yāvatā bhavet tāvatā eva upajīvya tvam svarapasya eva na kvacid sarva lakṣaṇa yuktam tu svarūpam yadi bhaṇyate astu naḥ na eva hāniḥ syāt sva pakṣaḥ ca ayam añjasā yasmāt anvitaḥ eva arthaḥ śabdānām api sarvaśas viśeṣa sāmanyatayā svarūpam akhilam bhavet 
AVy_3,4.165–3,4.168	 puras varti tva pūrvāṇi devadatta ādika bhrame vyāvartayanti tad rūpam caitra mātrat vinā eva hi brahmaṇaḥ nirviśeṣa tvāt vyāvartayati kim punar yasmāt kasmāt cid api arthāt tāvat ced siddha sādhanam cit mātra tvam ca naiveṣyam aviśeṣa tva vādinaḥ tāvat mātram yat īṣyam syāt sarvajña tvam kutas na tat cit mātra abheda sādhye api siddham tat prativādinaḥ sva abheda aṅgīkṛteḥ eva cit tvam svasya api yat matam 
AVy_3,4.169–3,4.171	 sarva apekṣa tayā sarvajña tvam iti eva tat na hi iti ced cetana tvam ca jña tvam na jñeya varjitam sva jñeya tvam ca na eva asau manyate sa viśeṣatas sva śabdaḥ api para apekṣaḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ eva hi sva śabda arthaḥ iti proktaḥ svarūpam nāma kim na ced rūpa śabdena pūrṇa tvāt tat ca sāmānyatā vacaḥ na svarūpa abhidhāyi syāt vaiyarthyam svaravasya yat 
AVy_3,4.172–3,4.175	 cetanasya svabhāvaḥ hi caitanyam iti gīyate tasmāt viśeṣa bāhulyam caitanyasya viśeṣataḥ na jñeya jñātṛ hīnam hi jñānam nāma kvacid bhavet jñeya jñāna vihīnaḥ ca jñaḥ iti atra ca na pramā jñātṛ jñeya vihīnam ca jñānam ced bhoktṛ bhojyataḥ hīnam bhojanam eva syāt tāḍanam kartṛ tāḍyataḥ nitya tvāt tādṛśam ca syāt iti ced nitya vāc api vācya vaktṛ vihīnā syāt na hi sā ca eva tādṛśī 
AVy_3,4.176–3,4.179	 draṣṭāraḥ veda vācaḥ hi santi vācyāni ca añjasā nityaḥ draṣṭā ca vācyaḥ ca bhagavān eva ca svayam na hi vaktṛ vihīnā ca vācya hīnā api vāc kvacid jñātṛ jñeya vihīnam ca jñānam evam na tat bhavet na hi nityaḥ api vaktā asti vākya vācya vivarjitaḥ jñāna jñeya vihīnaḥ ca jñaḥ api evam na eva vidyate kiñca sarva vilopaḥ ca kena mānena gamyate sarveṇa saha tat vākyām arthaḥ ca yadi gṛhyate tad abhāvena sarvasya na apalāpaḥ bhavet tadā 
AVy_3,4.180–3,4.183	 na gṛhyate ced tad nyāyāt apalāpaḥ na hi kvacid upapatti vihīnasya vākyasya arthaḥ na gamyate upakrama ādi liṅgānām balīyaḥ hi uttarottaram śruti ādau pūrva pūrvam ca brahma tarka vinirṇayāt pratyakṣam upapattiḥ ca bahavaḥ ca āgamā yadā viruddhayante naca arthaḥ asti yatra liṅga virodhitā saḥ eva arthaḥ katham grāhyaḥ upapanne avirodhinī mukhya arthe vidyamāne tu kva sāvarjñyam niṣiddhayate 
AVy_3,4.184–3,4.187	 atas sarva guṇaiḥ yuktam brahma aṅgīkāyarmā iva hi apalāpaḥ api sarvasya na kathañcana yujyate anādi yogya tā ca uktā tena grāhyā eva sarvathā muktānām tāratamyam ca mānaiḥ uktaiḥ na cālyate jñāninaḥ api yatas nityam kurvanti śubham eva hi tāratamyam tu muktau ca tena eva adhyavasīyate tāratamyam na ced muktau kutas kuryuḥ śubham punar kṛcchreṇa api tapaḥ jñānam karma api ete caranti hi 
AVy_3,4.188–3,4.190	 bibhyati sma aśubhān nityam sa kāmāḥ ca śubhe sadā na ca svabhāvaḥ eva ayam bhaya pūrva pravṛttitaḥ kṛcchreṇa ācaraṇāt ca eva śubhasya eva punar punar tādṛśaḥ api svabhāvaḥ ced ajñasya api bhavet tathā phalavat tve pramāṇam ced tatra jñasya samam hi tat niṣkāmam jñāna pūrvam ca nivṛttam iha ca ucyate nivṛttam sevamānaḥ tu brahma abhyeti sanātanam 
AVy_3,4.191–3,4.193	 śubhena ānanda vṛddhi syāt ghrāsaḥ ca eva aśubhena hi jñāninaḥ api yatas tena kartavyam śubham eva taiḥ upāste sa yaḥ ātmānam kṣīyate na asya karma ha asmāt hayā iva ātmanaḥ yat yat kāmayet sṛjate ca tat avidvān bahu karmā api hi anta vat phalam āpnuyāt yat eva vidyayā kuryāt tat eva hi ati vīrya vat ityādi vākya sāmarthyāt tāratamyam vimukti gam 
AVy_3,4.194–3,4.196	 na cātra upāsakasya eva phalam akṣayam ucyate na hi jñānam vinā kvāpi phalasya akṣayatā bhavet jñāna dvāreṇa ced tasya na asmad pakṣa pratīpa tā jñāna uttarasya evam api hi akṣaya tvam na ca anyathā pūrva bhāvi śubhānām hi jñānena eva kṛtārtha tā prārabdhānām tu bhogena tad jñāna uttara karmaṇām muktau= anupraveśaḥ syāt anyathā tad kṛtiḥ nahi 
AVy_3,4.197–3,4.200	 jñānāt pūrvāṇi sarvāṇi śubhāni jñāna siddhaye akāmyāni niṣiddhāni jñāna rodhāya bhuktaye yogyatāyāḥ balāt yat ca śubha bāhulyam āditas jñāna bāhulyam eva etat kuryāt na anyasya kāraṇam jñānasya bhakti bhāga tvāt bhaktiḥ jñānam iti īryate jñānasya eva viśeṣaḥ yat bhaktiḥ iti abhidhīyate parokṣa tva aparokṣa tve viśeṣau jñāna gau yathā sneha yogaḥ api tadvat syāt viśeṣaḥ jñāna gocaraḥ 
AVy_3,4.201–3,4.204	 iti ābhiprāyataḥ prāyas jñānam eva vimuktaye vadanti śrutayaḥ saḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ api hi udīryate bhaktiḥ jñānam iti kvāpi na hi dveṣa yutā dṛśiḥ puruṣa arthāya bhavati sarva śruti virodhataḥ cetanasya dvayam bhogyam saṃsāraḥ muktiḥ eva ca saṃsāraḥ trividhaḥ tatra svargaḥ madhyam adhas tathā muktiḥ ca dvividhā tatra sukham nityam tathā aparam nitya duḥkham iti jñeyam sādhanam saṃsṛtau= api kāmyam karma niṣiddham ca sa ajñānam iti niścayaḥ 
AVy_3,4.205–3,4.207	 dveṣaḥ bhaktiḥ ca muktau tu mukti dvaya vidhāyakam iti paiṅgi śruteḥ dveṣaḥ na eva sat mukti kāraṇam asat mukteḥ kāraṇam ca muktau= iti atra keśavaḥ mukti śabda uditaḥ mokṣam sva bhaktānām karoti yat dveṣataḥ api vimuktiḥ ced mahātātparya rodhanam bhaktayā prasannataḥ devān muktiḥ iti eva tad guṇān vadanti śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ purāṇāni āgamāḥ api 
AVy_3,4.208–3,4.210	 yadi dveṣeṇa muktiḥ syāt vaktavyaḥ doṣa sañcayaḥ smartavyaḥ bhagavān nityam iti arthena eva hi kvacid dveṣāt iva guṇān āha purāṇe kruddha vākya vat yathā kruddhaḥ pitā putram mara iti ākṣepa pūrvakam proktasya anyasya kṛti artham vadati evam purāṇa gam vākyam śruti virodhena sva virodhena ca añjasā bahu āgama virodhāt ca na dveṣāt mukti vācakam 
AVy_3,4.211–3,4.213	 tamaḥ dveṣeṇa saṃyānti bhaktayā muktim tathā eva ca viṣṇau viṣṇu prasādena viloma tvena ca añjasā iti ṣāḍguṇya vacanam api ukta artha niyāmakam mahātātparya rodhe ca katham vākyam pramāṇa tām yāti sarva artha rūpam hi mahātāt paryam iṣyate vācaka tvam hi tātparyam yad arthāḥ akhilāḥ ravāḥ saḥ arthaḥ katham parityājyaḥ eka śabdasya saṃśaye atas vijñāna bhaktibhyām puruṣa arthaḥ paraḥ bhavet 
AVy_3,4.214–3,4.217	 yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau tasya ete kathitāḥ hi arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ bhaktyā jñānam tatas bhaktiḥ tatas dṛṣṭiḥ tatas ca sā tatas muktiḥ tatas bhaktiḥ sā eva syāt sukha rūpiṇī bhaktayā prasannaḥ bhagavān dadyāt jñānam anākulam tayā eva darśanam yātaḥ pradadyāt muktim etayā na aham vedaiḥ na tapasā na dānena naca ijyayā śakyaḥ evaṃvidhaḥ draṣṭum pradadyāt muktim etayā 
AVy_3,4.218–3,4.220	 bhaktayā tu ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidhaḥ arjunaḥ jñātum draṣṭum ca tattvena praveṣyum ca parantapaḥ ityādi vākyataḥ ca eva saḥ ayam ukta arthaḥ īyate na ca prasādam āpnoti dveṣāt bhaktyā tam āpnuyāt iti dṛṣṭa anusāri tvam api asmin= arthaḥ īyate ye pṛthak vihitāḥ viṣṇoḥ guṇāḥ vedena sa ādaram te eva dṛṣṭa vailomyāt aṅgīkāryāḥ na ca aparam 
AVy_3,4.221–3,4.224	 anyat dṛṣṭa anusāreṇa vāsudeve api gṛhyate doṣa abhāvāḥ ca ye vedaiḥ uditāḥ avihāya tān anuktāḥ apica grāhyā mahātātparya śaktitaḥ evam bṛhat saṃhitā vāc siddhāntaḥ hi tat īritaḥ tāratamyena tad bhakteṣu api bhaktiḥ viniścayāt kartavyā eṣā api tad bhaktiḥ loka veda anusārataḥ yaḥ hi bhaktaḥ pradhāne syāt tadīyeṣu api bhaktimān dṛśyate asau niyamataḥ viparītaḥ viparyaye 
AVy_3,4.225–3,4.228	 vyabhicāraḥ yadi kvāpi bhakti hrāsaḥ atra kalpyate bhakti doṣaḥ hi asau yat na tad bhakteṣu api bhaktimān tāratamyena teṣu addhā bhaktiḥ dṛṣṭa anusārataḥ viṣṇu prasāda anusārāt kāryā doṣaḥ tat anyathā sva prīti anusṛtau prītiḥ loke api addhā eva dṛśyate tāratamya parijñānam api etena eva sādhanam lakṣmī viriñca vāṇi īśa girija indra aṅgirassutāḥ sūrya ādayaḥ ca kramaśas bhagavat prīti gocarāḥ 
AVy_3,4.229–3,4.232	 teṣu bhaktiḥ krameṇa eva kāryā nityam mumukṣubhiḥ sarve api guravaḥ ca ete puruṣasya sadā eva hi tasmāt pūjyāḥ ca namyāḥ ca dhyeyāḥ ca paritas harim iti ṣāḍguṇya vacanāt api eṣaḥ arthaḥ avasīyate haribhaktiḥ krameṇa eva tadīyeṣu harismṛtiḥ hari stutiḥ tad smṛtiḥ ca tad stutiḥ hari pūjanam tad pūjā vihita tyāgaḥ iti mukteḥ krameṇa hi niyamāt sādhanāni eva nitya sādhyāni ca akhilaiḥ 
AVy_3,4.233–3,4.235	 iti pravṛtta vacanam sādhanasya vinirṇaye pravṛtte pañca rātre hi sādhanasya ati niścayaḥ haridveṣaḥ na śubha da sat dveṣa tvāt yathā guroḥ kramāt bhaktiḥ hari prīti kāraṇam tad priya aupagā bhaktiḥ yatas yathā svasmin= itya ādyāḥ yuktiḥ atra ca prādhānya tāratamya anusāriṇī bhaktiḥ uttamā prīti daiva hareḥ yasmāt bhaktiḥ sā sva upagāḥ yathā 
AVy_3,4.236–3,4.239	 iti vā jñāna karma ādi phalam ca eṣu krama upagam svātantrya tāratamyena phalam hi phalinām bhavet aśubham tu aśubhe api eṣām svātantryāt prītitaḥ hareḥ ājñayā ca anya gam na eva bhogāya bhavati kvacid puṇyam eva amum āpānoti na devān pāpam āpnuyāt ityādi śrutayaḥ mānam ukte arthe yuktayaḥ aparāḥ upāsana adharma phalam yatas deha antare sthitiḥ vāsudeva ājñayā ca eva pūrva karma anusārataḥ 
AVy_3,4.240–3,4.243	 prerayanti hi te jīvān puṇya pāpeṣu nityaśas arāga dveṣataḥ ca eva katham doṣān avāpnuyuḥ haryājñā karaṇāt eva puṇyam ebhiḥ avāpyate hari pūjā iti ca uddeśāt katham na śubham āpnuyuḥ atas yathākramam dharma jñānayoḥ phalam añjasā sarva prāṇi gatam devāḥ prāpnuvantyā viriñcataḥ devāḥ eva hi devānām viśiṣṭāḥ viniyāmakāḥ brahmā tu akhila devānām narāṇām ca niyāmakaḥ atas sarva guṇān eṣa prāpanoti adhikam anyatas 
AVy_3,4.244–3,4.247	 dravya svātantrya vijñāna prayatnaiḥ adhikam phalam devānām anya gam ca api teṣu yat brahmaṇaḥ hi tat bṛhat tantra uditam vākyam hariṇā phala nirṇaye loke api etādṛśa guṇaiḥ phala ādhikyam hi dṛśyate evañca kali pūrvāṇām asurāṇām mahat phalam aśubheṣu sadā eva syāt mithyā jñāna ādikeṣu hi śubha aśubha phalam devāḥ asurāḥ ca samāpnuyuḥ krameṇa eva yathāśakti yathā ye ye prayojakāḥ 
AVy_3,4.248–3,4.251	 prerakāḥ api pāpānām na devāḥ pāpam āpnuyuḥ iti prakāśikāyām hi provāca hariḥ añjasā yadi api evam surāṇām ca daityānām ca mahat phalam śubha aśubhebhyaḥ evañca kartuḥ ca syāt yathā uditam tasmāt niraya mānuṣya svarga mukti upabhoginaḥ mānuṣa uttamam ārabhya devāḥ tu nirayam vinā asurāḥ tu vinā muktim tamaḥ andham api ca āpnuyuḥ iti tattva viveka uktam svayam bhagavatā vacaḥ 
AVy_3,4.252–3,4.254	 jñāna dā apica ācāryāḥ viśeṣāt phalam āpnuyuḥ muktau= aṣṭaguṇam śiṣyāt guruḥ āpanoti śobhanam tad guruḥ dviguṇam tasmāt sārdham tāvat tatas apare devāḥ sahasra guṇitam kramāt tasmāt yathottaram brahmā mahā ogha guṇitam evam phala vinirṇayaḥ iti āha bhagavān śāstre guru vṛtta abhidhe svayam yuktam ca tat na godātā go mātra phalam āpnuyāt 
AVy_3,4.255–3,4.257	 yaḥ imam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ na ca tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me priya kṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmāt anyaḥ priyataraḥ bhuvi iti āha bhagavān evam api pātram apekṣyate evam eva avirodhena prārabdhasya eva karmaṇaḥ jñānam dṛṣṭa phalam proktam muktiḥ ca iha eva labhyate 
AVy_4,1.1–4,1.4	 samanvaya avirodhābhyām siddhe vastuni sādhane vicāriteṣu aśeṣeṣu sādhaneṣu viśeṣataḥ nityaśas kāryam atyantam avaśyam bhāvi sādhanam cintyate prathamam tatra śravaṇa ādi sakṛt kriyā āvṛttiḥ vā iti sandehe kartavyā avṛttiḥ eva hi upadeśaḥ atat tvam asi iti ādiḥ hi asakṛt eva yat liṅgāt lātavyataḥ pūrva mṛjobarrahma tvataḥ śatāt śuśrāva ugratapāḥ nāma yogyaḥ rudra padasya yaḥ 
AVy_4,1.5–4,1.7	 sārddham parārddham viṣṇoḥ tu guṇān bhaktayā sadā udyataḥ tad tri bhāgam upāsām ca cakre sambhṛta mānasaḥ daśa manvantaram śakra pada yogyaḥ garutmataḥ pada yogyāt sumanasaḥ sunandaḥ nāma ca aśṛṇot upāsām cakraḥ udyuktaḥ manvantara catuṣī ayam sūryācandramasoḥ ca eva pada yogyau su tejasau surūpaḥ śānta rūpaḥ ca manvantara catuṣī ayam aśṛṇvatām sumanasaḥ manvantaram upāsatām 
AVy_4,1.8–4,1.10	 tatas proktāḥ tu te sarve bhaktayaḥ gratapaa ādayaḥ apaśyan paramam viṣṇum tad prasādedhitāḥ sadā iti uktam viṣṇunā sākṣāt granthe sattatva sañjñite ātmā iti nāma kathitam sākṣāt nārāyaṇasya hi ātmā brahma mahān= tāraḥ parameśaḥ śuciśravāḥ viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ anantaḥ iti śrīpatiḥ īryate iti piṅgaśrutiḥ ca eva tathā eva parama śrutiḥ 
AVy_4,1.11–4,1.14	 oma ātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ ātma ānandaḥ akṣaraḥ svarāj viśva trātā nṛsiṃhaḥ ajaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ urukramaḥ anasūyā tathā eva atreḥ jajñe putrān akalmaṣān dattam durvāsasam somam ātma īśa brahma sambhavān iti bhāgavate ca eva tasmāt ātmā janārdanaḥ tasmāt upāsyaḥ viṣṇuḥ iti jñātavyaḥ sat janaiḥ sadā tathā eva upāsate santaḥ tathā eva upadiśanti ca ādāna artha tvataḥ ca ayam ātma śabdaḥ patim vadet svāmī me viṣṇuḥ iti eva nityadā upāsyam añjasā 
AVy_4,1.15–4,1.17	 svāmī viṣṇuḥ iti dhyānam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyataḥ kartavyam sarvathā eva etat na kathañcana vismaret iti sat tattva vacanam ṣāḍguṇya vacanam param mama svāmī hariḥ nityam sarvasya patiḥ eva ca iti dhyeyaḥ sarvadā eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ pratīka viṣaya tvena na kāryā viṣṇu bhāvanā pratīkam na eva viṣṇuḥ yat mithyā upāsā hi anathardā 
AVy_4,1.18–4,1.21	 yaḥ anyathā santam ātma īśam anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa ātma apahāriṇā yaḥ anyathā santam ātmānam anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa īśa apa hāriṇā yaḥ anyathā eva sthitam viṣṇum anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa brahmacāriṇā sva ātmānam pratimām vā api devatā antaram eva vā cetana acetanam vā anyat dhyāyet yaḥ keśavaḥ tu iti kim tena na kṛtam pāpam cāreṇa īśa apa hāriṇā 
AVy_4,1.22–4,1.25	 yaḥ anyat viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet jānīyāt vā harim tathā andhe tamasi majjet sa yatra na eva utthitiḥ kvacid yaḥ anyat viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet viṣṇuḥ anyat iti sma vā anyathā dhyāna doṣeṇa mahātamasi majjati yaḥ anyat viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet viṣṇuḥ anyat iti sma vā mahātamasi magnasya tasya na eva utthitiḥ kvacid yat kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā dhyātam añjasā dhyātuḥ mahā doṣa karam kimu sarva īśvaraḥ hariḥ 
AVy_4,1.26–4,1.29	 yat kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā jñātam añjasā mahā doṣa karam viṣṇuḥ kimu sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ yat kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā jñātam añjasā anartha kāraṇam loke kimu sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ na kiñcid anyathā jñeyam dhyeyam vā tena kutracid kimu sarva uttamaḥ viṣṇuḥ jñeyaḥ nīca tayā kvacid tasmāt vastu yathārūpam jñeyam dhyeyam ca sarvadā kāraṇam puruṣa arthasya na anyathā bhavati kvacid 
AVy_4,1.30–4,1.33	 iti śruti purāṇa ukti balataḥ na pratīkatā dhyeyāḥ viṣṇoḥ kvacid yasmāt mithyājñānam anartha dam iti abhipretya na hi saḥ iti āha bhagavān prabhuḥ pratīka saṃsthita tvena dhyeyaḥ viṣṇuḥ naca anyathā brahma iti ca sadā dhyeyaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ añjasā utkṛṣṭaḥ brahma śabda arthaḥ pūrṇa tvam brahma tā yatas ādhi vyādhi nimittena vikṣipta manasaḥ api tu dhyeyā eva brahma tā nityam viṣṇoḥ bhaktayā nirantaram iti prakāśikāyām ca vacanam viṣṇunā īritam 
AVy_4,1.34–4,1.36	 na ātmā iti sūtram īśasya jīva tvapratipādakam ātma śabdam yatas hetum kṛtvā jīvam nyavārayat sva śabdāt prāṇabhṛt ca eva na uktaḥ iti eva veda rāj yadi ātma śabdaḥ jīve api katham sa vinivārayet ātma śabda uditaḥ tasmāt viṣṇuḥ eva naca aparaḥ ātma brahma ādayaḥ śabda astam ṛte viṣṇum avyayam na vadanti yatas na āptā kvāpi taiḥ guṇa pūrṇa tā nārāyaṇa adhyātma gatam iti yat vaiṣṇavam vacaḥ 
AVy_4,1.37–4,1.40	 yadi jīveśayoḥ veda patiḥ aikyam ca manyate ātma śabdam katham tasmāt nivārayati yuktitaḥ bhedasya vyapadeśam ca sthitim ca adanam eva ca bheda dārḍhye hetum āha satātparyam jagatpatiḥ vyāvahārika bhedaḥ ced kva asau= avyāvahārikaḥ vyāvahārikam iti eva vacanam vyāvahārikam uta na iti vikalpe tu yadi syāt vyāvahārikam tasya api bādhya tā ced syāt bhedaḥ syāt pāramārthikaḥ 
AVy_4,1.41–4,1.43	 avyāvahārika tvam ced bhedaḥ ayam satya tām gataḥ ekasya asatya tāyām hi dvayoḥ eva viruddhayoḥ anyasya satyatā eva syāt iti kena nivāryate asatyam na uktam iti ukte satyam uktam iti prajāḥ jānanti uktam tu no satyam iti ukte asatya tām api na svapne api dvayam mithyā tatra ekam satyam eva hi bhāva abhāvau= ubhau tatra katham mithyā bhaviṣyataḥ 
AVy_4,1.44–4,1.47	 bhāvasya hi niṣedhe tu na abhāvasya niṣedhanam sva vācaḥ asatya tā ced syāt tasmāt bhedasya satya tā tasmāt jīveśayoḥ bhedaḥ ukta nyāyena gamyate etasmāt ātma śabdaḥ ayam paramātmā abhidhā bhavet pratīka viṣaya tvena viṣṇu dṛṣṭiḥ na tat bhavet pratīke viṣṇuḥ iti eva tasmāt kāryā hi upāsanāḥ na ca viṣṇuḥ pratīkam yat tasmāt na ātmā iti upāsanāḥ iti pakṣaḥ yadā brahma dṛṣṭiḥ ca atra viruddhayate sa na iti yuktiḥ tatra api sameti ukta viruddha tā 
AVy_4,1.48–4,1.50	 yadi api utkarṣa mātreṇa hi atad bhave api upāsanāḥ utkarṣaḥ ātmanaḥ api syāt cetana tvāt acetanāt tasamāda tattvam na upāsyam iti veda vidaḥ matam utkarṣāt brahma tā dhyāne yadi syāt phalam añjasā brahmaṇaḥ nīca tā dhyānāt anarthaḥ kim na jāyate acetanasya brahma tva dhyāne tuṣyiḥ nahi kvacid nīcasya sva ātma tā dhyāne kupyati brahma loka vat 
AVy_4,1.51–4,1.54	 caṇḍālaḥ nṛpaḥ iti ukte nṛpaḥ caṇḍāle iti api kaḥ viśeṣaḥ parijñāte nṛpeṇa syāt kathañcana puratas naradevasya caṇḍālaḥ yadi pūjyate rāja vat kim na kopaḥ syāt rājñaḥ loke hi paśyati rājñaḥ tu puratas prokte caṇḍālam nṛpaḥ iti api ātmānam saḥ iti proktam itivat dhayā iva kupyati abhede na etayoḥ dhyāne kaḥ viśeṣaḥ vacasi api ayam rājā tvam iti ukte caṇḍāle atha nṛpe api ca caṇḍālaḥ iti tu prokte samam eva hi dūṣaṇam 
AVy_4,1.55–4,1.57	 dhyāte tu ekasya tad bhāve tad bhāvaḥ anyasya kim na tat naca eva tat avijñātam sarvajña brahmaṇā kvacid tasmāt apeśalam sarvam anyasya brahma tā vacaḥ tasmāt yathā ukta mārgeṇa brahma upāsyam mumukṣubhiḥ tathā upāsya añjasā dṛṣṭam brahma pāpam ca bhasmasāt karoti nikhilam pūrvam pāścāttyasya api asaṅga tām karoti tat dviṣaḥ ca evam puṇya nāśaḥ api asaṅga tā 
AVy_4,1.58–4,1.61	 yat eva vidyayā iti atra pūrva uktāt hi viśiṣṭate pūrvam svarga ādi labdhi artham vīryavat tvena coditam karma vidyā yutam paścāt mokṣe vīrya pradam tu iti tatas bhogena puṇyam ca kṣapayitvā itarat tathā brahma dviṣ brahmadarśī ca tamaḥ mokṣau= avāpnutaḥ brahmāṇam śata kālāt tu pūrvam ārabdha saṅkṣayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tu eva tāvat tvam pañcāśat brahmaṇaḥ tathā rudrasya viṃśat eva syāt indrasya arka ādike daśa anyeṣām brahma mātrasya tu antaḥ ārabdha saṅkṣayaḥ brahmaṇā eva sahātas ca param nārāyaṇam vrajet iti sat tattva vacanam svayam bhagavatā uditam 
AVy_4,2.1–4,2.4	 devānām ca manuṣyāṇām etāvat samam eva hi utkrānti mārgau devānām na prāyeṇa bhaviṣyataḥ karma kṣaya sa tatha utkrāntiḥ mārgaḥ bhogaḥ catuṣyayam phalam mokṣaḥ iti proktaḥ kramāt pādeṣu coditaḥ sraṣṭṛṣu eva tu sṛjyānām praveśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ laye devānām mārgaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ na arcirādiḥ naca utkramaḥ sraṣṭuḥ tu grāsa bhūtasya dehaḥ tatra layam vrajet yatas sṛjyasya devasya na eva utkrāntiḥ tatas bhavet 
AVy_4,2.5–4,2.8	 layāt ca eva arcira ādīnām lokānām api sarvaśas katham mārgaḥ bhavet teṣām viśatām uttamam svatas jātānām mānuṣe loke devānām ca kadācana utkrānti mārgau bhavataḥ na tadā muktiḥ iṣyate anyeṣām api sākṣāt tu muktiḥ prāpya api tam harim saha eva brahmaṇā bhūyāt iti śāstrasya nirṇayaḥ kṣmā ambhaḥ nala anila viyat ma nā aindriya artha bhūta ādibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ pratisañjighṛkṣuḥ avyākṛtam viśati yarhi guṇatraya ātmā kālam param svam anubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ 
AVy_4,2.9–4,2.11	 evam paretya bhagavantam anupraviṣṭāḥ ye yoginaḥ jita marut manasaḥ virāgāḥ tena eva sākam amṛtam puruṣam purāṇam brahma pradhānam upayānti agata abhimānāḥ bhagavantam anuprāptāḥ api tu brahmaṇā saha paramam mokṣam āyānti liṅga bhaṅgena yoginaḥ prāptāḥ api param devam saha eva brahmaṇā punar ānanda vyaktiyāyānti pūrṇām liṅgasya bhaṅgataḥ 
AVy_4,2.12–4,2.14	 iti śruti purāṇa ukti balāt vijñāyate ca tat bhogaḥ tu sarva devānām nara ādīnām ca vidyate tatra praveśaḥ devānām uttarottarataḥ kramāt ucyate deha gānām ca vṛttīnām evam eva tu tatra mokṣa svarūpam tu vādinaḥ pratibhā āśrayāt nānā vadanti puṃsām hi matayaḥ guṇa bhedataḥ pṛthak pṛthak prajāyante tamasā eva anyathāmatiḥ 
AVy_4,2.15–4,2.17	 rajasā miśra buddhi tvam sattvena eva yathā matiḥ guṇa atītā vimuktānām matiḥ śuddha citiḥ yatas sāmyak evā atha nityā ca tad tad māhātmya yogataḥ bahaā ca ati viśadā spaṣṭā ca eva śriyaḥ matiḥ mahā śuddha citi tvena tatas api ati mahā citiḥ aśeṣa uru viśeṣāṇām ati spaṣṭa tayā dṛśiḥ nityam eka prakārā ca nārāyaṇa matiḥ parā 
AVy_4,2.18–4,2.20	 sūrya prabhāvat akhilam bhāsayanti nirantarā nirlepā vīta doṣā ca nityam eva avikāriṇī viśeṣa aṃsa tad gatān= tyaktavā prāyas tad lakṣaṇā śriyaḥ tathā eva spaṣṭa tā bhāvāt tad tantra tvāt ca kevalam na tādṛśī brahmaṇaḥ tu prāyas eva śriyaḥ yathā muktānām tu tad anyeṣām samudrataraā upamā agni jvālā vat eva syāt smṛti gānām dṛśaḥ bhavaḥ 
AVy_4,2.21–4,2.23	 evaṃvidheṣu jñāneṣu tamasā muṣya dṛṣṭayaḥ khadyota sadṛśa ati alpa jñāna tvāt anyathā dṛśaḥ vadanti vādinaḥ mokṣam nānā mata samāśrayāt āśritya pratibhām āha jinaḥ tatra atitāmasīm jñānāt karma kṣayāt mokṣaḥ bhavet deha ākhya pañjarāt pañjara unmukta khaga vat alākā kāśa gocaraḥ nityam ūrdhvam vrajati eva pudgalaḥ hasta pādavān 
AVy_4,2.24–4,2.26	 iti tat kena mānena mokṣa rūpam pradṛśyate gatiḥ ūrdhvā ca duḥkhetā gati tvāt laukikī yathā iti ukte ca anumāna eka śaraṇasya kim uttaram anūrdhva gati tā tatra yadi upādhiḥ khagasya ca dūra ūrdhva gamane duḥkham iti sādhya anugaḥ na saḥ pratisādhana rūpasya na anumānasya dūṣaṇam upādhiḥ pratirūpam hi sādhanam tat na ca aparam 
AVy_4,2.27–4,2.29	 atha api sa śarīra tvam ca atra upādhiḥ na vai bhavet gati tvam yatra dehi tvam iti yat sādhana anugam āgamān anusāri tve prasaṅgaḥ ayam yatas tatas na apasiddhānta tā doṣaḥ prasaṅge yadi sā bhavet tadā eva atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt na pasaṅgaḥ kvacid bhavet loka ākāśa gati tvam ced upādhiḥ sādhana anugaḥ saḥ api iti ukte vadet kim sa tasmāt veda uditaḥ bhavet 
AVy_4,2.30–4,2.33	 mokṣaḥ evam svayam viṣṇuḥ yadi api īśaḥ hi aśeṣa vid cakāra saugata matam mohāya eva cakāra yat asurāṇām ayogyānām vedamārge pravartatām atas asura adhikāra tvāt na grāhyam tat matam kvacid catuṣprakāram tat ca uktam śūnyam vijñānam ekalam anumeya bahis tattvam tathā pratyakṣa bāhya gam iti tatra tu ye śūnyam vadanti ajñāna mohitaḥ te mokṣam tādṛśam brūyuḥ niśśaṅkam māyinaḥ yathā 
AVy_4,2.34–4,2.37	 na kiñcina mukta yavasthāyām ātmā atmīyam atha api vā ekasmin saṃsṛteḥ mukte na kiñcid avaśiṣyate tad saṃvṛtyā eva bhedaḥ ayam cetana acetana ātmakaḥ dṛśyate saṃvṛteḥ dhvaṃse nirviśeṣa eva śūnyatā na sattvam na eva ca asattvam śūnya tattvasya vidyate na sukha tvam na duḥkha tvam na viśeṣaḥ api kaścana nirviśeṣam syayambhātam nirlepam ajara amaram śūnyam tattvam asambādham nānā saṃvṛti varjitam 
AVy_4,2.38–4,2.41	 aśeṣa doṣa rahitam manaḥ vācām agocaram mokṣaḥ iti ucyate asadbhiḥ nānā saṃvṛti dūṣitam saṃsṛti avastham vijñeyam saṃvṛtya eva viśeṣyate sthitayā dhvastayā ca eva saṃsṛtiḥ mokṣaḥ iti api kecid teṣu anyathā prāhuḥ saṃvṛtya eva tu anekadhā avacchinnam mahā śūnyam nānāna pudgala śabditam yasya śūnya eka rasa tā jñānāt sā tu apagacchati sa pudgala tva nirmuktaḥ mahā śūnya tvam eṣyati 
AVy_4,2.42–4,2.45	 saṃvṛtya anyaḥ tu avacchinnaḥ duḥkhāni anubhavati alam iti evam māyinaḥ ca āhuḥ eka jīva tva vādinaḥ bahu jīva matāḥ ca iti māyā teṣām tu saṃvṛtiḥ nirviśeṣa tva vācā eva śūnyam brahma eva naḥ bhidā saccit sukha ādikam ca eva kim kutas akhaṇḍa vādinaḥ vyāvartya mātra bhedaḥ tu vidyate śūnya vādinaḥ anṛta ādeḥ apoham tu svayam eva hi manyate nirviśeṣa tvataḥ na eva viśeṣaḥ brahma śūnyayoḥ 
AVy_4,2.46–4,2.48	 prāmāṇya ādi ca vedasya phalatas samam eva hi atattva avedakam yasmāt pramāṇam tena kathyate atattva avedaka tvam yat aprāmāṇyam satām matam dīrgha bhrānti karī ced syāt atattva āvedaka pramā rajju sarpa ādi vijñānāt api ādhikya adamāna tā syāt āgamasya anivartya mahā moha pradatvataḥ talanailya ādi vijñānam ākāśe māna tāṃ vrajet chatra ākāra tva vijñānaṃcandra prādeśa tā matiḥ 
AVy_4,2.49–4,2.52	 nirbheda tvam tu śūnyasya tena api aṅgīkṛtam sadā sattva asattva ādi dharmāṇām abhāvaḥ ubhaya ūḥ mataḥ na hi sat pratiyogi tvam śūnya tvam tena ca iṣyate na ca duḥkha virodhi tvāt anyā hi ānandata iṣyate māyinā śūnya pakṣe api jñānam jāḍya virodhi ca dharmaḥ te api na santi eva kaḥ viśeṣaḥ tatas tayoḥ etādṛśānām pakṣāṇām dūṣaṇam prabhurā kṛtam sva pakṣa sādanena eva na abhāvaḥ iti ca uktitaḥ 
AVy_4,2.53–4,2.55	 ātma abhāve pum arthaḥ kaḥ iṣṭasya ātma avadhiḥ yataḥ yadi na ātmā avadhiḥ mokṣaḥ mokṣaḥ syāt ghaṭa śūnyatā kalpita tvāt viśeṣāṇām māyinaḥ api samam hi tat dṛśyamāne viśeṣe api yadi ced aviśeṣa tā ghaṭa abhāvaḥ aviśeṣaḥ syāt pāścātyaḥ ca id anāgataḥ na mokṣaḥ vimataḥ yasmāt adehaḥ ghaṭa śūnyatā yathā iti ukte vadet kim sa yaḥ anumā mātra mānakaḥ 
AVy_4,2.56–4,2.59	 na ca māyī vadet tatra pūrva uktena eva vartmanā amāna tvāt śruteḥ tasya nacā deha tva vādinī śrutiḥ kācid adeha tvam aprākṛta śarīra gāḥ mokṣe bhogam yatas brūte jakṣan krīḍan= iti śrutiḥ nirduḥkha tvāt na tat mokṣaḥ pratipannam yathā iti ca anumādūṣaṇam kim syāt vādinoḥ śūnya māyinoḥ duḥkham duḥkhāt abhinna tvāt mokṣaḥ api syāt asaṃśayam bhede sa dvaitatā eva syāt iti ādi amita doṣataḥ heyam māyā matena eva saha śūnya matam budhaiḥ 
AVy_4,2.60–4,2.62	 evam vijñāna vādaḥ api jñāna mātra viśeṣataḥ tasya api bhaṅgura tva ādi viśeṣam apahāya hi advaitatā matam sākṣāt ukta doṣaḥ tatas bhavet kālaḥ na kevala jñānī kāla tvāt pratipanna vat etayā anumayā rodhāt na tādṛś mokṣa rūpa tā yadi kālaḥ api na iti āha kadā iti praśnaḥ uttaram kim vakṣyati yadā avasthām vadet sā pakṣatām vrajet 
AVy_4,2.63–4,2.66	 avasthātvāt iti hi eva hetuḥ sā api kadā iti ca pṛṣṭe kālaḥ ca vaktavyaḥ na akāla tvam tatas bhavet na kālaḥ iti sāmānya niṣedhe kālaga pramā niruṇaddhi vaktavyaḥ na akāla tvam tatas bhavet eka jīva tva pakṣe tu kāla abhāvāt iyam pramā kupitā kālam ādāya dvaitam eva upapādayet vimataḥ prapañcavān kālaḥ kāla tvāt pratipanna vat iti ca anya anumaika tvam jīvasya vinivārayet 
AVy_4,2.67–4,2.70	 kāla śabda īśvara eka tva matāni api evam eva hi nirākṛtāni teṣām ca samatvāt pakṣa doṣayoḥ jñānam svarasa bhaṅgayā iva nitya santām iṣyate bauddhābhyām aparābhyām tu tatra api ukta anumā ripuḥ mokṣaḥ na śuddha vijñāna santānī kāla gatvataḥ pratipannaḥ yathā iti etat anumānam tad uttaram anumānāni sarvāṇi pratisādhana yogataḥ niṣiddhāni ukta bhaṅgayā eva śrutayaḥ ca asmad ukti gāḥ 
AVy_4,2.71–4,2.74	 sāṅkhaya naiyāyika ādyāḥ ca prāhuḥ mokṣam tu nissukham icchā dveṣa prayatna ādeḥ api sarva ātmanā layam tatra āhuḥ na etat api atra śobhanam śrutayaḥ yatas mahānandam ca bhogam ca niyamena vadanti hi prākṛta priya hāniḥ tu priyā spṛṣṭiḥ iti īryate apriyam pratikūlam tat aviśeṣeṇa śabditam na asti hi aprākṛtam duḥkham sataḥ jīvasya kutracid priyam svarūpam eva asya bala ānanda ādi vākyataḥ 
AVy_4,2.75–4,2.77	 heya tvāt apapriyasya eva priya hāneḥ aniṣṭhataḥ na samasta priya abhāvaḥ mokṣe prokte tu yujyate apriyasya svarūpa tvam asureṣu eva hi śrutam asurāḥ na evam evam ca na evam ca akhila mānuṣāḥ iti ātma priya hānāya kaḥ yateta ca buddhimān sañjñā na asti iti api hi asya na amukta jñeyata iti hi dharmān ucchittim eva asya yatas vaktayuttara śrutiḥ 
AVy_4,2.78–4,2.79	 āśaṅkayā asya jñāna hānim maitreyyāḥ moham āha mām bhavān iti uktavatyā hi na aham moham vadāmi te iti uktavā yājñavalkyaḥ hi svarūpa anāśam ūcivān jñāna rūpasya vijñāna anāśaḥ tad nāśaḥ eva yat iti śūnyamata ucchittyai punar ānanda pūrvakān dharma ān āha api anucchinnān= tārkikaiḥ vinivāritān mātrā saṃsargam api āha tathā mādhyandina śrutiḥ 
AVy_4,2.80–4,2.83	 ācikṣepa matam tat ca yasmin na viṣayādanam ghrāṇa ādi bhoga abhāvasya tu aniṣṭa tva hṛdā śrutiḥ yena idam akhilam veda vijñātāram svam eva ca kena tam ca vijānīyāt iti aniṣṭam hi sarvathā na akhila jñāpakaḥ viṣṇuḥ ajñeyaḥ niyamena hi tad jñāna artham hi vedānām akhilānām pravartanam pratyakṣa āgama ātma vijñāna avirodha anubhavāt api na sva vijñānitāyām ca virodhaḥ kaścaneyate 
AVy_4,2.84–4,2.87	 kartṛ karma virodhaḥ ca nitya anubhava virodhataḥ katham eva padam gacchet virodhaḥ dṛṣṭa bādhanam saḥ aśnute sarva kāman= ca kāmānnī kāmarūpyatha iti ādi śrutayaḥ ca uktam artham eva vadanti hi asvātantryāt iva iti uktam na dvaita abhāvataḥ kvacid ātmā eva abhūt iti hi asmāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ asvātantrya upamā bheda bhedeṣu iva udīritaḥ śabda tattvaḥ iti proktam maitreyī ukta uttaram ca kim 
AVy_4,2.88–4,2.90	 sukha ādi dharma hānau tu mukteḥ kiñca prayojanam yadi arthaḥ duḥkha hāniḥ syāt anarthaḥ sukha nāśanam tayoḥ ca duḥkha hānāt hi sukha nāśaḥ adhikaḥ bhavet prāpya api duḥkham su mahat sukha leśa āptaye janaḥ yatate sukha hānau hi kaḥ mokṣāya yatet pumān alpāt ca sukha anāśāt hi bibheti atitarām janaḥ mahat ca duḥkham āpnoti sukha nāśa nivṛttaye 
AVy_4,2.91–4,2.93	 na ca rāga nimittam tat vīta rāgāḥ api sphuṭam nārada ādyāḥ sukha arthāya sahante duḥkham añjasā yuddha ādi darśanam yasmāt su duḥkhena api kuvarte yadā indra vairocanayoḥ brahmāstrābhyām su tāpitāḥ api na eva ajahuḥ yuddha rasāt te nārada ādayaḥ iti skānda vacaḥ tasmāt sukha abhāvasya kaḥ yatet vimataḥ duḥkha yuj yasmāt cetanaḥ san sukha ujkhitaḥ pratipannaḥ yathā iti eva ca anumā kena vāryate 
AVy_4,2.94–4,2.96	 sarva śruti purāṇeṣu sukha bhāva uktitaḥ tathā muktau na grāhyam eva etat sukha abhāva matam budhaiḥ saḥ anānandāt vimuktaḥ sanna ānandī bhavati sphuṭam nirguṇe brahmaṇi mayi dhārayan viśadam manaḥ parama ānandam āpnoti yatra kāmaḥ avasīyate na viṣṇu sadṛśam daivam na mokṣa sadṛśam sukham na veda sadṛśam vākyam na varṇaḥ akāra sammitaḥ 
AVy_4,2.97–4,2.100	 yatra ānandāḥ ca modāḥ ca mudaḥ pramudaḥ āsate kāmasya yatra āptāḥ kāmāḥ tatra mām amṛtam kṛdhi iti śruti purāṇāni tatra tatra vadanti hi atas mokṣe sukha abhāvaḥ iti yat kiñcid eva hi śiraḥ kara ādi abhāvaḥ ca na muktasya bhavet kvacid śrutayaḥ ca purāṇāni mānam atra bahūni ca na vartate yatra rajaḥ tamaḥ tayoḥ sattvam ca miśram na ca kāla vikramaḥ na yatra māyā kim uta apare hareḥ anuvratāḥ yatra sura asura arcitāḥ 
AVy_4,2.101–4,2.103	 śyāma avadātāḥ śatapatra locanāḥ piśaṅga vastrāḥ su rucaḥ supeśasaḥ sarve catur bāhavaḥ unmiṣat maṇi praveka niṣka ābharaṇāḥ suvarcasaḥ pravāa vaiḍūrya mṛṇāa varcasām parisphurat kuṇḍala mauli mālinām bhrājiṣṇubhiḥ yaḥ paritas virājate lasat vimāna āvalibhiḥ mahātmanām vidyotamāna pramadā uttamābhiḥ sa vidyut abhra āvalibhiḥ yathā nabhaḥ śrīḥ yatra rūpiṇī uru gāya pādayoḥ karoti mānam bahudhā vibhūtibhiḥ 
AVy_4,2.104–4,2.106	 ṛcām tvaḥ poṣam āste pupuṣvān gāyatram tvaḥ gāyati śakvarīṣu brahmā tvaḥ vadati jāta vidyām yajñasya mātram vimibhītaḥ u tvaḥ kāma anna rūpī carati iti pūrva śrutyā purāṇa uktibhiḥ api adoṣaḥ dehaḥ svarūpa ātmakaḥ eva teṣām muktim gatānām api ceyate hi śiraḥ kara ādyaiḥ api mukti bhājaḥ yuktāḥ yatas te puruṣāḥ idānīm yathā iti pūrvāḥ anumāḥ ca jīva svarūpam aṅga ādi yugāpayanti 
AVy_4,2.107–4,2.109	 na brahma rūpa tvam amuṣya dehinaḥ muktau= api syāt pramayā kathañcid sa brahmaṇā sahitaḥ aśeṣa bhogān bhuṅkte tathā upetya sukha arṇavam tam yat tat param jyotiḥ upetya jīvaḥ nija svara pūtvam avāpya kāmān bhuṅkte sa daivam puruṣottamaḥ ajaḥ ātmā iti ca uktaḥ guṇa pūrti hetoḥ setuḥ sa devaḥ akhila mukti bhāgāmuta amṛtasya iṣyaḥ iha īśitāḥ yat ityādi vākyaiḥ bhagavat vaśaḥ san bhuṅkte akhilān mukti gataḥ api bhogān 
AVy_4,2.110–4,2.112	 kālaḥ api asau na aikya yutaḥ pareṇa jīvasya kālaḥ yatas eṣa yadvat iti ādikāḥ api anumāḥ pramāṇam muktau ca jīvasya paratva rodhe katham ca yaḥ pūrvam asau na paścāt bhavet saḥ eva iti api yuktim eti yatas na dṛṣṭam yat abhūt na pūrvam paścāt tadāsa iti kutas ca kiñcid naca eva muktau tu hareḥ pṛthaktavam aikyam tathā syāt iti yuktim eti yatas na kutra api bhidā abhidā ca dṛṣṭā citaḥ cetanayā kutaścid 
AVy_4,2.113–4,2.115	 ittham matāni bhrama jāni yasmāt mokṣam samuddeśyam api bhrameṇa viduḥ na samyak yat api iha laukikāḥ sukham mama syāt ca sadā iti jānate audāryam uccāvaca śaktiḥ ātma svara pūda arḍhyam ca nija svabhāvaḥ svātantryam āpūrṇa viśeṣa yogya tā virodha hāniḥ ca caturtha pāde vyavasthitiḥ tu aviśeṣaḥ sthitiḥ ca niṣedha sāmānya vidhi kriyāṇām vibhakta tā ca atvarayā eva siddhiḥ vipakṣa samprāpti viruddha hetavaḥ 
AVy_4,2.116–4,2.118	 su śakya tā śaśvat ati prasiddhi viveka vinyāsa vicāra sañjñāḥ nānā pravṛttiḥ kṛtakṛtya tā ca vipakṣa tarkāḥ samatīta pāde mahā phala tvam pravivikta tā ca sandhi grahaḥ sādhanam āpta kṛtyam viśeṣa kāryam kṛti saṃsthitiḥ ca su yuktayaḥ nirṇaya gāḥ sva pakṣe vyāmiśratā kārya kara tvam artha kptiḥ su dārḍhyam paratantra tā ca samāna dharmaḥ kṛta śeṣa tā ca loka upamā pūrva mata anusārāḥ 
AVy_4,2.119–4,2.120	 viśeṣa sāmya śrutiḥ āḍhya tā ca samāna lopaḥ mahimā viśeṣaḥ kṛtārtha tā śaśvat anupravṛttiḥ siddhānta nirṇīti viśiṣṭa hetavaḥ pradhāna vāyuḥ tu iha vāyu nāmā bhūteṣu iti prokta gataḥ api yuktayā yasmāt śrutau pavate ca iti bhūri proktaḥ yatas bhūta mānī ca saḥ api mahā mānī tu alpa mānī ca yasmāt tad śabdena api ucyate tena saḥ api 
AVy_4,2.121–4,2.123	 tasmin layam yānti bhūtāni aśeṣa krama avirodhena saḥ eva viṣṇau indra ādīnām tatra layaḥ kramam tu proktam viśeṣāt anusṛtya na anyat tasmāt aśeṣāḥ girijām praviśya tayā eva rudram saha tena vāṇīm tayā patim prāpya saha eva tena layam harau yānti samasta jīvāḥ somaḥ tu vāri īśa yutaḥ aniruddham viśati asau kāmam asau ca vāruṇīm sā śeṣa devam sa giram ca sā eva vāyum viśati añjaḥ iti iha nirṇayaḥ 
AVy_4,2.124–4,2.126	 umā girīśau= api bhāra tīrau= iti sma vāc veda gatā bravīti ahi indra patnī mahipam viriñca patnīm viriñcam ca vimukti kāle te eva yat tat padam āpnuvanti tad kāle etān samupāsya jīvāḥ brahma tva kāle praviśanti ca etāni iti sma vāc tādṛśatām upaiti sūryaḥ agni yuktaḥ gurum āpya tena śakram saha enena suparṇa patnīm tayā suparṇam saha tena vāṇīm brahmāṇam etat gataḥ eva yāti 
AVy_4,2.127–4,2.129	 indrapraveśaḥ tu yadā ucyate atra tadā hi um ā iti eva suparṇa patnī uktā suparṇaḥ ca girīśa nāmnā tatas virodhaḥ ca na kaścana atra bhṛgu ādayaḥ dakṣam avāpya tena prāpya indram etena suparṇa patnīm viśanti ye manavaḥ rāja mukhyāḥ manum praviśya atra gatā mahā indram ākāśaḥ urvī ca gurum praviśya tena eva yātaḥ puruhūta devam sana ādayaḥ yatayaḥ kāmam eva viśanti śiṣṭāḥ api havyavāham 
AVy_4,2.130–4,2.131	 varṇa āśrama ācāra ratāḥ manuṣyāḥ dharmam manum saḥ api sameti kāle tam eva sarve pitaraḥ sura anugāḥ sarve kuberam sa ca somam eva vimukti kāle praviśanti abhīkṣṇam bhogān= ca tad deha gatāḥ prabhuñjate ānandasu vyaktiḥ amutra teṣām bhavati atas ca iṣyate eva nirgatāḥ krīḍanti bhūyas ca samāviśanti tān eva sāyujyam idam vadanti 
AVy_4,2.132–4,2.134	 sāyujya hīnāḥ ca laye tu sarve proktena mārgeṇa viśanti sṛṣṭau bahis ca niryānti tatas anyadā api sāyujya bhājām bhavati praveśaḥ uktam samastam parama śrutau hi proktam tu sarga kramataḥ viparyayaḥ muktau laye yadvat atho layaḥ ca viparyayeṇa iti avadat girām patiḥ layaḥ yatas muktiḥ iyam surāṇām bhogaḥ viśeṣeṇa ca yam vadiṣyati uktaḥ ca bimba pratibimba bhāvaḥ piṅga śrutau= uktalayā anusārataḥ 
AVy_4,2.135–4,2.137	 bimbe layaḥ yat niyataḥ ca muktau cit ātmanām tad vaśatā ca sarvadā tejaḥ abhidhām tu śriyam āpya viṣṇum agre tatas putra tayā eva vāyuḥ āptaḥ prasūtaḥ punar eva viṣṇum praviśya muktaḥ praaye atra tiṣṭhati sarve api te mukta gaṇāḥ amanda sāndram nija ānandam aśeṣatas api bhuñjante eva asataḥ īśa dehe laye atha sarge bahis eva yānti prayāti dharmam nirṛtiḥ tu śakram marut gaṇāḥ pārṣadāḥ tathā eva sarve aniruddham pṛtanā adhipa ādyāḥ tura śrutiḥ hi ittham iyam vimuktiḥ 
AVy_4,3.1–4,3.3	 utkrānta mārgaḥ ca vimukta gamyam pāda uditam su krama vikramau ca sāntānikam prāptiḥ abhīṣyatā ca saukayarmiti anya matasya tarkāḥ viśeṣa samprāptiḥ uru tvam āptiḥ krama anurāgaḥ kathita anuvṛttiḥ siddhānta nirṇīti karāḥ pratīkam deha ādikam tat gatam eva ye narāḥ upāsate te puratas samāpnuyuḥ brahmāṇam asmān matim āpya viṣṇum prāpsyanti atas anye api tam āpya tasmāt harim gatāḥ mukti bhājaḥ para ante 
AVy_4,4.1–4,4.3	 atikrama uktiḥ kṛtiḥ artha lābhaḥ parā gatiḥ pāra gatiḥ tad okaḥ samasta kāryam vaśitā ca viśva sambhāvanāḥ yuktayaḥ tu anya pakṣe sāmānya rūpam pratibhāna muktiḥ āścarya tā kṛtrimatā asta doṣaḥ viśeṣa kptiḥ kṛta niḥśramaḥ ca māhātmyam iti eva su nirṇaya arthāḥ ananya bhṛtya tvam iha uditabhyaḥ tu anyasya bhṛtya tva nivāraṇāya patim yat eṣām api viṣṇum āha hi uta amṛta tvasya patitva vāc dhareḥ 
AVy_4,4.4–4,4.6	 ete api cānya adhipati tva yuktā viṣṇu anya cittvena yathā pumāṃsaḥ prasiddhi bhājaḥ tu iti ca anumā eva hi abhīṣya siddhayai bhavati iha niścayāt mukta svakīyā varayan tṛtā asti muktau= api brahma purassarāṇām anena devena tathā amunā ca hīṣye parārvāktana lokinām iti phalam śrutiḥ jñānataḥ āha muktau= etat ca sarva aśubha nāśa liṅgāt loka ādhipatyam ca vidhātuḥ eva sarva ātmanā iti āha tura śrutiḥ ca sarve balim deva gaṇāḥ vahanti iti etat ca na anyasya hi yuktim eti 
AVy_4,4.7–4,4.8	 lokāḥ iti iha api tu lokinām vacaḥ lokāḥ iti hi eva ravaḥ prajāsu prayujyate sarva janaiḥ sadā eva tad māninaḥ loka padena ca uktāḥ tad gāḥ tu muktāḥ iha loka śabdāḥ anyonya nāthāḥ iti paiṅginām śrutiḥ aloka śabdena vimukti bhājaḥ vācyāḥ padam tādṛś api iha yuktam loka abhidhāḥ ca api yatas hi muktāḥ prakāśa rūpāḥ satatam ca sarve brahmā eva loka adhipatiḥ vimuktaḥ bhavet iti prāha tura śrutiḥ ca 
AVy_4,4.9–4,4.11	 naca iha vijñāna phalam samuktam loka ādhipatyam ravi bimbataḥ harau uktam pṛthak tat ca purā eva yasmāt bhedaḥ amunā ityādi ca samyak uktaḥ tu apratyayam ca api atihāya na eva rūpeṇa tena iti bhavet iha arthaḥ bhavati asau= iti aṇu śabdam atra vihāya vākyāni bahūni doṣaḥ atas jaga dvaya āpṛtimantaḥ eva brahma ādayaḥ pūrṇa guṇāḥ krameṇa amandam ānandam ajasram eva bhuñjantaḥ ātmīyam ajāt samāsate 
AVy_4,4.12–4,4.14	 namaḥ namaḥ aśeṣa viśeṣa pūrṇa guṇa eka dhāmne puruṣottamāya bhakta anukampāt ati śuddha saṃvid dātre anupādhi priya sat guṇa ātmane yasya trīṇi uditāni veda vacane rūpāṇi divya analam baj tat darśatam ittham eva nihitam devasya bhargaḥ mahat vāyo rāma vacaḥ nayam prathamakam pṛkṣaḥ dvitīyam vapuḥ madhvaḥ yat tu tṛtīyam etat anumā granthaḥ kṛtaḥ keśave niḥśeṣa doṣa rahita kalyāṇa akhila sat guṇaḥ bhūti svayambhu śarva ādi vandyam tvām naumi me priyam
